
-----title
温州 (出生地)
-----detail

class='switch'>—</span></a><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1134&endYear=1139')">1134-1139年</a>，1-6岁</div><div id='895eec4f719549ce9ca6688cd6d4695b' class='detail'><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1134&endYear=1134')">1134年6月</a>　生于六月甲戌。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1135&endYear=1138')">1135-1138年</a>　居乡。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1139&endYear=1139')">1139年1月11日</a>　居乡。父薛徽言卒。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1139&endYear=1139')">1139年1月24日</a>　居乡。母胡氏卒。<br /></div><div class='label1' id='13ce96567ff54b788ff98500862e0dde_label'><a href='javascript: DetailSwitch("13ce96567ff54b788ff98500862e0dde");'><span id='13ce96567ff54b788ff98500862e0dde_link' class='switch'>—</span></a><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1154&endYear=1154')">1154年</a>，21岁</div><div id='13ce96567ff54b788ff98500862e0dde' class='detail'><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1154&endYear=1154')">1154年</a>　返归永嘉故里，遍阅家书，整理父亲遗书。<br /></div><div class='label1' id='e48b42c5d5d543c282926d7f862f06ee_label'><a href='javascript: DetailSwitch("e48b42c5d5d543c282926d7f862f06ee");'><span id='e48b42c5d5d543c282926d7f862f06ee_link' class='switch'>—</span></a><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1155&endYear=1155')">1155年</a>，22岁</div><div id='e48b42c5d5d543c282926d7f862f06ee' class='detail'><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1155&endYear=1155')">1155年</a>　在永嘉故里。<br /></div><div class='label1' id='5c5b6160398c4848a1349ab0b10c0698_label'><a href='javascript: DetailSwitch("5c5b6160398c4848a1349ab0b10c0698");'><span id='5c5b6160398c4848a1349ab0b10c0698_link' class='switch'>—</span></a><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1158&endYear=1158')">1158年</a>，25岁</div><div id='5c5b6160398c4848a1349ab0b10c0698' class='detail'><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1158&endYear=1158')">1158年</a>　安葬岳父后，不久返抵永嘉。<br /></div><div class='label1' id='2516b750c5314b5e9a94ab0068bc58d9_label'><a href='javascript: DetailSwitch("2516b750c5314b5e9a94ab0068bc58d9");'><span id='2516b750c5314b5e9a94ab0068bc58d9_link' class='switch'>—</span></a><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1159&endYear=1159')">1159年</a>，26岁</div><div id='2516b750c5314b5e9a94ab0068bc58d9' class='detail'><span style='margin: 0 0.5em; color: gray;'>▪</span>在永嘉故里闭门读书，潜心向学。是年冬，季宣本之《诗序》而作《诗广序》<br /><span style='margin: 0 0.5em; color: gray;'>▪</span>在永嘉故里闭门读书，潜心向学。作《克斋后记》<div id='poem_1273840' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1273840' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1273840?labeling=true' target='_blank'>克斋后记</a><span class='authorDate'>（1159年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 南宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(31376, "南宋", "薛季宣", "poem_title_1273840")'>薛季宣</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1273840_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1273840'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1273840'>始，走以「损」名斋，记其命之意，既三祀矣，友生有至自钱湖者，道其所闻曰：「上方作室禁省，谓之损斋，窃尝睹斋记尧文」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1273840_comment'></div>询之于人，良是也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1273840_comment'></div>小臣矍而慨曰：圣人与我同虑哉！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1273840_comment'></div>夫人达道而行，是则人所共有，圣人先得我心之所同然者，诚足喜哉！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1273840_comment'></div>礼，贵贱虽不嫌同名，而天壤一号，不可也，假名存而毋害，亦不能一朝居也，思有以更其名而未得。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1273840_comment'></div>已而知所以自解曰：天道人所共有，可以君为道而寘之哉！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1273840_comment'></div>仍故名而不安，亦辟之而已尔。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1273840_comment'></div>君臣之学自有辨，又何疑焉！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1273840_comment'></div>于是即记以求名，而□克己复礼之义，名斋曰「克」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1273840_comment'></div>叙之以续前志，曰：颜子问克己复礼之目，仲尼告以「非礼勿视、非礼勿听、非礼勿言、非礼勿动」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1273840_comment'></div>夫仁者，人也；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1273840_comment'></div>仁之道，谓人无之，可哉？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1273840_comment'></div>惟以物迁，是以去仁而不省。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1273840_comment'></div>圣人戒慎乎所不睹，恐惧乎所不闻，动容周旋中礼，不违于终食之间，物何自迁？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1273840_comment'></div>是以仁浃乎四体。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1273840_comment'></div>夫如是，乃尽人之道，颜子之所以拳拳服膺而毋失自致，具体而微者也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1273840_comment'></div>学者以颜子为准绳，于此岂可不务！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1273840_comment'></div>走细人也，固不可以希圣，然知人者人之道，则吾之道也；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1273840_comment'></div>吾虽失道，将可自绝于人？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1273840_comment'></div>克己归仁，何敢缓也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1273840_comment'></div>顾走之失，有不若人者八焉：闻道而未之能行，一不若人也；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1273840_comment'></div>放心而未之能制，二不若人也；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1273840_comment'></div>处己而未之能尽，三不若人也；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1273840_comment'></div>多言而未之能法，四不若人也；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1273840_comment'></div>乐善而未之能择，五不若人也；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1273840_comment'></div>爱物而未之能容，六不若人也；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1273840_comment'></div>居世而未之能处，七不若人也；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1273840_comment'></div>任私而未之能去，八不若人也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1273840_comment'></div>凡所为不若人者，皆性天之所无有，从欲而得，反身而未之能善，有一于此，不可谓仁，况有其八乎！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1273840_comment'></div>弗亟去之，无以为人矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1273840_comment'></div>及今能以礼自克，率性而知道哉，或庶几乎可也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_30_1273840_comment'></div>为诗铭之，以自警云：</div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_31_1273840'>穹弘地天，灏灏无垠。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_31_1273840_comment'></div>惟道参之，粹焉者人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_32_1273840_comment'></div>人安其仁，则惟圣神。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_33_1273840_comment'></div>往而不反，曷为其身！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_34_1273840_comment'></div>循道而行，无事于勤。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_35_1273840_comment'></div>出入惟时，乃凝乎真。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_36_1273840_comment'></div>勒之铭诗，请法先民<sup class='reference inlineComment2'>⑴</sup>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_37_1273840_comment'></div></div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_38_1273840'>「斋记」下，四库本注云「阙」。</div><div id='poem_sentence_38_1273840_comment'></div></div><div class='poemNote' id='poem_note_1273840'><div class='inline1'><div id='poem_sentence_37_1273840_0'>⑴ 《浪语集》卷三一。又见光绪《永嘉县志》卷三二。</div></div></div><div id='poem_note_1273840_comment'></div></div><br /></div><div class='label1' id='a126dceb08f84514a25b2bdf682560dd_label'><a href='javascript: DetailSwitch("a126dceb08f84514a25b2bdf682560dd");'><span id='a126dceb08f84514a25b2bdf682560dd_link' class='switch'>—</span></a><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1163&endYear=1163')">1163年</a>，30岁</div><div id='a126dceb08f84514a25b2bdf682560dd' class='detail'><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1163&endYear=1163')">1163年7月</a>　辞去汪澈等人的举辟，回到永嘉故里。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1163&endYear=1163')">1163年7月</a>　汤思退任宰相，主和议。薛季宣上书汤思退，论沿边形势。作品：上汤相论边事。<div id='poem_1273677' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1273677' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1273677?labeling=true' target='_blank'>上汤相论边事书</a><span class='authorDate'>（1163年7月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 南宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(31376, "南宋", "薛季宣", "poem_title_1273677")'>薛季宣</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1273677_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1273677'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1273677'>某窃见逆亮歼灭以来，国家宵衣旰食，思备边之计，更年积月，迄无成规。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1273677_comment'></div>此封疆之臣不能远虑深思，以称庙堂倚属之意也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1273677_comment'></div>某小生晚进，安知军旅，然窃食近塞，经涉四年，见之既详，究之亦悉，故敢辄以鄙陋之见，思补庙谟之万一。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1273677_comment'></div>非敢自谓必得，惟所裁择而弃置焉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1273677_comment'></div>冒渎钧严，某下情无任皇惧之至！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1273677_comment'></div></div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_5_1273677'>一、某闻之《兵法》：勿恃敌之可胜，恃吾之不可胜。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1273677_comment'></div>是故先为不可胜。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1273677_comment'></div>上策自治，此不可胜之略也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1273677_comment'></div>今北鄙之弱甚矣，窃聆边人之语，谓虏之谋入寇者凡有三说：其一，屯田淮北，使我困于飞挽，而彼坐收其弊；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1273677_comment'></div>其二，分军并进，以夺我之江流；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1273677_comment'></div>其三，压唐、邓而袭蕲、黄，上游可不战而取。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1273677_comment'></div>虽道听涂说，未足深信，使彼计果出此，亦危道矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1273677_comment'></div>敌今屯军汴、宋、许、蔡诸郡，在形势最为要切。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1273677_comment'></div>数年以来，见我军戍单弱，往往分军轶出，觇我空虚；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1273677_comment'></div>我军奔走而趋之，其去已远，奔命之役，未尝一日无之，先人制人，恐不如此。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1273677_comment'></div>敌既未有可乘之隙，而我之不可胜者又皆若是，日复一日，惧难悠久。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1273677_comment'></div>某尝窃论当今之急，莫若因形势而列屯营，宿兵聚粮，分戍险隘，来不与战，去则据险而要之；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1273677_comment'></div>重镇诸屯，首尾相救，自处閒暇，不奔命于敌人，非惟足以自坊，而制人之术在其中矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1273677_comment'></div>敢以近边形便闻见之所及者，疏其要略，条于左方：</div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_18_1273677'>两淮为北门屏翰，盱眙、濠梁寔当虏冲，今魏公已有成规，不容复议。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1273677_comment'></div>有如虏出顺昌、下蔡，则寿春、合淝为之冲。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1273677_comment'></div>合淝之南，濡须之坞，夹石之戍，乃吴时历阳、皖城之险要，在议者不可不讲。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1273677_comment'></div></div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_21_1273677'>中流为荆、扬之要领，虏出上蔡，则武昌、夏口当其冲，在建炎间，虏尝出此以袭江西矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1273677_comment'></div>其地里比诸州特近，又坦夷无绝险，宜戍麻城、白沙而以黄之旧州为重，使与安陆之军互相应接。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1273677_comment'></div>比缘两淮、荆襄各有分域，此道遂亢而不虞，庙堂之间，尤所当虑。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1273677_comment'></div>信阳、光州亦古重地，可以藩蔽德安、黄州，然而防扼颇难，粮运亦远，若以轻兵杂土人而守，聚忠义军辈屯之，亦可弥缝上游、中流之阙，而为之斥候。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1273677_comment'></div></div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_25_1273677'>唐邓四战之地，在我与敌有之，皆难为守。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1273677_comment'></div>盖屯重兵则粮运回远，轻兵则不足以自立，然我失之则襄、郢暴露。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1273677_comment'></div>沔北尽为敌境，运输屯守尤难为力，如欲坚守二郡，则方城、比阳之戍所不可轻。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1273677_comment'></div>似闻议者以为无险可凭，第欲填守唐、邓，薄险要而保城郭，窃恐用骑之地，尤非我之所长。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1273677_comment'></div></div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_29_1273677'>德安北接随、唐，东黄南鄂，西接荆、郢，亦江、汉间一都会也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1273677_comment'></div>其东北有三关之险道，皆出于信阳，而大寨岭为平易。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_30_1273677_comment'></div>其南旧镇，直黄陂及旧黄州为不远，西南仵落，乃德安漕舟屯泊之地，泛涢而下，不三日可达武昌、鄂州，虽德安屯军亦在其后，此不可不虞者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_31_1273677_comment'></div></div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_32_1273677'>荆襄，上游之根本，吴、蜀咽吭之地，国家最为要切。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_32_1273677_comment'></div>向来未得唐、邓，守备颇严，今既移戍于边，内镇亦弱。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_33_1273677_comment'></div>由枣阳以涉贾堑，趋荆南为轻捷，晚唐黄巢盖尝出此；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_34_1273677_comment'></div>而内乡、顺阳，西接嵩洛，最为襄阳要害，亦宜豫为之防。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_35_1273677_comment'></div></div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_36_1273677'>金、房南蔽夔、峡，西接梁、洋，荆、梁之间一控扼也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_36_1273677_comment'></div>国初征蜀，尝由此以袭夔州，比年用兵，亦尝调其士马入蜀，甚非良算。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_37_1273677_comment'></div>今其兵力幸众，更望为之区处，使之专守一面，不复轻为调发。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_38_1273677_comment'></div></div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_39_1273677'>一、忠义军士，率多淮蔡间人，与虏结怨既深，必能尽力于我。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_39_1273677_comment'></div>其将非武勇廉俭，亦无以得其士心，然多自负其长，不能弥缝上下。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_40_1273677_comment'></div>故正军诸将，好攻其短，正须曲加抚纳，毋使猜贰。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_41_1273677_comment'></div>然其军无粮饷，不免剽掠取资。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_42_1273677_comment'></div>以此失北人之心，甚非吊民之意，更乞朝廷熟议裁处。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_43_1273677_comment'></div></div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_44_1273677'>一、上游粮饷，由沔而达襄、郢，由涢而入安、随，二水通流则转输无阂。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_44_1273677_comment'></div>然此二川方春才有数月之水，秋水涸，漕舟不可上通，濡滞转般，费广而中有不给之患，军须急阙，不免役及于民，役民运粮，其弊有不可胜言者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_45_1273677_comment'></div>若为措置，使运输所向如二水之类者，皆以春冬之际集于江口，一岁之食，必令及春而辨，其宽民力，不可胜计，惟庙堂察之！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_46_1273677_comment'></div></div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_47_1273677'>一、某窃观历古南国战守之计，未尝不保据城壁，虽南唐之弱，当周之胜，犹能历岁坚守。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_47_1273677_comment'></div>此无他，郡县之兵盖与国兵为二，一专为守，一专为战，则事集矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_48_1273677_comment'></div>伏自国家渡江以来，专以大军为重，大军一去，无复坚城。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_49_1273677_comment'></div>夫民岂不念其室家？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_50_1273677_comment'></div>盖无法以自保矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_51_1273677_comment'></div>某观江汉、淮南之俗，其民敦实雄健，涉历世故，颇知用武。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_52_1273677_comment'></div>若朝廷不惜少少赋入，蠲其田租，略以陕西弓箭手法维之，使之人自为战，制其勋赏，一同正军，亦严边之一术也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_53_1273677_comment'></div>比年议者稍知措置保甲及山水寨，然初无豫定之法可以必行，缓急无以相维，散者不可复集。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_54_1273677_comment'></div>考汉晁错之策，似可施用于今，如蒙朝廷孰虑而急图之，使其坞壁粗立，平时可保妻子而不废农桑之业，缓急足以自卫，国家既收其用，全生之赐亦大矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_55_1273677_comment'></div></div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_56_1273677'>一、长江之险，以人为固。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_56_1273677_comment'></div>今我兵力单弱，进战则无守御之备，万一事出意表，可为寒心。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_57_1273677_comment'></div>尝论沿江之民习于舟楫之利，如能蠲其徭役，使水手自为团结，立之部伍，假以舟船，以时隶习，而无害其农功，使之稍识旗鼓，专保乡社，守之勿懈，则数万之众可以不费粮饷而集，异时兼正兵而用，亦守江之一助也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_58_1273677_comment'></div>然此非廉干之吏，少假事权、久任责成不能辨也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_59_1273677_comment'></div>不然，徒为文具，扰而无益，行之不如其已，伏乞钧照。</div><div id='poem_sentence_60_1273677_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1163&endYear=1163')">1163年7月</a>　上书汤思退，批评和、攻二说，主战、守二策。作品：再上汤相书。<div id='poem_1273678' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1273678' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1273678?labeling=true' target='_blank'>再上汤相书</a><span class='authorDate'>（1163年7月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 南宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(31376, "南宋", "薛季宣", "poem_title_1273678")'>薛季宣</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1273678_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1273678'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1273678'>某前任鄂州武昌县令，自县境至蔡州小路三百馀里，行商络绎，又尝转输至信阳境上，颇闻北事之详。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1273678_comment'></div>葛王旧号阑子郎君，盖华言所谓「浪子」者，逆亮屠剪宗戚，乃尝三以计免，包藏晦迹，遂成篡窃之计。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1273678_comment'></div>亮入淮甸，时已僭号燕京，能绥行者之家，除亮苛虐之政，鸣镝之事则为有以殴之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1273678_comment'></div>诸军之还，一日斩万户二十七辈；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1273678_comment'></div>张忠彦久不受代，乃因益戍而代之，陕西之人不觉易帅。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1273678_comment'></div>其他施设，类能阔略从宽。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1273678_comment'></div>凡边事所当施为，往往不俟申请而伪命已下，故虽盗国未久，号令颇行。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1273678_comment'></div>其大臣惟张浩、宋满最为旧人，其馀如萧安远、麻都监、那健元帅、二韩将军之属，类皆拔之小官，不次而用。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1273678_comment'></div>萧等皆佼佼后进，知盗窃仁义以立声名，其持军御下亦和而整，计非万全不动，虽非粘罕、娄宿等辈，然亦未易败袭。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1273678_comment'></div>中原机会，未有间鏬可乘，诸处所遣间探之徒，例皆不能深入；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1273678_comment'></div>纵能深入，又不能察其事情，还则揣所乐闻以悦其上。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1273678_comment'></div>故如符离之役，虏人固已先有勿焚积聚以待南军之令，边远皆知贼意，而淮南顾不知之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1273678_comment'></div>虽以某之愚，亦尝为荆襄督帅言之矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1273678_comment'></div>凡事本无深远，而贪功喜事之臣役于私意，故虽庙堂之上，未易悉察。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1273678_comment'></div>又如通和一事，尤虏乐为，然不能屈辱如前，未易成也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1273678_comment'></div>况当讲战未定，其间何所不有，又况今日之弱，良以前日之和。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1273678_comment'></div>自古国无外患而能安不忘危者，殆人主之所难，故当有害而无补，和之不成，我之幸也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1273678_comment'></div>如以前此数事以为南北之势已成，中原不可复得，是乃不知义命之论；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1273678_comment'></div>徼功轻举，又为非计。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1273678_comment'></div>某谓方今将骄卒惰，边障不修，备御之方，率多施之无所用功之地，至所当务亦未必知，此朝廷所当虑者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1273678_comment'></div>窃尝论为邦之道，自治为急。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1273678_comment'></div>敌之强弱非所当问，又况虏情顽犷，易为骄怠，我能为自强之计，政事修，贤材用，名实不戾，刑赏有章，则夫机会之来，庸有穷尽。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1273678_comment'></div>伏惟某官图维鉴念，以为天下社稷无穷之计。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1273678_comment'></div>去十二月都堂新有敕榜，颁陈边计泄事机之禁。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1273678_comment'></div>某疏远贱吏，身不足以膏斧钺，今也犯此两禁，以渎上公，未见颜色而言，其为狂瞽愚聋甚矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1273678_comment'></div>然某窃念天下一家，孰非身事，游谈靡靡，徒丽心目；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1273678_comment'></div>事功无补，亦何堪用！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1273678_comment'></div>然拘挛讳忌，又非士夫之节，自非在上者以天下为度，心无适莫而洞照事情者，亦不足与言也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1273678_comment'></div>间者某不避僭越，妄以边事琐屑干听，方惧得诛绝之罪，伏蒙某官不赐鄙斥，呼召使前。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1273678_comment'></div>既去，虽不及亲，足见其开之以言也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1273678_comment'></div>此而不言，非惟有负门下，自负其心矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_30_1273678_comment'></div>然此所陈事状，似谈仇敌之美，在蚩蚩薄俗摇手知禁者深所嗤笑，而某辄露悃臆而索言之者，诚以某官量包天地，忠贯日月，至诚体国，乐闻人所难言。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_31_1273678_comment'></div>而近世士风，习为软美之态，此等情状，窃意有知而不言者，事情何自而察哉？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_32_1273678_comment'></div>如某又不敢言，则是终无言者，使国家遂轻此虏，岂为经久之计？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_33_1273678_comment'></div>以故忘其微贱，冒昧而陈之耳。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_34_1273678_comment'></div>《诗》曰：「采葑采菲，无以下体」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_35_1273678_comment'></div>又曰：「人之为言，胡得焉」？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_36_1273678_comment'></div>此言大人君子不间寒远，视言之所从来也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_37_1273678_comment'></div>伏惟某官察其狂狷，而采刍荛之末论，覆其瑕玼而勿为人所闻知，此区区之愿也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_38_1273678_comment'></div>干渎钧听，某下情无任恐惧战慄之至。</div><div id='poem_sentence_39_1273678_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1163&endYear=1163')">1163年8月</a>　致书汪澈，言及乡居生活。作品：与汪参政明远。<br /></div><div class='label1' id='58e54c7aa2e443da9a55ea89e1d878fe_label'><a href='javascript: DetailSwitch("58e54c7aa2e443da9a55ea89e1d878fe");'><span id='58e54c7aa2e443da9a55ea89e1d878fe_link' class='switch'>—</span></a><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1164&endYear=1168')">1164-1168年</a>，31-35岁</div><div id='58e54c7aa2e443da9a55ea89e1d878fe' class='detail'><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1164&endYear=1164')">1164年4月</a>　回到永嘉故里，妻子暴病。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1164&endYear=1164')">1164年5月</a>　上书汪澈，告知杭州见闻。作品：与汪参政明远。<span class='inlineComment2'>（系年作品名称为录入者据张良权点校《薛季宣集》（上海社会科学院出版社2003年版）卷二十二补。）</span><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1164&endYear=1164')">1164年</a>　家居待次，潜心向学。作品：中庸解。大学解。皇极解序。春秋经解旨要序。书古文训序。<div id='poem_1273818' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1273818' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1273818?labeling=true' target='_blank'>中庸解</a><span class='authorDate'>（1164年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 南宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(31376, "南宋", "薛季宣", "poem_title_1273818")'>薛季宣</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1273818_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1273818'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1273818'>天命之谓性，率性之谓道，修道之谓教。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1273818_comment'></div>道也者，不可须臾离也，可离非道也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1273818_comment'></div>是故君子戒慎乎其所不睹，恐惧乎其所不闻，莫见乎隐，莫显乎微，故君子慎其独也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1273818_comment'></div></div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_1273818'>天命，上天之载也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1273818_comment'></div>性，人受天地之中以生者也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1273818_comment'></div>道，日用也；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1273818_comment'></div>教，<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_6_1273818", 1273818, "Clauses/18/Comments/0")'>成物</span>者也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1273818_comment'></div>天命即性也，率性即道也，修道即教也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1273818_comment'></div>性、命、道、教，皆非自外作者，在乎不失其正而已。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1273818_comment'></div>于所不见不闻之地，有毫釐之差，则失性命之正；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1273818_comment'></div>失性命之正，则去道远矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1273818_comment'></div>隐见微显，本一道也，未有动乎中而不形于外者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1273818_comment'></div>戒慎恐惧，所以贞夫一也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1273818_comment'></div>人之于道也，造次颠沛而不可违者也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1273818_comment'></div>无入而不自得，观感之教也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1273818_comment'></div></div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_15_1273818'>喜怒哀乐之未发谓之中，发而皆中节谓之和。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1273818_comment'></div>中也者，天下之大本也；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1273818_comment'></div>和也者，天下之<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_17_1273818", 1273818, "Clauses/44/Comments/0")'>达道</span>也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1273818_comment'></div>致中和，天地位焉，万物育焉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1273818_comment'></div></div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_19_1273818'>物生而静，天之性也；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1273818_comment'></div>感物而动，性之欲也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1273818_comment'></div>喜怒哀乐，皆性中之物也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1273818_comment'></div>方其未发，不可谓之有；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1273818_comment'></div>及其既发，不可谓之无。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1273818_comment'></div>喜怒哀乐正于未发，可不谓中乎？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1273818_comment'></div>发而不失其所谓中，可不谓和乎？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1273818_comment'></div>中者道之所自出，故谓之大本；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1273818_comment'></div>和者物之所同归，故谓之<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_27_1273818", 1273818, "Clauses/65/Comments/0")'>达道</span>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1273818_comment'></div>天地之大，万物之夥，未有离乎道者也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1273818_comment'></div>泯中和而不离，开物成务之道也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1273818_comment'></div></div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_30_1273818'>仲尼曰：君子中庸，小人反中庸。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_30_1273818_comment'></div>君子之中庸也，君子而时中；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_31_1273818_comment'></div>小人之中庸也，小人而无忌惮也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_32_1273818_comment'></div></div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_33_1273818'>君子之中庸，中庸也；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_33_1273818_comment'></div>小人之中庸，反中庸也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_34_1273818_comment'></div>时中，<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_35_1273818", 1273818, "Clauses/83/Comments/0")'>时措</span>之宜也，中节者也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_35_1273818_comment'></div>反中庸则安于不善，此小人之中庸也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_36_1273818_comment'></div></div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_37_1273818'>子曰：中庸其至矣乎！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_37_1273818_comment'></div>民鲜能久矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_38_1273818_comment'></div></div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_39_1273818'>中，正性也；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_39_1273818_comment'></div>庸，常道也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_40_1273818_comment'></div>居正有常，所谓至德。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_41_1273818_comment'></div>安之为贵，安之悠久之道也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_42_1273818_comment'></div>择中庸而不能守，非所谓安之者也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_43_1273818_comment'></div></div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_44_1273818'>子曰：道之不行也，我知之矣，知者过之，愚者不及也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_44_1273818_comment'></div>道之不明也，我知之矣，贤者过之，不肖者不及也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_45_1273818_comment'></div>人莫不饮食也，鲜能知味也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_46_1273818_comment'></div>子曰：道其不行矣夫！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_47_1273818_comment'></div></div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_48_1273818'>所贵于知者，为其能有择也；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_48_1273818_comment'></div>所贵于贤者，为其能有见也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_49_1273818_comment'></div>人之望也，所赖以先民也，愚者固不及矣，知者又过中道，道何从而行乎？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_50_1273818_comment'></div>不肖固不及矣，贤者又过中道，道何从而明乎？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_51_1273818_comment'></div>孔子兴「道不行」之叹，盖叹贤而知者过犹不及。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_52_1273818_comment'></div>君子小人之间，不能以寸。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_53_1273818_comment'></div>饮食而知其味之正，斯无嗜好之僻也，毋偏毋颇，则近道矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_54_1273818_comment'></div>过物之累，所恶其凿者也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_55_1273818_comment'></div></div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_56_1273818'>子曰：舜其大知也与！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_56_1273818_comment'></div>舜好问而好察迩言，隐恶而扬善，执其两端，用其中于民，其斯以为舜乎！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_57_1273818_comment'></div></div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_58_1273818'>所恶于知者，为其凿也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_58_1273818_comment'></div>舜好问而好察迩言，盖未始自用，而亦不轻信之也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_59_1273818_comment'></div>迩言犹察，况其远者乎！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_60_1273818_comment'></div>天下之理，未有无二端者，好问而察迩言，遏恶而扬善，此执两端而用其中之道也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_61_1273818_comment'></div>欲求中而二端之弃，吾见其执一而非中也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_62_1273818_comment'></div></div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_63_1273818'>子曰：人皆曰予知，驱而纳诸罟擭陷阱之中，而莫之知辟也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_63_1273818_comment'></div>人皆曰予知，择乎中庸，而不能期月守也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_64_1273818_comment'></div>子曰：回之为人也，择乎中庸，得一善则拳拳服膺而弗失之矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_65_1273818_comment'></div></div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_66_1273818'>子曰：「君子可以大受，而不可小知也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_66_1273818_comment'></div>小人不可大受而可小知也」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_67_1273818_comment'></div>二者适反，君子小人之辨。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_68_1273818_comment'></div>众人之知，所谓小知也；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_69_1273818_comment'></div>惟知之小，陷乎大患而不自觉，虽知中庸之择，固无安之之理。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_70_1273818_comment'></div>夫小知而大知自见，惟不役于小尔。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_71_1273818_comment'></div>久于中庸之德，其惟大受者乎！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_72_1273818_comment'></div>颜子择中庸而得一善，所谓识道也；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_73_1273818_comment'></div>拳拳服膺则心服而身守之矣，未尝须臾离也，何从而失之乎！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_74_1273818_comment'></div>舜之为舜，不过执两端而用其中；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_75_1273818_comment'></div>颜之为颜，不过择中庸而得一善，君子之道，焉可诬也，在乎知本而已。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_76_1273818_comment'></div></div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_77_1273818'>子曰：天下国家可均也，爵禄可辞也，白刃可蹈也，中庸不可能也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_77_1273818_comment'></div></div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_78_1273818'>天下之事可以强为者，是皆可能者也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_78_1273818_comment'></div>中庸，天道也，不可以能之也，能之非道也，执中而无方者也，故曰：神而明之，存乎德行。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_79_1273818_comment'></div></div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_80_1273818'>子路问强，子曰：南方之强与？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_80_1273818_comment'></div>北方之强与？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_81_1273818_comment'></div>抑而强与？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_82_1273818_comment'></div>宽柔以教，不报无道，南方之强也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_83_1273818_comment'></div>君子居之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_84_1273818_comment'></div>衽金革，死而不厌，北方之强也；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_85_1273818_comment'></div>而强者居之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_86_1273818_comment'></div>故君子和而不流，强哉矫；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_87_1273818_comment'></div>中立而不倚，强哉矫；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_88_1273818_comment'></div>国有道，不变塞焉，强哉矫；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_89_1273818_comment'></div>国无道，至死不变，强哉矫。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_90_1273818_comment'></div></div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_91_1273818'>子路之问，盖强弱之强也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_91_1273818_comment'></div>孔子分君子、小人之辨，托南方、北方之强应之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_92_1273818_comment'></div>南方之强，君子居之，所谓养其大者，犯而不校之类；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_93_1273818_comment'></div>此伯夷、叔齐所以廉顽立懦，求仁得仁也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_94_1273818_comment'></div>北方之强，盖子路所谓强者，此匹夫之勇尔。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_95_1273818_comment'></div>和而不流，中立不倚，国有道不废，不为无道改节，自强矫矫，惟有道者能之，而汝也矫。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_96_1273818_comment'></div>矫，特立貌。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_97_1273818_comment'></div></div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_98_1273818'>子曰：素隐行怪，后世有述焉，吾弗为之矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_98_1273818_comment'></div>君子遵道而行，半涂而废，吾弗能已矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_99_1273818_comment'></div>君子依乎中庸，遁世不见知而不悔，唯圣者能之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_100_1273818_comment'></div></div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_101_1273818'>素隐行怪，掩其素行，行其僻左，以欺世盗名者，半途而废，自暴自弃者，若之人也，皆为人者也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_101_1273818_comment'></div>圣人有所不能为，为之不能已也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_102_1273818_comment'></div>君子之道，乾乾而不息者也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_103_1273818_comment'></div>遁世不见知而不闷，非惟人之知也，依乎中庸，徒以成身而已，非圣人而能与于此乎！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_104_1273818_comment'></div></div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_105_1273818'>君子之道，费而隐；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_105_1273818_comment'></div>夫妇之愚，可以与知焉，及其至也，虽圣人亦有所不知焉；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_106_1273818_comment'></div>夫妇之不肖，可以能行焉，及其至也，虽圣人亦有所不能焉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_107_1273818_comment'></div>天地之大也，人犹有所憾，故君子语大，天下莫能载焉；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_108_1273818_comment'></div>语小，天下莫能破焉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_109_1273818_comment'></div>《诗》云「鸢飞戾天，鱼跃于渊」，言其上下察也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_110_1273818_comment'></div>君子之道，造端乎夫妇，及其至也，察乎天地。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_111_1273818_comment'></div></div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_112_1273818'>道不远人，故虽匹夫匹妇，可以与知之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_112_1273818_comment'></div>至大至神，虽圣人不可以意知，不可以己能，所谓费而隐者，其中庸之至乎！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_113_1273818_comment'></div>天地之大，而人有所憾，不能成其大尔。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_114_1273818_comment'></div>夫子之言性与天道，不可得而闻也；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_115_1273818_comment'></div>言必有物，安得举而破之乎！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_116_1273818_comment'></div>造端乎夫妇，可以与知也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_117_1273818_comment'></div>察乎天地，所谓上下察也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_118_1273818_comment'></div>鸢飞鱼跃，各正性命者也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_119_1273818_comment'></div>致中和，天地位焉，万物育焉，豚鱼鸟兽，夫岂外此哉！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_120_1273818_comment'></div></div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_121_1273818'>子曰：道不远人，人之为道而远人，不可以为道。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_121_1273818_comment'></div>《诗》云：「伐柯伐柯，其则不远」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_122_1273818_comment'></div>执柯以伐柯，睨而视之，犹以为远。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_123_1273818_comment'></div></div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_124_1273818'>伐柯执柯以为远，此近于天地之大，犹有所恨者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_124_1273818_comment'></div>日用饮食，此民之不可须臾离者也，道不可离，又何远焉！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_125_1273818_comment'></div>知修道之在人，可以语率性之道矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_126_1273818_comment'></div></div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_127_1273818'>故君子以人治人，改而止，忠恕违道不远，施诸己而不愿，亦勿施于人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_127_1273818_comment'></div></div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_128_1273818'>以人治人，非求诸远者；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_128_1273818_comment'></div>过而能改，为善莫加焉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_129_1273818_comment'></div>夫子一以贯之，盖无所谓忠恕。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_130_1273818_comment'></div>忠恕之道，譬诸己而已矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_131_1273818_comment'></div>立己与物，则其去道逾远，无人我之辨，所谓一以贯之也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_132_1273818_comment'></div>不欲人之加诸我者，吾亦欲无加诸人，善推所为，能忠于恕，则近之矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_133_1273818_comment'></div>违道不远，犹非道也；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_134_1273818_comment'></div>一贯之也，无所俟于推矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_135_1273818_comment'></div></div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_136_1273818'>君子之道四，丘未能一焉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_136_1273818_comment'></div>所求乎子以事父，未能也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_137_1273818_comment'></div>所求乎臣以事君，未能也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_138_1273818_comment'></div>所求乎弟以事兄，未能也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_139_1273818_comment'></div>所求乎朋友先施之，未能也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_140_1273818_comment'></div>庸德之行，庸言之谨，有所不足，不敢不勉，有馀，不敢尽。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_141_1273818_comment'></div>言顾行，行顾言，君子胡不慥慥尔！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_142_1273818_comment'></div></div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_143_1273818'>君子之道四：君臣也，父子也，兄弟也，朋友之交也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_143_1273818_comment'></div>是皆不可能也，在修其在我者也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_144_1273818_comment'></div>庸德之行，庸言之谨，所谓修道也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_145_1273818_comment'></div>不足，不敢不勉，有馀，不敢尽，聿求厥中者也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_146_1273818_comment'></div>言行相应，则所谓君子之道者，丘未能一，所以能一之也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_147_1273818_comment'></div>慥慥谨也，言不可不慥慥然也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_148_1273818_comment'></div></div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_149_1273818'>君子素其位而行，不愿乎其外。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_149_1273818_comment'></div>素富贵行乎富贵，素贫贱行乎贫贱，素夷狄行乎夷狄，素患难行乎患难，君子无入而不自得焉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_150_1273818_comment'></div>在上位不陵下，在下位不援上，正己而不求于人，则无怨。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_151_1273818_comment'></div>上不怨天，下不尤人，故君子居易以俟命，小人行险以徼幸。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_152_1273818_comment'></div></div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_153_1273818'>素其位，所谓居易也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_153_1273818_comment'></div>不愿乎外，不易乎世者也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_154_1273818_comment'></div>不易乎世而行其素，无适而不中矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_155_1273818_comment'></div>上之陵下，下之援上，皆徇物而外驰者，故怨尤生焉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_156_1273818_comment'></div>内求于己，又谁怨乎？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_157_1273818_comment'></div>行险徼幸，盖不知命者也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_158_1273818_comment'></div>得之不得，曰有命，所以穷通而长乐也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_159_1273818_comment'></div></div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_160_1273818'>子曰：射有似乎君子，失诸正鹄，反求诸其身。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_160_1273818_comment'></div>君子之道，<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_161_1273818", 1273818, "Clauses/453/Comments/0")'>辟如</span>行远必自迩，<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_161_1273818", 1273818, "Clauses/454/Comments/0")'>辟如</span>登高必自卑。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_161_1273818_comment'></div>《诗》曰：「妻子好合，如鼓瑟琴。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_162_1273818_comment'></div>兄弟既翕，和乐且耽。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_163_1273818_comment'></div>宜尔室家，乐尔妻帑」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_164_1273818_comment'></div>子曰：父母其顺矣乎！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_165_1273818_comment'></div></div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_166_1273818'>道不远人，在我而已。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_166_1273818_comment'></div>大学之道，自正心诚意以至化家刑国，未有本乱而末治者也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_167_1273818_comment'></div>身不行，道不行于妻子，故君子必自反也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_168_1273818_comment'></div>仁之实，事亲是也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_169_1273818_comment'></div>孝悌为仁之本，岂有它哉！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_170_1273818_comment'></div></div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_171_1273818'>子曰：鬼神之为德，其盛矣乎！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_171_1273818_comment'></div>视之而弗见，听之而弗闻，体物而不可遗。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_172_1273818_comment'></div>使天下之人齐明盛服，以承祭祀，<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_173_1273818", 1273818, "Clauses/484/Comments/0")'>洋洋</span>乎如在其上，如在其左右。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_173_1273818_comment'></div>《诗》曰：「神之格思，不可度思。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_174_1273818_comment'></div>矧可射思，夫微之显」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_175_1273818_comment'></div>诚之不可掩如此夫。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_176_1273818_comment'></div></div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_177_1273818'>鬼神，至幽者也，而人莫敢不敬，以其体物之著也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_177_1273818_comment'></div>诚之不息则著，岂外是哉！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_178_1273818_comment'></div>譬射以有反身之仁，穷神以见<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_179_1273818", 1273818, "Clauses/499/Comments/0")'>至诚</span>之德，知微之显，知远之近，则可以言中矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_179_1273818_comment'></div></div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_180_1273818'>子曰：舜其大孝也与！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_180_1273818_comment'></div>德为圣人，尊为天子，富有四海之内，宗庙飨之，子孙保之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_181_1273818_comment'></div>故大德必得其位，必得其禄，必得其名，必得其寿。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_182_1273818_comment'></div>故天之生物，必因其材而笃焉，故栽者培之，倾者覆之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_183_1273818_comment'></div>《诗》曰：「嘉乐君子，宪宪令德。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_184_1273818_comment'></div>宜民宜人，受禄于天。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_185_1273818_comment'></div>保佑命之，自天申之」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_186_1273818_comment'></div>故大德者必受命。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_187_1273818_comment'></div></div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_188_1273818'>舜之受命，所谓天地合其德者，原其宗本，不过充事亲之孝，因天材而笃之尔。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_188_1273818_comment'></div>栽培倾覆，皆天道之当然者，舜何与焉！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_189_1273818_comment'></div>达天之德，而不能得天者，未之有也，而况于迩者乎！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_190_1273818_comment'></div></div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_191_1273818'>子曰：无忧者，其唯文王乎？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_191_1273818_comment'></div>以王季为父，以武王为子，父作之，子述之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_192_1273818_comment'></div>武王缵大王、王季、文王之绪，壹戎衣而有天下，身不失天下之显名，尊为天子，富有四海之内，宗庙飨之，子孙保之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_193_1273818_comment'></div>武王末受命，周公成文、武之德，追王大王、王季，上祀先公以天子之礼。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_194_1273818_comment'></div>斯礼也，达乎诸侯、大夫及士庶人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_195_1273818_comment'></div>父为大夫，子为士，葬以大夫，祭以士；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_196_1273818_comment'></div>父为士，子为大夫，葬以士，祭以大夫。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_197_1273818_comment'></div>期之丧，达乎大夫；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_198_1273818_comment'></div>三年之丧，达乎天子；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_199_1273818_comment'></div>父母之丧，无贵贱一也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_200_1273818_comment'></div>子曰：武王、周公，其<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_201_1273818", 1273818, "Clauses/574/Comments/0")'>达孝</span>矣乎！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_201_1273818_comment'></div>夫孝者，善继人之志，善述人之事者也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_202_1273818_comment'></div>春秋修其祖庙，陈其宗器，设其裳衣，荐其时食，宗庙之礼，所以序昭穆也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_203_1273818_comment'></div>序爵，所以辨贵贱也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_204_1273818_comment'></div>序事，所以辨贤也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_205_1273818_comment'></div>旅酬下为上，所以逮贱也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_206_1273818_comment'></div>燕毛，所以序齿也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_207_1273818_comment'></div>践其位，行其礼，奏其乐，敬其所尊，爱其所亲，事死如事生，事亡如事存，孝之至也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_208_1273818_comment'></div>郊社之礼，所以事上帝也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_209_1273818_comment'></div>宗庙之礼，所以祀乎其先也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_210_1273818_comment'></div>明乎郊社之礼，禘尝之义，治国其如示诸掌乎！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_211_1273818_comment'></div></div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_212_1273818'>无忧，得天者也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_212_1273818_comment'></div><span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_213_1273818", 1273818, "Clauses/609/Comments/0")'>达孝</span>，仁亲者也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_213_1273818_comment'></div>文王上有以得其亲，下有以施乎子，全其天乐，又何忧乎！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_214_1273818_comment'></div>武王、周公所以上继文王，善推其所为而已。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_215_1273818_comment'></div>近而事亲，大而事天，治人神，和上下，未始不本文王之道，无或不当理者，则文王之无忧，武王、周公之<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_216_1273818", 1273818, "Clauses/624/Comments/1")'>达孝</span>，其至矣乎！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_216_1273818_comment'></div>郊社禘尝，所以交神有道，指掌之示，夫何远之有哉！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_217_1273818_comment'></div></div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_218_1273818'>哀公<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_218_1273818", 1273818, "Clauses/630/Comments/0")'>问政</span>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_218_1273818_comment'></div>子曰：文武之政，布在<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_219_1273818", 1273818, "Clauses/633/Comments/0")'>方策</span>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_219_1273818_comment'></div>其人存，则其政举；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_220_1273818_comment'></div>其人亡，则其政息。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_221_1273818_comment'></div>人道敏政，地道敏树。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_222_1273818_comment'></div>夫政也者，蒲卢也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_223_1273818_comment'></div>故为政在人，取人以身，修身以道，修道以仁。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_224_1273818_comment'></div>仁者，人也，亲亲为大；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_225_1273818_comment'></div>义者，宜也，尊贤为大。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_226_1273818_comment'></div>亲亲之杀，尊贤之等，礼所生也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_227_1273818_comment'></div>在下位不获乎上，民不可得而治矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_228_1273818_comment'></div>故君子不可以不修身，思修身不可以不事亲，思事亲不可以不知人，思知人不可以不知天。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_229_1273818_comment'></div></div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_230_1273818'>知天，知命也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_230_1273818_comment'></div>知人，知道也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_231_1273818_comment'></div>为政在人，所谓<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_232_1273818", 1273818, "Clauses/666/Comments/0")'>人存政举</span>，<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_232_1273818", 1273818, "Clauses/667/Comments/0")'>人亡政息</span>者也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_232_1273818_comment'></div>地道之可察者，莫敏于树，人道之可通者，莫敏于政。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_233_1273818_comment'></div>文武之政具在，而人莫之行也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_234_1273818_comment'></div>得人行之，则其化物，何异于蒲卢之变？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_235_1273818_comment'></div>然待其人而后行尔。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_236_1273818_comment'></div>为政之道，得人为本。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_237_1273818_comment'></div>身不明道，无以知人；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_238_1273818_comment'></div>不先体仁，无以入道。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_239_1273818_comment'></div>君子之道无他，仁义而已矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_240_1273818_comment'></div>知事亲为人事之本，尊贤为适道之宜，由是而之焉，则礼可以义起矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_241_1273818_comment'></div>是故为政莫善于知天，知天莫尚于知人，知人莫大于尊亲，尊亲莫过于修身。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_242_1273818_comment'></div>知修身，则可以仁民矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_243_1273818_comment'></div>凡为政而不及于修身知化，皆非所谓正也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_244_1273818_comment'></div></div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_245_1273818'>天下之<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_245_1273818", 1273818, "Clauses/698/Comments/0")'>达道</span>五，所以行之者三：曰君臣也，父子也，夫妇也，昆弟也，朋友之交也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_245_1273818_comment'></div>五者天下之<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_246_1273818", 1273818, "Clauses/705/Comments/0")'>达道</span>也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_246_1273818_comment'></div>知、仁、勇三者，天下之达德也，所以行之者一也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_247_1273818_comment'></div>或生而知之，或学而知之，或困而知之，及其知之一也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_248_1273818_comment'></div>或安而行之，或利而行之，或勉强而行之，及其成功一也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_249_1273818_comment'></div></div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_250_1273818'>达德所以行<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_250_1273818", 1273818, "Clauses/717/Comments/0")'>达道</span>，一所以行三也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_250_1273818_comment'></div>仁以本之，知以通之，勇以成之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_251_1273818_comment'></div>知、仁、勇三者相须为用，而不可偏废，所以行之不过曰一而已。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_252_1273818_comment'></div>一者何也？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_253_1273818_comment'></div>所谓知天者也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_254_1273818_comment'></div>孔子曰：「不知命无以为君子也」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_255_1273818_comment'></div>清明在躬，气志如神，则知、仁、勇之三，未始离乎一也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_256_1273818_comment'></div>天下<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_257_1273818", 1273818, "Clauses/733/Comments/0")'>达道</span>亦大矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_257_1273818_comment'></div>交亲之际尽而足，通乎达德，则未见其五也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_258_1273818_comment'></div>斯道也在人而已。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_259_1273818_comment'></div>人之资质有限，能强而至于道，则与生而知之，安而行之者等尔。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_260_1273818_comment'></div>明于蒲卢之喻，则可以言政矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_261_1273818_comment'></div></div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_262_1273818'>子曰：好学近乎知，力行近乎仁，知耻近乎勇。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_262_1273818_comment'></div>知斯三者，则知所以修身。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_263_1273818_comment'></div>知所以修身，则知所以治人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_264_1273818_comment'></div>知所以治人，则知所以治天下国家矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_265_1273818_comment'></div></div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_266_1273818'>知、仁、勇三者，天下之达德也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_266_1273818_comment'></div>而好学、力行、知耻者近之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_267_1273818_comment'></div>三者之心，人皆有之，充其所为，则达德可致，身修而可以为政矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_268_1273818_comment'></div>修道之谓教，而于天下国家何有！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_269_1273818_comment'></div></div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_270_1273818'>凡为天下国家有<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_270_1273818", 1273818, "Clauses/764/Comments/0")'>九经</span>，曰：「修身也，尊贤也，亲亲也，敬大臣也，体群臣也，子庶民也，来百工也，柔远人也，怀诸侯也」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_270_1273818_comment'></div>修身则道立，尊贤则不惑，亲亲则诸父昆弟不怨，敬大臣则不眩，体群臣则士之报礼重，子庶民则百姓劝，来百工则财用足，柔远人则四方归之，怀诸侯则天下畏之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_271_1273818_comment'></div>齐明盛服，非礼不动，所以修身也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_272_1273818_comment'></div>去谗远色，贱货而贵德，所以劝贤也，尊其位，重其禄，同其好恶，所以劝亲亲也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_273_1273818_comment'></div>官盛任使，所以劝大臣也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_274_1273818_comment'></div>忠信重禄，所以劝士也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_275_1273818_comment'></div>时使薄敛，所以劝百姓也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_276_1273818_comment'></div>日省月试，既禀称事，所以劝百工也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_277_1273818_comment'></div>送往迎来，嘉善而矜不能，所以柔远人也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_278_1273818_comment'></div>继绝世，举<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_279_1273818", 1273818, "Clauses/807/Comments/0")'>废国</span>，治乱<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_279_1273818", 1273818, "Clauses/808/Comments/0")'>持危</span>，朝聘以时，厚往而薄来，所以怀诸侯也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_279_1273818_comment'></div>凡为天下国家有<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_280_1273818", 1273818, "Clauses/812/Comments/0")'>九经</span>，所以行之者一也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_280_1273818_comment'></div></div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_281_1273818'><span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_281_1273818", 1273818, "Clauses/814/Comments/0")'>九经</span>之治，自修身始，所谓行之者一，皆行其所无事也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_281_1273818_comment'></div>尊贤先于亲亲，所以立道也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_282_1273818_comment'></div>大臣之敬，不敢亵也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_283_1273818_comment'></div>小臣之体，恐疏之也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_284_1273818_comment'></div>子庶民，来百工，内之所以安治；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_285_1273818_comment'></div>柔远人，怀诸侯，外之所以信服。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_286_1273818_comment'></div>皆行其所无事，而以修身为本。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_287_1273818_comment'></div>君子之于天下也，将以安全之也，非徒有之而已。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_288_1273818_comment'></div>修身以教，各因其材而笃，使人得之观感，咸事其事，不敢不勉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_289_1273818_comment'></div>以尊乎治者，先王修道之教也，皆自我出也，所以行之者广，求诸己者，岂不约乎！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_290_1273818_comment'></div></div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_291_1273818'>凡事豫则立，不豫则废。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_291_1273818_comment'></div>言<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_292_1273818", 1273818, "Clauses/848/Comments/0")'>前定</span>则不跲，事<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_292_1273818", 1273818, "Clauses/849/Comments/0")'>前定</span>则不困，行<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_292_1273818", 1273818, "Clauses/850/Comments/0")'>前定</span>则不疚，道<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_292_1273818", 1273818, "Clauses/851/Comments/0")'>前定</span>则不穷。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_292_1273818_comment'></div>在下位不获乎上，民不可得而治矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_293_1273818_comment'></div>获乎上有道，不信乎朋友，不获乎上矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_294_1273818_comment'></div>信乎朋友有道，不顺乎亲，不信乎朋友矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_295_1273818_comment'></div>顺乎亲有道，反诸身不诚，不顺乎亲矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_296_1273818_comment'></div><span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_297_1273818", 1273818, "Clauses/863/Comments/0")'>诚身</span>有道，不明乎善，不诚乎身矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_297_1273818_comment'></div></div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_298_1273818'>治天下国家有<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_298_1273818", 1273818, "Clauses/866/Comments/0")'>九经</span>，所以行之者一，曰豫而已。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_298_1273818_comment'></div>事不可以意知，不可以已能，皆以修身为本。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_299_1273818_comment'></div>诚明乎善，所以立事也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_300_1273818_comment'></div>道也，行也，事也，言也，豫皆<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_301_1273818", 1273818, "Clauses/878/Comments/0")'>前定</span>之矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_301_1273818_comment'></div>见之事业，宁有穷乎！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_302_1273818_comment'></div>所贵乎坐进此道。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_303_1273818_comment'></div>诚者，所以立豫也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_304_1273818_comment'></div><span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_305_1273818", 1273818, "Clauses/884/Comments/0")'>至诚</span>与天地同流，不诚无物矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_305_1273818_comment'></div>不诚无物，则不明于善。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_306_1273818_comment'></div>交人之际，将何以有行乎！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_307_1273818_comment'></div>道之不行，不诚故尔。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_308_1273818_comment'></div>《易》曰：「君子安其身而后动，易其心而后语，定其交而后求」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_309_1273818_comment'></div>率此而行，则无往而不济矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_310_1273818_comment'></div></div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_311_1273818'>诚者，天之道也；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_311_1273818_comment'></div>诚之者，人之道也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_312_1273818_comment'></div>诚者，不勉而中，不思而得，从容中道，圣人也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_313_1273818_comment'></div>诚之者，择善而固执之者也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_314_1273818_comment'></div>博学之、审问之、慎思之、明辨之、笃行之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_315_1273818_comment'></div>有弗学，学之弗能，弗措也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_316_1273818_comment'></div>有弗问，问之弗知，弗措也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_317_1273818_comment'></div>有弗思，思之弗得，弗措也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_318_1273818_comment'></div>有弗辨，辨之弗明，弗措也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_319_1273818_comment'></div>有弗行，行之弗笃，弗措也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_320_1273818_comment'></div>人一能之，己百之，人十能之，己千之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_321_1273818_comment'></div>果能此道矣，虽愚必明，虽柔必强。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_322_1273818_comment'></div></div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_323_1273818'>天道，本然者也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_323_1273818_comment'></div>人道，当然者也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_324_1273818_comment'></div><span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_325_1273818", 1273818, "Clauses/936/Comments/0")'>至诚</span>，则无它事矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_325_1273818_comment'></div>此舜所以从欲而治，孔子纵心所欲而不踰矩也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_326_1273818_comment'></div>学、问、思、辨、行，所以诚之者也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_327_1273818_comment'></div>学之贵博，问之贵审，思之贵慎，辨之贵明，行之贵笃，知此五者，可以无失矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_328_1273818_comment'></div>审于问，笃于行，其功常十倍于人，未有不至者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_329_1273818_comment'></div>致曲能有诚也，学者所贵以<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_330_1273818", 1273818, "Clauses/954/Comments/0")'>诚身</span>也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_330_1273818_comment'></div>不诚乎身，则何贵于学！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_331_1273818_comment'></div>诚者，天之道也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_332_1273818_comment'></div>至明至强，固有之也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_333_1273818_comment'></div>柔愚逐物，害之也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_334_1273818_comment'></div><span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_335_1273818", 1273818, "Clauses/963/Comments/0")'>至诚</span>则本然者见矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_335_1273818_comment'></div>故学而未至于启蒙发蔀，如蒲卢之变，皆不足以言学也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_336_1273818_comment'></div></div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_337_1273818'>自诚明，谓之性；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_337_1273818_comment'></div>自明诚，谓之教。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_338_1273818_comment'></div>诚则明矣，明则诚矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_339_1273818_comment'></div>唯天下<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_340_1273818", 1273818, "Clauses/973/Comments/0")'>至诚</span>，为能尽其性；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_340_1273818_comment'></div>能尽其性，则能尽人之性；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_341_1273818_comment'></div>能尽人之性，则能尽物之性；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_342_1273818_comment'></div>能尽物之性，则可以赞天地之化育；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_343_1273818_comment'></div>可以赞天地之化育，则可以与天地参矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_344_1273818_comment'></div>其次致曲，曲能有诚，诚则形，形则著，著则明，明则动，动则变，变则化。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_345_1273818_comment'></div>唯天下<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_346_1273818", 1273818, "Clauses/991/Comments/0")'>至诚</span>为能化。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_346_1273818_comment'></div></div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_347_1273818'>性，本然者也；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_347_1273818_comment'></div>教，当然者也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_348_1273818_comment'></div>本然者未尝不著，由当然以即本然，则本然之性见矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_349_1273818_comment'></div>故虽圣人，未有不由学而至者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_350_1273818_comment'></div>所谓致曲也，知所谓教，自愚而圣，无难者，诚明盖一道尔。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_351_1273818_comment'></div>诚，天道也，地道也，人道也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_352_1273818_comment'></div>明者，诚之著也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_353_1273818_comment'></div><span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_354_1273818", 1273818, "Clauses/1012/Comments/0")'>至诚</span>复性，则上下咸察，吾性中之本然者，而焉有不尽哉！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_354_1273818_comment'></div>赞天地之化育，则可以言命矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_355_1273818_comment'></div>立命之道，自反身始也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_356_1273818_comment'></div>参乎天地，非尽性者能之乎！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_357_1273818_comment'></div>致曲无所不用其至者，每用其至，至则诚矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_358_1273818_comment'></div><span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_359_1273818", 1273818, "Clauses/1025/Comments/0")'>至诚</span>不息，则形而发见。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_359_1273818_comment'></div>故变化自我出也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_360_1273818_comment'></div></div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_361_1273818'><span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_361_1273818", 1273818, "Clauses/1028/Comments/0")'>至诚</span>之道，可以<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_361_1273818", 1273818, "Clauses/1029/Comments/0")'>前知</span>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_361_1273818_comment'></div>国家将兴，必有祯祥；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_362_1273818_comment'></div>国家将亡，必有妖孽。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_363_1273818_comment'></div>见乎蓍龟，动乎四体。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_364_1273818_comment'></div>祸、福将至，善必先知之，不善必先知之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_365_1273818_comment'></div>故<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_366_1273818", 1273818, "Clauses/1039/Comments/0")'>至诚</span>如神。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_366_1273818_comment'></div></div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_367_1273818'>天道之神，所以能体物者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_367_1273818_comment'></div>诚一之至，未始离于物也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_368_1273818_comment'></div><span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_369_1273818", 1273818, "Clauses/1044/Comments/0")'>至诚</span>与天道相似，故神神而明之，所谓格物也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_369_1273818_comment'></div>格物而不明，则善不善之将然者，无所潜于隐伏矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_370_1273818_comment'></div></div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_371_1273818'>诚者，自成也；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_371_1273818_comment'></div>而道，自道也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_372_1273818_comment'></div>诚者，物之终始，不诚无物。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_373_1273818_comment'></div>是故君子诚之为贵。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_374_1273818_comment'></div>诚者，非自成己而已也，所以<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_375_1273818", 1273818, "Clauses/1060/Comments/0")'>成物</span>也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_375_1273818_comment'></div>成己，仁也；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_376_1273818_comment'></div><span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_377_1273818", 1273818, "Clauses/1063/Comments/0")'>成物</span>，知也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_377_1273818_comment'></div>性之德也，合外内之道也，故<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_378_1273818", 1273818, "Clauses/1067/Comments/0")'>时措</span>之宜也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_378_1273818_comment'></div></div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_379_1273818'>天生烝民，有物有则。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_379_1273818_comment'></div>诚自成，道自道，夫岂外物邪？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_380_1273818_comment'></div>物则之尽，在诚而已，不诚无物，故以诚为物之终始也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_381_1273818_comment'></div>诚者物之终始，岂徒<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_382_1273818", 1273818, "Clauses/1078/Comments/0")'>诚身</span>而已哉！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_382_1273818_comment'></div>尽己尽物，则中和致而天地位，万物育。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_383_1273818_comment'></div>无物不一，无适非中，皆吾性之成德，安有内外之分乎！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_384_1273818_comment'></div>仁也知也，由<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_385_1273818", 1273818, "Clauses/1087/Comments/1")'>成己、成物</span>辨也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_385_1273818_comment'></div>仁知之辨，惟其时而已。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_386_1273818_comment'></div></div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_387_1273818'>故<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_387_1273818", 1273818, "Clauses/1090/Comments/0")'>至诚</span><span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_387_1273818", 1273818, "Clauses/1090/Comments/1")'>无息</span>，不息则久，久则徵，徵则悠远，悠远则博厚，博厚则高明。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_387_1273818_comment'></div>博厚所以载物也，高明所以覆物也，悠久所以<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_388_1273818", 1273818, "Clauses/1098/Comments/0")'>成物</span>也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_388_1273818_comment'></div>博厚配地，高明配天，悠久无疆，如此者不见而章，不动而变，无为而成，天地之道，可壹言而尽也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_389_1273818_comment'></div>其为物不贰，则其生物不测。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_390_1273818_comment'></div></div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_391_1273818'>不贰，诚也；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_391_1273818_comment'></div>不测，神也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_392_1273818_comment'></div>天地之神，亦诚而已矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_393_1273818_comment'></div><span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_394_1273818", 1273818, "Clauses/1115/Comments/0")'>至诚</span>斯不贰矣，不贰则自然不息，以至于尽神。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_394_1273818_comment'></div>天之高，地之厚，道之悠久，神之不测，惟<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_395_1273818", 1273818, "Clauses/1122/Comments/0")'>至诚</span>可以与于此。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_395_1273818_comment'></div>诚之为道，顾不大邪！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_396_1273818_comment'></div>不见而章，不动而变，无为而成，兹天道之变化。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_397_1273818_comment'></div>一言可尽，曰诚而已。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_398_1273818_comment'></div></div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_399_1273818'>天地之道，博也，厚也，高也，明也，悠也，久也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_399_1273818_comment'></div>今夫天，斯昭昭之多，及其无穷也，日月星辰系焉，万物覆焉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_400_1273818_comment'></div>今夫地，一撮土之多，及其广厚，载华岳而不重，振河海而不泄，万物载焉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_401_1273818_comment'></div>今夫山，一卷石之多，及其广大，草木生之，禽兽居之，宝藏兴焉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_402_1273818_comment'></div>今夫水，一勺之多，及其不测，鼋鼍蛟龙鱼鳖生焉，货财殖焉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_403_1273818_comment'></div></div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_404_1273818'>高明、博厚、悠久者，天地之道，此其可知者也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_404_1273818_comment'></div>天昭昭之多，地一撮土之多，山一卷石之多，水一勺之多，皆近而小者，及其至也，盖不可知之也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_405_1273818_comment'></div>其所以为天地山川而不可知者，曰诚而已。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_406_1273818_comment'></div></div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_407_1273818'>《诗》曰「惟天之命，于穆不已」，盖曰天之所以为天也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_407_1273818_comment'></div>「于乎不显，文王之德之纯」，盖曰文王之所以为文也，纯亦不已。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_408_1273818_comment'></div>大哉圣人之道！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_409_1273818_comment'></div><span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_410_1273818", 1273818, "Clauses/1180/Comments/0")'>洋洋</span>乎<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_410_1273818", 1273818, "Clauses/1180/Comments/1")'>发育</span>万物，峻极于天，优优大哉！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_410_1273818_comment'></div>礼仪三百，威仪三千，待其人而后行，故曰：苟不至德，至道不凝焉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_411_1273818_comment'></div></div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_412_1273818'>「于穆不已」，天之命也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_412_1273818_comment'></div>不显之德，文王所以受命也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_413_1273818_comment'></div>「<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_414_1273818", 1273818, "Clauses/1193/Comments/1")'>洋洋</span>乎<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_414_1273818", 1273818, "Clauses/1193/Comments/2")'>发育</span>万物，峻极于天」，礼仪、威仪，待其人而后行者，此于乎不显，纯亦不已之德也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_414_1273818_comment'></div>全乎天德，至道之归也，故曰：苟非其人，道不虚行。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_415_1273818_comment'></div>天之为天，文王之为文王，其道非它，诚之不息而已。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_416_1273818_comment'></div></div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_417_1273818'>故君子尊德性而道问学，致广大而尽精微，极高明而道中庸，温故而知新，敦厚以崇礼。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_417_1273818_comment'></div>是故居上不骄，为下不倍。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_418_1273818_comment'></div>国有道，其言足以兴国；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_419_1273818_comment'></div>无道，其默足以容。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_420_1273818_comment'></div>《诗》曰：「既明且哲，以保其身」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_421_1273818_comment'></div>其此之谓与？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_422_1273818_comment'></div>子曰：「愚而好自用，贱而好自专，生乎今之世，反古之道，如此者灾及其身者也」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_423_1273818_comment'></div></div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_424_1273818'>君子之道，行其所无事也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_424_1273818_comment'></div>德性，天性之本然者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_425_1273818_comment'></div>问学，尽性之本然者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_426_1273818_comment'></div>广大，措之四方上下而准者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_427_1273818_comment'></div>精微，至约之在人者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_428_1273818_comment'></div>高明，所以覆物者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_429_1273818_comment'></div>中庸，所以<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_430_1273818", 1273818, "Clauses/1242/Comments/0")'>成物</span>者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_430_1273818_comment'></div>温故，反本者；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_431_1273818_comment'></div>知新，知来者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_432_1273818_comment'></div>敦厚，自广者；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_433_1273818_comment'></div>崇礼，接物者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_434_1273818_comment'></div>皆以修身为本，廓而充之，则与天地准矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_435_1273818_comment'></div>为上处下，兴邦免祸，未有不自此途出，此明哲之所以保其身也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_436_1273818_comment'></div>学不由此，所谓反古之道也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_437_1273818_comment'></div>自用之愚，自专之贱，灾其自取之也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_438_1273818_comment'></div></div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_439_1273818'>非天子不议礼，不制度，不考文。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_439_1273818_comment'></div>今天下车同轨，书同文，行同伦，虽有其位，苟无其德，不敢作礼乐焉；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_440_1273818_comment'></div>虽有其德，苟无其位，亦不敢作礼乐焉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_441_1273818_comment'></div>子曰：「吾说夏礼，杞不足徵也；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_442_1273818_comment'></div>吾学殷礼，有宋存焉，吾学周礼，今用之，吾从周」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_443_1273818_comment'></div></div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_444_1273818'>礼乐，圣人之事也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_444_1273818_comment'></div>制礼作乐，天子之事也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_445_1273818_comment'></div>今天下有其时者也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_446_1273818_comment'></div>不以圣人居天子之位，礼乐不可作也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_447_1273818_comment'></div>此天之道也，作之者妄也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_448_1273818_comment'></div>夏礼不足徵矣，殷礼可学而不可从也；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_449_1273818_comment'></div>礼从时，孔子之所以从周也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_450_1273818_comment'></div>孔子之不能制礼作乐，无其时，且无其位也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_451_1273818_comment'></div></div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_452_1273818'>王天下有三重焉，其寡过矣乎！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_452_1273818_comment'></div>上焉者，虽善无徵，无徵不信，不信民弗从。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_453_1273818_comment'></div>下焉者，虽善不尊，不尊不信，不信民弗从。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_454_1273818_comment'></div>故君子之道，本诸身，徵诸庶民，考诸三王而不缪，建诸天地而不悖，质诸鬼神而无疑，百世以俟圣人而不惑。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_455_1273818_comment'></div>质诸鬼神而无疑，知天也；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_456_1273818_comment'></div>百世以俟圣人而不惑，知人也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_457_1273818_comment'></div>是故君子动而世为天下道，行而世为天下法，言而世为天下则，远之则有望，近之则不厌。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_458_1273818_comment'></div>《诗》曰：「在彼无恶，在此无射。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_459_1273818_comment'></div>庶几夙夜，以永终誉」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_460_1273818_comment'></div>君子未有不如此而蚤有誉于天下者也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_461_1273818_comment'></div></div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_462_1273818'>三重，三节也，上焉不可使知之者也，下焉日用而不知者也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_462_1273818_comment'></div>故君子用其中，必本于修身。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_463_1273818_comment'></div>本诸身，徵诸庶民，匹夫匹妇皆可与知之，上无太高，下无太渎，百姓心悦诚服，知所徵信，则敬而从之，所以适道也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_464_1273818_comment'></div>天地鬼神，先圣后圣，其道一而已矣，莫不以人为本。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_465_1273818_comment'></div>知天知人，不过内外之合而已。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_466_1273818_comment'></div>民有所徵而能信，无思不服，不可得而远近，吾修道之教也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_467_1273818_comment'></div>见誉有由矣，外是而求誉，非永终誉者也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_468_1273818_comment'></div></div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_469_1273818'>仲尼祖述尧、舜，宪章文、武，上律天时，下袭<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_469_1273818", 1273818, "Clauses/1362/Comments/0")'>水土</span>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_469_1273818_comment'></div><span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_470_1273818", 1273818, "Clauses/1363/Comments/0")'>辟如</span>天地之无不持载，无不覆帱；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_470_1273818_comment'></div><span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_471_1273818", 1273818, "Clauses/1365/Comments/0")'>辟如</span>四时之错行，如日月之<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_471_1273818", 1273818, "Clauses/1366/Comments/0")'>代明</span>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_471_1273818_comment'></div>万物并育而不相害，道并行而不相悖，小德<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_472_1273818", 1273818, "Clauses/1369/Comments/0")'>川流</span>，大德<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_472_1273818", 1273818, "Clauses/1370/Comments/0")'>敦化</span>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_472_1273818_comment'></div>此天地之所以为大也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_473_1273818_comment'></div></div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_474_1273818'>天地之大，诚而不已者也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_474_1273818_comment'></div>仲尼远继前圣，合德二仪，博厚高明，应物无迹，大小咸德，体合万殊。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_475_1273818_comment'></div>小者如水之流通，异行而俱入于海；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_476_1273818_comment'></div>大者如物之自化，不可见而未始踰闲。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_477_1273818_comment'></div>天德之至，所以为夫子哉！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_478_1273818_comment'></div></div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_479_1273818'>唯天下<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_479_1273818", 1273818, "Clauses/1386/Comments/0")'>至圣</span>，为能聪明睿知，足以有临也；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_479_1273818_comment'></div>宽裕温柔，足以有容也；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_480_1273818_comment'></div>发强刚毅，足以有执也；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_481_1273818_comment'></div>齐庄中正，足以有敬也；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_482_1273818_comment'></div>文理密察，足以有别也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_483_1273818_comment'></div>溥博渊泉，而时出之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_484_1273818_comment'></div>溥博如天，渊泉如渊，见而民莫不敬，言而民莫不信，行而民莫不说。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_485_1273818_comment'></div>是以声名洋溢乎中国，施及蛮貊。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_486_1273818_comment'></div>舟车所至，人力所通，天之所覆，地之所载，日月所照，霜露所队，凡有血气者，莫不尊亲，故曰配天。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_487_1273818_comment'></div></div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_488_1273818'>《书》曰：「帝德<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_488_1273818", 1273818, "Clauses/1416/Comments/1")'>广运</span>，乃圣乃神，乃武乃文」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_488_1273818_comment'></div>所见不同，一于<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_489_1273818", 1273818, "Clauses/1420/Comments/0")'>广运</span>之德尔。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_489_1273818_comment'></div>成配天之德，则其处身接物，皆顺而不妄，动而愈出，惟有本者能之尔。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_490_1273818_comment'></div>天地之大，何所不容，何所不逮。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_491_1273818_comment'></div>苟能此道，则有不言之信，无为之教，声容言动，其有不格者乎？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_492_1273818_comment'></div>此为天道之当然，所谓无思不服者也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_493_1273818_comment'></div>此道也，可以见天地，可以贯金石，有血气者而能外于是乎！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_494_1273818_comment'></div></div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_495_1273818'>唯天下<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_495_1273818", 1273818, "Clauses/1440/Comments/0")'>至诚</span>，为能<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_495_1273818", 1273818, "Clauses/1441/Comments/0")'>经纶</span>天下之大经，立天下之大本，知天地之化育，夫焉有所倚。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_495_1273818_comment'></div>肫肫其仁，渊渊其渊，浩浩其天。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_496_1273818_comment'></div>苟不固聪明圣知达天德者，其孰能知之！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_497_1273818_comment'></div></div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_498_1273818'>天下之大经，正也；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_498_1273818_comment'></div>天下之大本，中也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_499_1273818_comment'></div><span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_500_1273818", 1273818, "Clauses/1454/Comments/0")'>经纶</span>大经而立大本，非全于天者不能也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_500_1273818_comment'></div>求全于天，诚之而已。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_501_1273818_comment'></div>诚者，天地万物所受以生也，人之所以自成也，夫焉有所倚。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_502_1273818_comment'></div>然亦不可诬也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_503_1273818_comment'></div>望之弥高，钻之弥坚，瞻之在前，忽然在后，卓然如有立，参然如倚衡。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_504_1273818_comment'></div>有所倚者，其何能然！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_505_1273818_comment'></div>此道之本，可得而知者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_506_1273818_comment'></div>聪明圣知，性中之本然者，固有之也，唯全于天者尔。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_507_1273818_comment'></div>天全而后诚至，而中正立矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_508_1273818_comment'></div></div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_509_1273818'>《诗》曰「衣锦尚絅」，恶其文之著也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_509_1273818_comment'></div>故君子之道，<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_510_1273818", 1273818, "Clauses/1482/Comments/0")'>闇然</span>而<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_510_1273818", 1273818, "Clauses/1482/Comments/1")'>日章</span>；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_510_1273818_comment'></div>小人之道，<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_511_1273818", 1273818, "Clauses/1484/Comments/0")'>的然</span>而日亡。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_511_1273818_comment'></div>君子之道，淡而不厌，简而文，温而理，知远之近，知风之自，知微之显，可与<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_512_1273818", 1273818, "Clauses/1492/Comments/0")'>入德</span>矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_512_1273818_comment'></div></div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_513_1273818'>君子之道，其可知者，非其至也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_513_1273818_comment'></div>至不可以意知，而可与有行也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_514_1273818_comment'></div>小道<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_515_1273818", 1273818, "Clauses/1498/Comments/0")'>的然</span>，则<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_515_1273818", 1273818, "Clauses/1499/Comments/0")'>的然</span>而已矣，其将何以为远？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_515_1273818_comment'></div>知行远之自迩，登高之自卑，则可以适君子之道。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_516_1273818_comment'></div>淡而不厌，简而文，温而理，所谓不显之德也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_517_1273818_comment'></div>知德之不显，则知<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_518_1273818", 1273818, "Clauses/1509/Comments/0")'>的然</span>之恶矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_518_1273818_comment'></div>子夏以谓小道可观，而泥于致远；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_519_1273818_comment'></div>非可观，则何以为小道欤！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_520_1273818_comment'></div></div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_521_1273818'>《诗》云：「潜虽伏矣，亦孔之昭」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_521_1273818_comment'></div>故君子内省不疚，无恶于志。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_522_1273818_comment'></div>君子之所不可及者，其唯人之所不见乎！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_523_1273818_comment'></div>《诗》云：「相在尔室，尚不愧于屋漏」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_524_1273818_comment'></div>故君子不动而敬，不言而信。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_525_1273818_comment'></div></div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_526_1273818'>莫见乎隐，莫显乎微，君子所以戒慎恐惧也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_526_1273818_comment'></div>自反而缩，吾何慊乎哉！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_527_1273818_comment'></div>故君子敬其独尔。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_528_1273818_comment'></div>内不自欺，曾何人所不见之有。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_529_1273818_comment'></div>人所不见，而谓之难也，况己所不见乎！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_530_1273818_comment'></div>此君子所以大过人也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_531_1273818_comment'></div>「相在尔室」，室非身之外也，况室以为喻也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_532_1273818_comment'></div>内且不愧于屋漏，敬信其日用尔。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_533_1273818_comment'></div>不动之敬，不言之信，何有哉！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_534_1273818_comment'></div></div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_535_1273818'>《诗》曰：「奏假无言，时靡有争」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_535_1273818_comment'></div>是故君子不赏而民劝，不怒民威于鈇钺。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_536_1273818_comment'></div>《诗》曰：「不显惟德，百辟其刑之」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_537_1273818_comment'></div>是故君子笃恭而天下平。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_538_1273818_comment'></div></div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_539_1273818'>君子之道本诸身，加乎天下，莫不以修身为本也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_539_1273818_comment'></div>修身本乎诚敬，所谓笃恭也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_540_1273818_comment'></div>笃恭而天下平，修道之教也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_541_1273818_comment'></div>「奏假无言」，「不显惟德」，至于「时靡有争」、「百辟刑之」，惟<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_542_1273818", 1273818, "Clauses/1565/Comments/0")'>至诚</span>之格物，如此民心悦而诚服，天下有不平乎？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_542_1273818_comment'></div>庆赏刑威，劝赏之道也，不用而民不倍，诚之至也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_543_1273818_comment'></div></div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_544_1273818'>《诗》云：「予怀明德，不大声以色」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_544_1273818_comment'></div>子曰：「声色之于以化民，末也」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_545_1273818_comment'></div>《诗》曰「<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_546_1273818", 1273818, "Clauses/1578/Comments/4")'>德輶如毛</span>」，毛犹有伦，「上天之载，无声无臭」，至矣！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_546_1273818_comment'></div></div><div
