class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_547_1273818'>声色之感，岂所以化服人心乎！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_547_1273818_comment'></div>圣人不以感人，知德而已。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_548_1273818_comment'></div>故夫子言本末之辨。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_549_1273818_comment'></div>毛，轻微之至也；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_550_1273818_comment'></div>道，微乎微者也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_551_1273818_comment'></div>知道之妙，则知非毛之所可伦拟也，尚不可得而伦拟，矧可射乎！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_552_1273818_comment'></div>无声无臭，天道之始也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_553_1273818_comment'></div>中庸之学，所以研求性命之正，和同天人之理，不知天道之始，其何以为至哉！</div><div id='poem_sentence_554_1273818_comment'></div></div></div><div id='poem_1273820' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1273820' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1273820?labeling=true' target='_blank'>大学解</a><span class='authorDate'>（1164年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 南宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(31376, "南宋", "薛季宣", "poem_title_1273820")'>薛季宣</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1273820_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1273820'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1273820'>大学之道，在明明德，在亲民，在<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_0_1273820", 1273820, "Clauses/3/Comments/0")'>止于至善</span>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1273820_comment'></div>知止而后有定，定而后能静，静而后能安，安而后能虑。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1273820_comment'></div>虑而后能得。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1273820_comment'></div>物有本末，事有终始，知所先后，则近道矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1273820_comment'></div></div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_1273820'>天生烝民，有物有则；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1273820_comment'></div>民之秉彝，好是懿德。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1273820_comment'></div>能明是德，则近人矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1273820_comment'></div>能明是德，则知止矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1273820_comment'></div>有止故不妄，不妄故能安，能安故能动。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1273820_comment'></div>明德，本也；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1273820_comment'></div>应物，未也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1273820_comment'></div>故学道贵知本，知本则知缓急后先之序，而无过举之患矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1273820_comment'></div>不诚，未有能动者也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1273820_comment'></div>能安而静，物莫之挠，动而应物者，盖无难矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1273820_comment'></div></div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_14_1273820'>古之欲明明德于天下者，先治其国；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1273820_comment'></div>欲治其国者，先齐其家；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1273820_comment'></div>欲齐其家者，先修其身；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1273820_comment'></div>欲修其身者，先正其心；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1273820_comment'></div>欲正其心者，先诚其意；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1273820_comment'></div>欲诚其意者，先致其知。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1273820_comment'></div>致知在格物，物格而后知至，知至而后意诚，意诚而后心正，心正而后身修，身修而后家齐，家齐而后国治，国治而后天下平。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1273820_comment'></div>自天子以至于庶人，壹是皆以修身为本，其本乱而末治者否矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1273820_comment'></div>其所厚者薄，而其所薄者厚，未之有也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1273820_comment'></div>此谓知本，此谓知之至也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1273820_comment'></div></div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_24_1273820'>有良知，有小知。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1273820_comment'></div>良知，知德者也；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1273820_comment'></div>小知，小小知见也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1273820_comment'></div>域于小知，良知无自发也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1273820_comment'></div>能致其知，则知之至者见矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1273820_comment'></div>物物则之，在人者不明明德，则物无以尽；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1273820_comment'></div>不能尽物，则知之至者无自而发。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_30_1273820_comment'></div>格，至也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_31_1273820_comment'></div>物至则良知见也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_32_1273820_comment'></div>良知发见，则所知必至，意无有不诚，心无有不正，家国天下无不自正。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_33_1273820_comment'></div>所施者寡，所被者博矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_34_1273820_comment'></div>《洪范》曰：「皇建其有极，敛时五福，用敷锡厥庶民。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_35_1273820_comment'></div>惟时厥庶民于汝极，锡汝保极」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_36_1273820_comment'></div>所谓格物也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_37_1273820_comment'></div>「而康而色，曰予攸好德，汝则锡之福。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_38_1273820_comment'></div>时人斯其惟皇之极」，「汝弗能使有好于而家，时人斯其辜」，「汝虽锡之福，其作汝用咎」，以知德修身为本也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_39_1273820_comment'></div>「凡厥庶民，极之敷言，是训是行，以近天子之光」，曰天子作民父母，以为天下王，天子、庶人之一是也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_40_1273820_comment'></div>尧自「克明俊德」至于「黎民于变」，仲尼由「三十而立」至于「所欲不踰矩」，大学之道无它，在乎格物而已。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_41_1273820_comment'></div>不知尽己而欲尽人之道，难矣哉！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_42_1273820_comment'></div></div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_43_1273820'>所谓诚其意者，毋自欺也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_43_1273820_comment'></div>如恶恶臭，如好好色，此之谓<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_44_1273820", 1273820, "Clauses/123/Comments/0")'>自谦</span>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_44_1273820_comment'></div>故君子必慎其独也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_45_1273820_comment'></div>小人閒居，为不善无所不至，见君子而后厌然，掩其不善，而著其善。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_46_1273820_comment'></div>人之视己，如见其肺肝，然则何益矣？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_47_1273820_comment'></div>此谓诚于中，形于外，故君子必慎其独也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_48_1273820_comment'></div>曾子曰：「十目所视，十手所指，其严乎」？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_49_1273820_comment'></div>富润屋，德润身，心广体胖，故君子必诚其意。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_50_1273820_comment'></div></div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_51_1273820'>大学之道，自知德始，意诚而下，皆其序也，不可躐而至也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_51_1273820_comment'></div>慎独，致一之道也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_52_1273820_comment'></div>致一之至，不戒而严矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_53_1273820_comment'></div>《易》曰「无有师保，如临父母」，严之至也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_54_1273820_comment'></div>不欺其内，好之如色，恶于欺也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_55_1273820_comment'></div>如恶恶臭，自牧如此，非出勉强而后可以为。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_56_1273820_comment'></div>谦谦，慎独之始也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_57_1273820_comment'></div>不诚无物，君子其可欺乎！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_58_1273820_comment'></div>小人为欺，徒以自欺而已。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_59_1273820_comment'></div>十目十指，其将谁欺！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_60_1273820_comment'></div>德之润身，由其意之诚也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_61_1273820_comment'></div>心广体胖，至诚之道，将与天地参矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_62_1273820_comment'></div></div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_63_1273820'>《诗》云：「瞻彼淇澳，菉竹猗猗。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_63_1273820_comment'></div>有斐君子，如切如磋，如琢如磨。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_64_1273820_comment'></div>瑟兮僩兮，赫兮喧兮。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_65_1273820_comment'></div>有斐君子，终不可諠兮」！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_66_1273820_comment'></div>「如切如磋」者，道学也；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_67_1273820_comment'></div>「如琢如磨」者，自修也；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_68_1273820_comment'></div>「瑟兮僩兮」者，恂慄也；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_69_1273820_comment'></div>「赫兮喧兮」者，威仪也；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_70_1273820_comment'></div>「有斐君子，终不可諠兮」者，道盛德<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_71_1273820", 1273820, "Clauses/195/Comments/0")'>至善</span>，民之不能忘也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_71_1273820_comment'></div>《诗》云：「于戏，前王不忘」！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_72_1273820_comment'></div>君子贤其贤而亲其亲，小人乐其乐而利其利，此以没世不忘也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_73_1273820_comment'></div></div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_74_1273820'>《淇澳》之诗，美武公之德者，「如切如磋，如琢如磨」，所以形容之也，为天造而人功之似也，由其知学而自修者至也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_74_1273820_comment'></div>恂慄，和敬也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_75_1273820_comment'></div>威仪，度数也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_76_1273820_comment'></div>修道在己，而民之不能忘者，各以其所求得也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_77_1273820_comment'></div>君子乐得其志，小人乐得其事，凡以身修而应之有道也，故必诚其意。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_78_1273820_comment'></div></div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_79_1273820'>《康诰》曰「克明德」，《大甲》曰「顾諟天之明命」，《帝典》曰「克明峻德」，皆自明也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_79_1273820_comment'></div>汤之《盘铭》曰「茍日新，日日新，又日新」，《康诰》曰：「作新民」，《诗》曰「周虽旧邦，其命惟新」，是故君子无所不用其极。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_80_1273820_comment'></div></div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_81_1273820'>明德，俊德也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_81_1273820_comment'></div>日新，德新也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_82_1273820_comment'></div>惟天阴骘下民，民之受中以生者，明于是也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_83_1273820_comment'></div>圣人所以达天德也，由其固有之也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_84_1273820_comment'></div>克明则克类矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_85_1273820_comment'></div>文王纯亦不已，日新之盛德也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_86_1273820_comment'></div>尽斯尔也，用其极之谓也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_87_1273820_comment'></div></div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_88_1273820'>《诗》云：「邦畿千里，惟民所止」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_88_1273820_comment'></div>《诗》云：「缗蛮黄鸟，止于丘隅」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_89_1273820_comment'></div>子曰：「于止知其所止，可以人而不如鸟乎」！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_90_1273820_comment'></div>《诗》云：「穆穆文王，于缉熙敬止」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_91_1273820_comment'></div>为人君止于仁，为人臣止于敬，为人子止于孝，为人父止于慈，与国人交止于信。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_92_1273820_comment'></div>子曰：「听讼，吾犹人也，必也使无讼乎」！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_93_1273820_comment'></div>无情者不得尽其辞，大畏民志，此谓知本。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_94_1273820_comment'></div></div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_95_1273820'>止，极也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_95_1273820_comment'></div>仁之至，义之尽也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_96_1273820_comment'></div>知止而后能定，能定则不它矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_97_1273820_comment'></div>此谓知本。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_98_1273820_comment'></div>古人之所以大过人者，无所不用其极也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_99_1273820_comment'></div>能知所止，无所往而不建其极也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_100_1273820_comment'></div>黄鸟尚知安身之所，人而不求所止，可乎？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_101_1273820_comment'></div>讼之起也，中无所定也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_102_1273820_comment'></div>知止，自不欺矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_103_1273820_comment'></div>犯而不校，夫何讼之有乎！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_104_1273820_comment'></div></div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_105_1273820'>所谓修身在正其心者，身有所<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_105_1273820", 1273820, "Clauses/292/Comments/0")'>忿懥</span>，则不得其正；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_105_1273820_comment'></div>有所恐惧，则不得其正；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_106_1273820_comment'></div>有所好乐，则不得其正；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_107_1273820_comment'></div>有所忧患，则不得其正。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_108_1273820_comment'></div>心不在焉，视而不见，听而不闻，食而不知其味。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_109_1273820_comment'></div>此谓修身在正其心。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_110_1273820_comment'></div></div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_111_1273820'>中庸之学，以率性为道。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_111_1273820_comment'></div>喜怒哀乐，未发谓之中；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_112_1273820_comment'></div>有所<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_113_1273820", 1273820, "Clauses/309/Comments/0")'>忿懥</span>恐惧，则非所谓中，而本性昏矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_113_1273820_comment'></div>心者神明之舍，居中虚以治五官者也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_114_1273820_comment'></div>心为事夺，五官皆失其正，非所以安神明也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_115_1273820_comment'></div>一正心而本性正矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_116_1273820_comment'></div></div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_117_1273820'>所谓齐其家在修其身者，人之其所亲爱而辟焉，之其所<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_117_1273820", 1273820, "Clauses/320/Comments/0")'>贱恶</span>而辟焉，之其所畏敬而辟焉，之其所哀矜而辟焉，之其所敖惰而辟焉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_117_1273820_comment'></div>故好而知其恶，恶而知其美者，天下鲜矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_118_1273820_comment'></div>故谚有之曰：「人莫知其子之恶，莫知其苗之硕」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_119_1273820_comment'></div>此谓身不修，不可以齐其家。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_120_1273820_comment'></div></div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_121_1273820'>有一言而可以终身行之者，其恕乎！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_121_1273820_comment'></div>己所不欲，勿施于人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_122_1273820_comment'></div>君子之道无他，善推其所为而已。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_123_1273820_comment'></div>譬所亲爱，譬所畏敬，譬所哀矜，譬所敖惰。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_124_1273820_comment'></div>取譬反覆，视我心之轻重，则失其正者见矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_125_1273820_comment'></div>好而不知其恶，恶而不知其善，皆有所偏也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_126_1273820_comment'></div>心有所偏，则吾之是非错谬失伦；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_127_1273820_comment'></div>轻重无准，失其所以成已。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_128_1273820_comment'></div>近而无以齐家，犹爱而不知其子，贪而不知其苗也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_129_1273820_comment'></div>「无偏无党，王道荡荡」，则会归于极矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_130_1273820_comment'></div>是故修身以正心为本，心正而天下平矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_131_1273820_comment'></div></div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_132_1273820'>所谓治国必先齐其家者，其家不可教，而能教人者无之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_132_1273820_comment'></div>故君子不出家而成教于国。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_133_1273820_comment'></div>孝者所以事君也，弟者所以事长也，慈者所以使众也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_134_1273820_comment'></div>《康诰》曰：「如保赤子」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_135_1273820_comment'></div>心诚求之，虽不中，不远矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_136_1273820_comment'></div>未有学养子而后嫁者也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_137_1273820_comment'></div></div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_138_1273820'>《孝经》曰：闺门之内，具礼矣乎！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_138_1273820_comment'></div>严父严兄，妻子臣妾，犹百姓徒役也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_139_1273820_comment'></div>为国以礼，能踰上下之交乎！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_140_1273820_comment'></div>君子之为天下国家，皆以修身为本。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_141_1273820_comment'></div>事亲者可以事君，临下者可以临民。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_142_1273820_comment'></div>此皆不学而能者也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_143_1273820_comment'></div>若保赤子，敬之至也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_144_1273820_comment'></div>知敬恭之道，斯无失之者矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_145_1273820_comment'></div>君亲之辨，则惟其时物焉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_146_1273820_comment'></div>故曰「惟孝友于兄弟，施于有政，是亦为政，奚其为为政」，「克明俊德，黎民于变」，「文王以刑寡妻」者，御家邦，善推所为者乎！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_147_1273820_comment'></div></div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_148_1273820'>一家仁，一国兴仁；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_148_1273820_comment'></div>一家让，一国兴让；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_149_1273820_comment'></div>一人贪戾，一国作乱。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_150_1273820_comment'></div>其机如此，此谓一言<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_151_1273820", 1273820, "Clauses/408/Comments/0")'>偾事</span>，一人定国。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_151_1273820_comment'></div>尧、舜率天下以仁，而民从之；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_152_1273820_comment'></div>桀、纣率天下以暴，而民从之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_153_1273820_comment'></div>其所令反其所好，而民不从。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_154_1273820_comment'></div>是故君子有诸己，而后求诸人；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_155_1273820_comment'></div>无诸己，而后非诸人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_156_1273820_comment'></div>所藏乎身不恕，而能喻诸人者，未之有也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_157_1273820_comment'></div>故治国在齐其家。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_158_1273820_comment'></div>《诗》云：「桃之夭夭，其叶蓁蓁。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_159_1273820_comment'></div>之子于归，宜其家人」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_160_1273820_comment'></div>宜其家人，而后可以教国人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_161_1273820_comment'></div>《诗》云：「宜兄宜弟」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_162_1273820_comment'></div>宜兄宜弟，而后可以教国人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_163_1273820_comment'></div>《诗》云：「其仪不忒，正是四国」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_164_1273820_comment'></div>其为父子兄弟足法，而后民法之也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_165_1273820_comment'></div>此谓治国在齐其家。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_166_1273820_comment'></div></div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_167_1273820'>孔子曰：「声色之于化民也，末矣」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_167_1273820_comment'></div>修道之谓教。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_168_1273820_comment'></div>凡有血气，未有不缘观感而得也，此化俗之机也，皆自身修始也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_169_1273820_comment'></div>尧舜之民，灏灏如也；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_170_1273820_comment'></div>桀纣之民，比屋可诛，是岂声色化之也！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_171_1273820_comment'></div>皆观感然也，非勉强而从之也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_172_1273820_comment'></div>故君子必自反也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_173_1273820_comment'></div>内外之合，所谓恕也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_174_1273820_comment'></div>己所不欲，勿施于人，一言而可以终身行之者，笃恭而天下平，用此道也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_175_1273820_comment'></div>孔子曰：「其身正，不令而行；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_176_1273820_comment'></div>其身不正，虽令不从」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_177_1273820_comment'></div>故君子先正其身，不愿乎其外。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_178_1273820_comment'></div></div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_179_1273820'>所谓平天下在治其国者，上老老而民兴孝，上长长而民兴弟，上<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_179_1273820", 1273820, "Clauses/474/Comments/0")'>恤孤</span>而民<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_179_1273820", 1273820, "Clauses/474/Comments/1")'>不倍</span>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_179_1273820_comment'></div>是以君子有<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_180_1273820", 1273820, "Clauses/475/Comments/0")'>絜矩</span>之道也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_180_1273820_comment'></div>所恶于上，毋以使下；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_181_1273820_comment'></div>所恶于下，毋以事上；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_182_1273820_comment'></div>所恶于前，毋以先后；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_183_1273820_comment'></div>所恶于后，毋以从前；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_184_1273820_comment'></div>所恶于右，毋以交于左；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_185_1273820_comment'></div>所恶于左，毋以交于右。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_186_1273820_comment'></div>此之谓<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_187_1273820", 1273820, "Clauses/488/Comments/0")'>絜矩</span>之道。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_187_1273820_comment'></div></div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_188_1273820'>古之善为天下国家者，以天下为一家，中国为一人，无它焉，一以贯之而已。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_188_1273820_comment'></div>己所不欲，勿施于人，所出者正，则所从者顺。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_189_1273820_comment'></div>此之谓<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_190_1273820", 1273820, "Clauses/498/Comments/0")'>絜矩</span>之道，矩絜而民取制矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_190_1273820_comment'></div>是故动而为天下道，使民无不知爱其亲，知敬其长。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_191_1273820_comment'></div>风俗惇厚，盖所以率之者，顺矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_192_1273820_comment'></div>修道之教，不言之令，所谓<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_193_1273820", 1273820, "Clauses/508/Comments/0")'>絜矩</span>之道，皆以身修为本耳。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_193_1273820_comment'></div></div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_194_1273820'>《诗》云：「乐只君子，民之父母」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_194_1273820_comment'></div>民之所好好之，民之所恶恶之，此之谓民之父母。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_195_1273820_comment'></div>《诗》云：「节彼南山，维石岩岩。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_196_1273820_comment'></div>赫赫师尹，民具尔瞻」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_197_1273820_comment'></div>有国者不可以不慎，辟则为天下僇矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_198_1273820_comment'></div></div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_199_1273820'>国以民为本，民以心为本，君子之得其民，得其心也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_199_1273820_comment'></div>民之好恶，其心未尝不公；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_200_1273820_comment'></div>君子以民为心，公其好恶，则民爱之戴之，将父母若矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_201_1273820_comment'></div>为人上者，下人之所瞻望也，唯中立而不倚，则服而从之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_202_1273820_comment'></div>十手十目，其严乎！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_203_1273820_comment'></div>故君子在正其身。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_204_1273820_comment'></div></div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_205_1273820'>《诗》云：「殷之未丧师，克配上帝。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_205_1273820_comment'></div>仪监于殷，<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_206_1273820", 1273820, "Clauses/544/Comments/1")'>峻命</span>不易」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_206_1273820_comment'></div>道得众则得国，失众则失国。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_207_1273820_comment'></div>是故君子先慎乎德，有德此有人，有人此有土，有土此有财，有财此有用。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_208_1273820_comment'></div>德者本也，财者末也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_209_1273820_comment'></div>外本内末，争民施夺，是故财聚则民散，财散则民聚。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_210_1273820_comment'></div>是故言悖而出者，亦悖而入；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_211_1273820_comment'></div>货悖而入者，亦悖而出。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_212_1273820_comment'></div>《康诰》曰：「惟命不于常。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_213_1273820_comment'></div>道善则得之，不善则失之矣」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_214_1273820_comment'></div></div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_215_1273820'>皇天无亲，惟德是予，人之所欲，天必从之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_215_1273820_comment'></div>天听自我民听，天视自我民视。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_216_1273820_comment'></div>是故在得民也，得民在得心也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_217_1273820_comment'></div>惟有德者有以得民之心，故君子敬其独也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_218_1273820_comment'></div>政有本末，修身为本。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_219_1273820_comment'></div>身修德建，民可得而用矣，何财非我之有！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_220_1273820_comment'></div>不务建德而急于财用，民不知德，则惟财之靳，是施夺之道也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_221_1273820_comment'></div>是故有德斯有民，有民斯得天。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_222_1273820_comment'></div>后利先义，先王所以受命也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_223_1273820_comment'></div></div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_224_1273820'>《楚书》曰：「楚国无以为宝，惟善以为宝」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_224_1273820_comment'></div>舅犯曰：「<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_225_1273820", 1273820, "Clauses/593/Comments/1")'>亡人</span>无以为宝，仁亲以为宝」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_225_1273820_comment'></div>《秦誓》曰：「若有一个臣，断断兮无他技，其心休休焉，其如有容焉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_226_1273820_comment'></div>人之有技，若己有之；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_227_1273820_comment'></div>人之彦圣，其心好之；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_228_1273820_comment'></div>不啻若自其口出，寔能容之，以能保我子孙黎民，尚亦有利哉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_229_1273820_comment'></div>人之有技，媢疾以恶之；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_230_1273820_comment'></div>人之彦圣而违之，俾不通，寔不能容，以不能保我子孙黎民，亦曰殆哉」！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_231_1273820_comment'></div>唯仁人<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_232_1273820", 1273820, "Clauses/615/Comments/0")'>放流</span>之，迸诸四夷，不与同中国。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_232_1273820_comment'></div>此谓唯仁人为能爱人，能恶人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_233_1273820_comment'></div></div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_234_1273820'>为国之道，在知善恶；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_234_1273820_comment'></div>择善之道，仁身为本。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_235_1273820_comment'></div>仁身而后能择，能择然后知人，知人嘉善则可以保民矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_236_1273820_comment'></div>善人之道无它，贤贤而已。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_237_1273820_comment'></div>媢疾之心胜，则不能与人为善，而何以保身乎！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_238_1273820_comment'></div>惟仁者能好人，能恶人，修身而已。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_239_1273820_comment'></div></div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_240_1273820'>见贤而不能举，举而不能先，命也；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_240_1273820_comment'></div>见不善而不能退，退而不能远，过也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_241_1273820_comment'></div>好人之所恶，恶人之所好，是谓拂人之性，菑必逮夫身。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_242_1273820_comment'></div>是故君子有大道，必忠信以得之，<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_243_1273820", 1273820, "Clauses/647/Comments/0")'>骄泰</span>以失之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_243_1273820_comment'></div></div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_244_1273820'>进贤之法，莫崇礼貌；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_244_1273820_comment'></div>去恶之要，莫先克己。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_245_1273820_comment'></div>见贤而不能举，举而不能先，吾命之出者未至尔。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_246_1273820_comment'></div>见不善而不能退，退而不能远，是谁之过欤？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_247_1273820_comment'></div>惟能公其心者，可与论进贤退不肖之实。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_248_1273820_comment'></div>以百姓之心为心，忠信君子所以仁。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_249_1273820_comment'></div>菑必逮夫身者，<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_250_1273820", 1273820, "Clauses/663/Comments/0")'>骄泰</span>害之者也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_250_1273820_comment'></div>得失之要，在我而已。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_251_1273820_comment'></div>果能忠信，则身修而能公其好恶。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_252_1273820_comment'></div>贤不肖之进退，在此而不在彼也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_253_1273820_comment'></div></div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_254_1273820'>生财有大道，生之者众，食之者寡，为之者疾，用之者舒，则财恒足矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_254_1273820_comment'></div>仁者以财发身，不仁者以身发财。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_255_1273820_comment'></div>未有上好仁，而下不好义者也；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_256_1273820_comment'></div>未有好义，其事不终者也；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_257_1273820_comment'></div>未有府库财，非其财者也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_258_1273820_comment'></div>孟献子曰：「畜<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_259_1273820", 1273820, "Clauses/685/Comments/1")'>马乘</span>，不察于鸡豚；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_259_1273820_comment'></div>伐冰之家，不畜牛羊；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_260_1273820_comment'></div>百乘之家，不畜聚敛之臣，与其有聚敛之臣，宁有盗臣」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_261_1273820_comment'></div>此谓国不以利为利，以义为利也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_262_1273820_comment'></div>长国家而务财用者，必自小人矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_263_1273820_comment'></div>彼为善之，小人之使为国家，<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_264_1273820", 1273820, "Clauses/699/Comments/0")'>菑害</span>并至，虽有善者，亦<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_264_1273820", 1273820, "Clauses/701/Comments/0")'>无如之何</span>矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_264_1273820_comment'></div>此谓国不以利为利，以义为利也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_265_1273820_comment'></div></div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_266_1273820'>《易》称何以聚人？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_266_1273820_comment'></div>曰财。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_267_1273820_comment'></div>财者，国用所出，其可缓乎！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_268_1273820_comment'></div>虽然，为国务民之义而已。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_269_1273820_comment'></div>财者利之所在，人之所必争也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_270_1273820_comment'></div>人必争而我夺之，则利心生而礼义消矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_271_1273820_comment'></div>务民之义，则天下一家，而财不可胜用，藏之于下，犹在君也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_272_1273820_comment'></div>以财发身，用之者也；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_273_1273820_comment'></div>不知所以用之，身为财之役矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_274_1273820_comment'></div>故君子先正其本。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_275_1273820_comment'></div>为上有节，为下敦本，财用之出，庸有穷乎！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_276_1273820_comment'></div>是故务民之义，在乎修身以仁民；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_277_1273820_comment'></div>民化于仁，则爱之如父母，畏之如雷霆，上下情通，财皆可得而用，率斯道也，其有不终于义者乎！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_278_1273820_comment'></div>一家仁而一国兴仁，非他道也，务民之义，不以利为先尔。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_279_1273820_comment'></div>货悖而入，亦悖而出，此事势之必然者也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_280_1273820_comment'></div>谋大者尚皆不暇谋小，况君子而可争利于民乎？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_281_1273820_comment'></div>聚敛之臣，不知义之所在，害加于盗，以争利之民也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_282_1273820_comment'></div>民争利而至于乱，则不可救药矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_283_1273820_comment'></div>言利而析秋毫，必非养其大者之人也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_284_1273820_comment'></div>所见之小，恶知利义之和哉！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_285_1273820_comment'></div>惟知利者为义之和，而后可与共论生财之道。</div><div id='poem_sentence_286_1273820_comment'></div></div></div><div id='poem_1273819' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1273819' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1273819?labeling=true' target='_blank'>皇极解</a><span class='authorDate'>（1164年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 南宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(31376, "南宋", "薛季宣", "poem_title_1273819")'>薛季宣</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1273819_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1273819'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1273819'>《洪范》九畴，次五曰「建用皇极」，次皇极于中，数九畴用中于建也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1273819_comment'></div>尧舜之禅传，是中也；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1273819_comment'></div>孔颜之学明，是中也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1273819_comment'></div>自章句之说起，《洪范》为灾异之书，儒者间以意明之，其已駮矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1273819_comment'></div>无證而民不信，故君子难言之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1273819_comment'></div>虽然，极之敷言，帝之彝训也；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1273819_comment'></div>帝训不明于天下，走病焉，敷求厥中，颛以经学为解。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1273819_comment'></div></div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_7_1273819'>大中所谓命，中立而百顺备矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1273819_comment'></div>各正性命，民之中，中以生也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1273819_comment'></div>率性之谓道，中非自外至也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1273819_comment'></div>于时保之，莫非尔极也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1273819_comment'></div>《洪范》曰：「皇建其有极，敛时五福，用敷锡厥庶民。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1273819_comment'></div>惟时厥庶民于女极，锡女保极」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1273819_comment'></div>人之过也，各于其党；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1273819_comment'></div>人能弘道，非道之弘人也，是故立之斯立。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1273819_comment'></div>道之斯行，绥之斯来，动之斯和，无入而不自得者，惟不害者能之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1273819_comment'></div>天理之灭，人欲害之也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1273819_comment'></div>反身而诚，至诚则无他事矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1273819_comment'></div>百为事守，造次必于是，颠沛必于是，而后可以弗畔。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1273819_comment'></div>执中之道无它，卷卷服膺而已矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1273819_comment'></div>《洪范》曰：「凡厥庶民，亡有淫朋。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1273819_comment'></div>人亡有比德，惟皇作极。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1273819_comment'></div>凡厥庶民，有猷有为有守，女则念之」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1273819_comment'></div>子言之：「可与共学，未可与适道；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1273819_comment'></div>可与适道，未可与立；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1273819_comment'></div>可与立，未可与权；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1273819_comment'></div>君子之于天下也，无适也，无莫也，义之与比」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1273819_comment'></div>孟轲有言：「所谓大人者，言不必信，行不必果，惟义所在」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1273819_comment'></div>「执中无权，犹执一也」，是故识轻重之为贵，识轻重则知权矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1273819_comment'></div>君子之时中，时中为权，君子所过者化，所存者神，上下与天地同流。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1273819_comment'></div>夫大受者不可以小知也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_30_1273819_comment'></div>《洪范》曰：「不协于极，不罹于咎，皇则受之」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_31_1273819_comment'></div>语中德之盛也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_32_1273819_comment'></div>性无有不善，心无有不正，存心养性，所以事天也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_33_1273819_comment'></div>为仁由己，而由人乎哉！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_34_1273819_comment'></div>复之见天地之心不远。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_35_1273819_comment'></div>复无祗悔，一日克己复礼，而天下归仁焉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_36_1273819_comment'></div>一言善，而千里之外从之，是集义所生也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_37_1273819_comment'></div>《洪范》曰：「而康而色，曰予攸好德，女则锡之福。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_38_1273819_comment'></div>时人斯其惟皇之极」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_39_1273819_comment'></div>道不远人，在推其所为而已。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_40_1273819_comment'></div>「有一言而可以终身行之者，其恕乎！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_41_1273819_comment'></div>己所不欲，勿施于人」，「我不欲人之加诸我也，吾亦欲无加诸人」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_42_1273819_comment'></div>夫子之一以贯之，非多，学而识之也，所贵乎坐进此道。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_43_1273819_comment'></div>《诗》不云乎：「人亦有言，柔则茹之，刚则吐之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_44_1273819_comment'></div>惟仲山甫，柔亦不茹，刚亦不吐，不侮鳏寡，不畏彊御」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_45_1273819_comment'></div>故大人正己而物正，修身而天下平。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_46_1273819_comment'></div>《洪范》曰：「亡虐茕独，而畏高明。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_47_1273819_comment'></div>人之有能有为，使羞其行，而邦其昌」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_48_1273819_comment'></div>富有之谓大业，充实之谓美。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_49_1273819_comment'></div>渊泉溥博而时出之，有本者如是也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_50_1273819_comment'></div>古之欲明明德于天下者，必先修其身；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_51_1273819_comment'></div>欲修其身，必先正其心；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_52_1273819_comment'></div>欲正其心，必先诚其意。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_53_1273819_comment'></div>意诚而后心正，心正而后身修，身修而后家齐，家齐而后国治。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_54_1273819_comment'></div>内外正，天地之大义也，一正家而国定矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_55_1273819_comment'></div>舜刑于二女，文王刑于寡妻，至于兄弟，以御于家邦。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_56_1273819_comment'></div>身不行，道不行乎妻子。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_57_1273819_comment'></div>《洪范》曰：「凡厥正人，既富方谷。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_58_1273819_comment'></div>女弗能使有好于而家，时人斯其辜」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_59_1273819_comment'></div>有诸中，斯必形诸外。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_60_1273819_comment'></div>是故诚之为贵，诚之不息则著，著则通，通则放乎四方上下而准，不诚未有能动者也，故曰「不诚无物」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_61_1273819_comment'></div>《洪范》曰：「于其亡好德，女虽锡之福，其作女用咎」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_62_1273819_comment'></div>子言之，道其难行矣乎！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_63_1273819_comment'></div>智者过之，愚者不及也；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_64_1273819_comment'></div>贤者过之，不肖者不及也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_65_1273819_comment'></div>中庸其至矣乎！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_66_1273819_comment'></div>民鲜能久矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_67_1273819_comment'></div>舜执其两端而用其中于民。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_68_1273819_comment'></div>两端非执一也，其为物也不贰，则其动罔不中。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_69_1273819_comment'></div>在舜之命禹曰：「人心惟危，道心惟微。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_70_1273819_comment'></div>惟精惟一，允执厥中」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_71_1273819_comment'></div>人各有心，知微之显，则本心灼见，而中一见之矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_72_1273819_comment'></div>《洪范》曰：「毋偏毋颇，遵王之义<span class='inlineComment2'>（读如俄。）</span>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_73_1273819_comment'></div>毋有作好，遵王之道。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_74_1273819_comment'></div>毋有作恶，遵王之路。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_75_1273819_comment'></div>毋偏毋党，王道荡荡。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_76_1273819_comment'></div>毋党毋偏，王道平平。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_77_1273819_comment'></div>毋反毋侧，王道正直。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_78_1273819_comment'></div>会其有极，归其有极」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_79_1273819_comment'></div>天不言而四时行，百物生，以行与事，示之而已。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_80_1273819_comment'></div>圣人代天理物，修辞以尽意，知风霆雨露之无非教也，则可以言天矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_81_1273819_comment'></div>在《易·恒》之繇曰：「不恒其德，或承之羞」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_82_1273819_comment'></div>故君子言有物而行有常，有常之吉，不言之教也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_83_1273819_comment'></div>《洪范》曰：「曰皇极之敷言，是彝是训，于帝其训」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_84_1273819_comment'></div>人无有贵贱，道无有高下。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_85_1273819_comment'></div>不获乎上，无以使下；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_86_1273819_comment'></div>不获乎下，无以事上。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_87_1273819_comment'></div>中极之道，立九经以行三德者也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_88_1273819_comment'></div>故曰：欲为君，尽君道；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_89_1273819_comment'></div>欲为臣，尽臣道。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_90_1273819_comment'></div>中，其天下之道本乎！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_91_1273819_comment'></div>《记》曰：「喜怒哀乐之未发谓之中，发而皆中节谓之和」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_92_1273819_comment'></div>「致中和，天地位焉，万物育焉」，不能达之天下而可乎！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_93_1273819_comment'></div>《诗》云：「文王陟降，在帝左右。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_94_1273819_comment'></div>不识不知，顺帝之则」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_95_1273819_comment'></div>又曰：「夙夜匪懈，以事一人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_96_1273819_comment'></div>岂弟君子，民之父母」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_97_1273819_comment'></div>于乎！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_98_1273819_comment'></div>其有进于是夫。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_99_1273819_comment'></div>《洪范》曰：「凡厥庶民，极之敷言，是训是行，以近天子之光」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_100_1273819_comment'></div>曰：「天子作民父母，以为天下王」。</div><div id='poem_sentence_101_1273819_comment'></div></div></div><div id='poem_1273783' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1273783' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1273783?labeling=true' target='_blank'>春秋经解旨要序</a><span class='authorDate'>（1164年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 南宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(31376, "南宋", "薛季宣", "poem_title_1273783")'>薛季宣</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1273783_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1273783'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1273783'>《春秋》者何？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1273783_comment'></div>鲁史记之名也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1273783_comment'></div>史记何以名《春秋》？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1273783_comment'></div>春秋鲁历之所为更也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1273783_comment'></div>何更尔？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1273783_comment'></div>变周也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1273783_comment'></div>何言乎变周？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1273783_comment'></div>周正建子，以建寅为正岁，夏时得天，犹用夏也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1273783_comment'></div>春秋之序，鲁变之也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1273783_comment'></div>然则鲁变四时之序何？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1273783_comment'></div>史始官也，加春于建子而为王正月，建卯之月而为夏四月；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1273783_comment'></div>鲁史之作也，故凡春秋之序，皆舍周之旧也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1273783_comment'></div>曷为舍周之旧？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1273783_comment'></div>僭也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1273783_comment'></div>僭则《春秋》何以为经？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1273783_comment'></div>《春秋》反正之经也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1273783_comment'></div>《礼》、《易》、《诗》、《书》始终乎正，《春秋》纪录不正，所以反之正。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1273783_comment'></div>反正以其所不正，则五经之教，无时而或替也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1273783_comment'></div>《春秋》常事不书，书变常也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1273783_comment'></div>变常则何始于隐公？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1273783_comment'></div>疾始变也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1273783_comment'></div>始变昉于此乎？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1273783_comment'></div>前此矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1273783_comment'></div>前此则曷为始于此？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1273783_comment'></div>托始焉尔。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1273783_comment'></div>奈何《鲁春秋》之始也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1273783_comment'></div>《鲁春秋》之始何？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1273783_comment'></div>史之始作于诸侯也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1273783_comment'></div>诸侯孰谓？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1273783_comment'></div>谓隐公也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1273783_comment'></div>先王之制，诸侯无史，天子有外史，掌四方之志，而职于周之大史。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_30_1273783_comment'></div>隐之时也，始更鲁历而为鲁史，诸侯之有史，其周之衰乎！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_31_1273783_comment'></div>《费誓》、《秦誓》列于《周书》，《甘棠》、《韩奕》编之《南》、《雅》，乌在诸侯之有史也？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_32_1273783_comment'></div>晋《乘》始于殇叔，秦史作于文公，王室之微，诸侯之力政焉尔。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_33_1273783_comment'></div>然则《春秋》何取于鲁？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_34_1273783_comment'></div>因也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_35_1273783_comment'></div>其因何？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_36_1273783_comment'></div>因鲁之史记。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_37_1273783_comment'></div>其《春秋》，仲尼之志也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_38_1273783_comment'></div>《春秋》何以为仲尼之志？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_39_1273783_comment'></div>善扬其善，恶书其恶，而无私焉尔。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_40_1273783_comment'></div>何用见其善善恶恶而无私也？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_41_1273783_comment'></div>曰直笔以书其事，因事而致其辞，善则善，恶则恶，不为褒贬抑扬而乱是非之正也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_42_1273783_comment'></div>《春秋》用褒贬为道，其曰不为褒贬，何也？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_43_1273783_comment'></div>褒贬非仲尼之意也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_44_1273783_comment'></div>三家者托褒贬以为传也何？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_45_1273783_comment'></div>托褒贬以为传，舍褒贬则无以为传矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_46_1273783_comment'></div>三传之所为褒贬何也？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_47_1273783_comment'></div>不知《春秋》也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_48_1273783_comment'></div>三传何以不知《春秋》？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_49_1273783_comment'></div>《春秋》之教，治棼而不乱，处群而不党，是是非非，而天下之理归之矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_50_1273783_comment'></div>不知体要，不存教法，心移于毁誉，而事夺于《春秋》，则是褒贬之说，乱是非之正也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_51_1273783_comment'></div>事辞为教，《春秋》也，考辞而知其事，因事以观其理，不能显白，而待传以发，曰晦也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_52_1273783_comment'></div>晦之为道，传之为经，则事辞之教荒矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_53_1273783_comment'></div>孟轲有言曰：「王者之迹熄而诗亡，诗亡然后《春秋》作」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_54_1273783_comment'></div>平王之东也，变风害雅，五侯擅政，蛮夷乱夏，陪臣柄国，仲尼修《春秋》以明实录，将以反经之正，典常礼法无所与存焉，正乱常而还于旧物者也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_55_1273783_comment'></div>是故直书以明得失谓之辞，正辞以别是非谓之事，属辞比事，莫善于《春秋》，《春秋》之道，治乱之法也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_56_1273783_comment'></div>因史之僭，事乱之本也，事易其常，莫之或止，礼乐崩坏，《春秋》见之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_57_1273783_comment'></div>且夫事有是非，道有邪正，治乱之所从分也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_58_1273783_comment'></div>邪正不白，是非不辨，人行其意，其谁能有反！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_59_1273783_comment'></div>于是列纪以著之，修辞以述之，会盟朝聘之作，师役祠命之行，畋鱼游观之为，崩薨卒葬之礼，苟失其旧，无不备举。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_60_1273783_comment'></div>可行于当世，可示于方来，小人惮焉，君子达焉，则《春秋》之所用，尽在是矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_61_1273783_comment'></div>其事则齐桓、晋文，昭其义也；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_62_1273783_comment'></div>其文则史，正其辞也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_63_1273783_comment'></div>昭义正辞，则乱臣贼子云谁之不惧！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_64_1273783_comment'></div>拨乱世而反之正，《春秋》之谓也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_65_1273783_comment'></div>今夫浅害深非，乱是新变，旧传掩经，所谓反常也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_66_1273783_comment'></div>经之云正不累于辞，所谓服仁也；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_67_1273783_comment'></div>道反常，三传之失也；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_68_1273783_comment'></div>服仁守正，复古之道也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_69_1273783_comment'></div>经解之造，用经释经，而归正于经者也；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_70_1273783_comment'></div>旨要之谓，辞达而已。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_71_1273783_comment'></div>君子苟《春秋》之为好，不以弃传为过，而反求之《春秋》之义也，专门墨守，则非下走之所敢知。</div><div id='poem_sentence_72_1273783_comment'></div></div></div><div id='poem_1273781' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1273781' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1273781?labeling=true' target='_blank'>书古文训序</a><span class='authorDate'>（1164年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 南宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(31376, "南宋", "薛季宣", "poem_title_1273781")'>薛季宣</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1273781_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1273781'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1273781'>昔者子夏学《书》，见于孔子。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1273781_comment'></div>子曰：「商也，何为于《书」》？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1273781_comment'></div>子夏对曰：「《书》之论事也，昭昭如日月之代明，离离如星辰之错行，上有尧、舜之道，下有三王之义，凡商之所受《书》于夫子者，志之于心，弗敢忘。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1273781_comment'></div>退而穷居河济之间，深山之中，作壤室，编蓬户，弹琴瑟，歌咏先王之风，则可以发愤慨喟，忘己贫贱，有人亦乐之，无人亦乐之，而忽不知忧患与死也」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1273781_comment'></div>夫子造然变容曰：「嘻！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1273781_comment'></div>子殆可与言《书》矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1273781_comment'></div>虽然，其亦表之而已，未睹其里也」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1273781_comment'></div>颜渊曰：「何谓也」？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1273781_comment'></div>子曰：「窥其门而不入其中，睹其奥藏之所在乎？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1273781_comment'></div>然藏又非难也，丘尝悉心尽志以入其中，则前有高岸，后有大溪，填填正立而已矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1273781_comment'></div>是故《帝典》可以观美，《大禹谟》、《禹贡》可以观事，《皋陶谟》、《益稷》可以观政；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1273781_comment'></div>《洪范》可以观度，六誓可以观义，五诰可以观仁，《甫刑》可以观戒，通斯七者，《书》之大义举矣」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1273781_comment'></div>夫子于商之《书》谓之表，所以语回谓之义，自以填然正立，一时三语，若不相谋。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1273781_comment'></div>然则帝王之书，其不可识矣，君子察于三者而后可以言《书》。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1273781_comment'></div>今夫天之昭明，地之博厚，而人之灵于万物，匹夫匹妇无不固已知之，至于风霆雨霁之迭兴，海岳河山之流峙，所以知之盖鲜。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1273781_comment'></div>喜怒哀乐出乎尔者，其静其作，则或自知之不暇。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1273781_comment'></div>不察乎近，孰明乎远？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1273781_comment'></div>不得乎身，何以论古之人？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1273781_comment'></div>是故以《书》学《书》，《书》而已；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1273781_comment'></div>遗《书》学《书》，非《书》矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1273781_comment'></div>不以不遗，未足与于《书》之旨。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1273781_comment'></div>以而遗之，从之不可，或庶几乎！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1273781_comment'></div>《书》之大义云尔，子言之也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1273781_comment'></div>《书》之于事也，远而不阔，近而不迫，志尽而不怨，辞顺而不谄，吾于《高宗肜日》，见德有报之疾也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1273781_comment'></div>茍由其道，致其仁，则远方归志而致敬焉；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1273781_comment'></div>于《洪范》，见君子之不忍言人之恶，而质人之美也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1273781_comment'></div>发乎中而见乎外以成文者，其惟《洪范》乎！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1273781_comment'></div>尧、舜之命受于人，汤、武之命受于天，不读《诗》、《书》、《易》、《春秋》则不知圣人之心，无以别尧、舜之禅，汤、武之伐也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1273781_comment'></div>语之不切，见诸言外，斯言之辨，可以观虞、夏、商、周之书矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1273781_comment'></div>走之于《书》，学焉不如子夏，观焉何敢望回，世无孔子，则将何所取正？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1273781_comment'></div>述而藏之，以待能者，则庶乎以《书》观《书》者矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_30_1273781_comment'></div>隶古定《书》最古，孔氏文义，多本伏生之说，唐明皇帝更以正隶改定，而俗儒承诏，文多舛駮，古文是训，不劳乎是正之也；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_31_1273781_comment'></div>《书序》出于孔子，旨自有在，诠次百篇之后，将以归于古学，好古之僻，走何辞焉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_32_1273781_comment'></div>昔孔子学琴操而得文王之形，季子闻乐音而知其国之政，读其书不知其人，可乎！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_33_1273781_comment'></div>故叙篇端，论以读《书》之法。</div><div id='poem_sentence_34_1273781_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1165&endYear=1165')">1165年</a>　是年，在永嘉待阙。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1165&endYear=1165')">1165年</a>　在永嘉待阙。郑伯熊（字景望）被召为国子丞，季宣有诗相送。作品：送郑景望赴国子丞诗二首并序。<div id='poem_547911' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_547911' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/547911?labeling=true' target='_blank'>送郑景望赴国子丞诗二首<span style='margin: 0 0.5em'> 其一 </span></a><span class='authorDate'>（1165年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 南宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(31376, "南宋", "薛季宣", "poem_title_547911")'>薛季宣</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'>五言律诗</div></div><div id='poem_title_547911_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_547911'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_547911'>风喜樯乌顺，知难唤酒杯。<div id='poem_sentence_0_547911_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_547911'>好溪寒已半，京洛暖应回。<div id='poem_sentence_1_547911_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_547911'>僧舍方飘雪，江篱欲放梅。<div id='poem_sentence_2_547911_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_547911'>不须愁国步，之子栋梁材。<div id='poem_sentence_3_547911_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_547911'></div><div id='poem_sentence_4_547911_comment'></div></div></div><div id='poem_547912' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_547912' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/547912?labeling=true' target='_blank'><span style='margin: 0 0.5em'> 其二 </span></a><span class='authorDate'>（1165年）</span><br /><div class='titleIndent'>五言律诗</div></div><div id='poem_title_547912_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_547912'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_547912'>忾我论交晚，何堪又索居。<div id='poem_sentence_0_547912_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_547912'>朝阳鸣必凤，清水察无鱼。<div id='poem_sentence_1_547912_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_547912'>百恼愁成斛，群疑鬼载车。<div id='poem_sentence_2_547912_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_547912'>否臧亡可道，赢得腹诗书<sup class='reference inlineComment2'>⑴</sup>。<div id='poem_sentence_3_547912_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_547912'></div><div id='poem_sentence_4_547912_comment'></div></div><div class='poemNote' id='poem_note_547912'><div class='inline1'><div id='poem_sentence_3_547912_0'>⑴ 以上《艮斋先生薛常州浪语集》卷五</div></div></div><div id='poem_note_547912_comment'></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1165&endYear=1165')">1165年12月</a>　在永嘉待阙。十二月，汪澈知建康府，不久又除枢密使。薛季宣上书汪澈，论时事，斥偷安。作品：与汪留守明远。<div id='poem_1273709' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1273709' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1273709?labeling=true' target='_blank'>与汪留守明远书</a><span class='authorDate'>（1165年12月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 南宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(31376, "南宋", "薛季宣", "poem_title_1273709")'>薛季宣</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1273709_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1273709'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1273709'>窃闻北戎讲解议定，诚可以宽目下之急，在国家亦一幸事。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1273709_comment'></div>虽然，虏情万变，恐未必得其要领。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1273709_comment'></div>断国论者平居无事，鲜能推贤让能，与之图天下事，卒有意外之虑，则必逡循退缩，诿其素所难者与人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1273709_comment'></div>窃惟社稷重臣在江外者，其声名威著固无加于钧望，异时委寄，断可知矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1273709_comment'></div>如以宗祏之幸，径还国秉，格天之业，由中及外，盖有不待言。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1273709_comment'></div>脱有事如前虑，则今莫府部郡，地尽江表，循江以北，皆其障蔽。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1273709_comment'></div>如地形之险易，罗落之疏密，将帅之勇怯，兵旅之精惰，有不可不豫察者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1273709_comment'></div>帷幄之论，想已素定，投机合变，会当决胜于庙堂。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1273709_comment'></div>疏远之诚，然犹有不能自已者，妄陈僭说，敢惟不赐厌斥而采察之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1273709_comment'></div>凡今之究虏情者，例不喜闻其实；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1273709_comment'></div>图边事者，偷为一切之计。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1273709_comment'></div>充饥画饼，财足自诳。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1273709_comment'></div>大臣忧国，力之所不逮者，固无可奈何，有如得志得时，行其素蕴，上之正君治国，内清朝廷，下之泽物乂民，填安华夏，是皆道学馀事，当次第而行之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1273709_comment'></div>近时浅俗之夫，类皆见不及远。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1273709_comment'></div>方边隅无事，则趋时乡背，歌颂升平，一遇兵兴，则又高谈克复。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1273709_comment'></div>其说信美，然实非今所宜。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1273709_comment'></div>至如屯田淮南，所以守卫中国，如晁错、何承天之所建白，似可施之于时，而人无或图之，此又大不可晓者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1273709_comment'></div>自治之说，在所不论，比闻大政有礼官失于探讨，政府未能裁正者，所系甚大，处之当必有方，待人维持，众论固有属矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1273709_comment'></div>私心愤发，不觉深言，惟大度容之。</div><div id='poem_sentence_18_1273709_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1166&endYear=1166')">1166年</a>　是年，在永嘉候缺。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1166&endYear=1166')">1166年2月</a>　在永嘉候缺。二月中旬，作《风后握奇经》<div id='poem_1273771' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1273771' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1273771?labeling=true' target='_blank'>叙握奇经</a><span class='authorDate'>（1166年2月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 南宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(31376, "南宋", "薛季宣", "poem_title_1273771")'>薛季宣</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1273771_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1273771'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1273771'>《风后握奇经》三百八十四字，《续图》三百十五字，合标题七百九字，以众本《武经总要》阵法铨次，传著成章，而存异文于下，已缮写可读。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1273771_comment'></div>始，走游新都鱼复，观览武侯八阵石图，爱其文同《先天易图》，每恨阵法未能详究。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1273771_comment'></div>闻成都唐棋盘市虽章仇兼琼经始，而多得武侯遗意，履其市，道绳直，闾井交贯，百工类处，技别为行，识者晓知。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1273771_comment'></div>乍然入者至于尽日，迷不能去，方悟李卫公言古八阵龙虎蛇鸟之为旗，法前古服章之辨，为并识之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1273771_comment'></div>得《握奇经》读之，而八阵之势判然矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1273771_comment'></div>前闻袁隐君先生论六花阵法，明于八阵《握奇》，然后知其源本从来。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1273771_comment'></div>六八之阵不同，实方圆之数耳，触类而长，奇正庸有穷乎！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1273771_comment'></div>《握奇经》旧传风后受之玄女，用佐黄帝，杀蚩尤于涿鹿之野，荒唐之说，无所考信。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1273771_comment'></div>《汉志》兵阴阳家书有《风后》，刘歆、班固已言依托。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1273771_comment'></div>观公孙丞相注释，则非所谓书十三篇、图二卷者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1273771_comment'></div>先秦典籍，类皆口以传授，反复其义，未易以晚出浮伪訾也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1273771_comment'></div>《七略》兵家四种，《军礼》、《司马法》存者尚百五十五篇；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1273771_comment'></div>吴《孙子》八十二篇，图九卷；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1273771_comment'></div>齐《孙子》八十九篇，图四卷。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1273771_comment'></div>自神农、黄帝、伊尹、太公、范蠡、大夫种、吴起、魏公子、广武君、韩信、项羽诸家，其书具在，略皆亡矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1273771_comment'></div>今独《孙子》十三篇者为兵权谋之祖，论形势者本《握奇经》。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1273771_comment'></div>权谋在人，奇诡焉用？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1273771_comment'></div>形势、纪纲、军政，为天下者尚有取焉，又隐不章，可为懊叹。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1273771_comment'></div>旧文奥密，尚多错综微辞，传写不伦，颇难诵习。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1273771_comment'></div>李筌绘为八阵，既为不知而作；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1273771_comment'></div>《武经》虽存写本，不无讹以传讹，惟武侯《八阵石图》最为有徵。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1273771_comment'></div>走得马隆赞述，多所发明，遂为诠定其文，并绘阵图于后。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1273771_comment'></div>窃详古人存诸口诀之意，不敢妄疏条章，合图、赞以穷经，可以自得之矣。</div><div id='poem_sentence_22_1273771_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1166&endYear=1166')">1166年4月</a>　在永嘉候缺。四月，汪澈罢枢密使，出知宁国府。薛季宣致书汪澈，论士风与人才。作品：与汪枢使明远。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1166&endYear=1166')">1166年5月</a>　在永嘉候缺。五月，王炎知临安府。薛季宣致书王炎，论及酤榷之弊。作品：与王公明。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1166&endYear=1166')">1166年</a>　在永嘉候缺。是年，陈傅良在瑞安城南授徒，薛季宣时去访谈。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1167&endYear=1167')">1167年</a>　是年，在永嘉候缺，研究学术。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1167&endYear=1167')">1167年4月27日</a>　在永嘉候缺，研究学术。四月二十七日，有诗送郑伯英（字景元）作品：送郑景元赴秀州判官诗并序。<div id='poem_547913' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_547913' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/547913?labeling=true' target='_blank'>送郑景元赴秀州判官诗</a><span class='authorDate'>（1167年4月27日）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 南宋 · </span><a class='poemContent' id='poem_content_547913'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_547913'>恢炱煽炎毒，万里无来风。<div id='poem_sentence_0_547913_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_547913'>殿阁少微凉，况乃陌路中。<div id='poem_sentence_1_547913_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_547913'>纨扇可把挥，秋高网丝虫。<div id='poem_sentence_2_547913_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_547913'>冰山岂足恃，见睍聿消融。<div id='poem_sentence_3_547913_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_547913'>进退信惟谷，黄尘奈匆匆。<div id='poem_sentence_4_547913_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_5_547913'>郑君冰雪姿，干将依崆峒。<div id='poem_sentence_5_547913_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_6_547913'>竭蹶救头然，巾车佐元戎。<div id='poem_sentence_6_547913_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_7_547913'>生人在炽炭，吾何惮爞隆。<div id='poem_sentence_7_547913_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_8_547913'>往闻开元帝，逃暑绣岭宫。<div
