ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1167&endYear=1167')">1167年7月16日</a>　在永嘉候缺，研究学术。七月十六日，作《梦仙谣》诗。<div id='poem_548226' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_548226' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/548226?labeling=true' target='_blank'>梦仙谣</a><span class='authorDate'>（1167年7月16日）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 南宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(31376, "南宋", "薛季宣", "poem_title_548226")'>薛季宣</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_548226_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_548226'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_548226'>长城役罢骊山起，秦人断念还居里。<div id='poem_sentence_0_548226_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_548226'>一呼或化为侯王，避之却是神仙子。<div id='poem_sentence_1_548226_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_548226'>汉家宫殿生荆棘，桃源千<span class='inlineComment2'>（四库本作树）</span>树长春色。<div id='poem_sentence_2_548226_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_548226'>花香破鼻桃离离，只在人间人不知。<div id='poem_sentence_3_548226_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_548226'>梦中有客曾一到，屋舍<span class='inlineComment2'>（四库本作室）</span>衣裳殊草草。<div id='poem_sentence_4_548226_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_5_548226'>狗彘鸡豚还治生，若度流年不知老。<div id='poem_sentence_5_548226_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_6_548226'>南华砎壁连天起，人家庭户多流水。<div id='poem_sentence_6_548226_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_7_548226'>红碧夭桃百种花，不似凡间锦和绮。<div id='poem_sentence_7_548226_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_8_548226'>仙人容貌闲且都，居处虽贫乐有馀。<div id='poem_sentence_8_548226_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_9_548226'>老子桃红入双脸，皤然只有银为须。<div id='poem_sentence_9_548226_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_10_548226'>仙家女儿多茜衣，桃花宜面叶宜眉。<div id='poem_sentence_10_548226_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_11_548226'>离宫茅舍略相似，别有谯丽<span class='inlineComment2'>（四库本作丽谯）</span>璇为题。<div id='poem_sentence_11_548226_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_12_548226'>仙君名氏犹属秦，许由往往陪游人。<div id='poem_sentence_12_548226_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_13_548226'>老人石上问行客，传今几世秦之君。<div id='poem_sentence_13_548226_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_14_548226'>为言天下方南北，人鹿千龄经几得。<div id='poem_sentence_14_548226_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_15_548226'>嗟说来时桃始华，桃子而今未成核。<div id='poem_sentence_15_548226_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_16_548226'>祖龙往日亲曾见，六合连兵事攻战。<div id='poem_sentence_16_548226_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_17_548226'>北城紫塞南陆梁，倾赀未足供输挽。<div id='poem_sentence_17_548226_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_18_548226'>诚知黔首无聊生，侧目有诛正视刑。<div id='poem_sentence_18_548226_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_19_548226'>剖心不独商王受，当时论杀诸儒生。<div id='poem_sentence_19_548226_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_20_548226'>我本何辜一何幸，避役离乡共亡命。<div id='poem_sentence_20_548226_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_21_548226'>石髓药苗聊解饥，经年陡觉侪仙圣。<div id='poem_sentence_21_548226_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_22_548226'>讯今丞相胡为者，振古如今同土苴。<div id='poem_sentence_22_548226_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_23_548226'>惊起城头角调哀，顿觉令人小天下。<div id='poem_sentence_23_548226_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_24_548226'>秦政求仙徒尔为，避秦役夫能至之。<div id='poem_sentence_24_548226_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_25_548226'>还知道可无心得，学道有心无乃痴<sup class='reference inlineComment2'>⑴</sup>。<div id='poem_sentence_25_548226_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_26_548226'></div><div id='poem_sentence_26_548226_comment'></div></div><div class='poemNote' id='poem_note_548226'><div class='inline1'><div id='poem_sentence_25_548226_0'>⑴ 自注：事异于《桃花源记》者，皆梦中闻见尔。陶潜、伍安贫记黄道真误入桃花源事，世传以为仙，或曰非也。近人有梦游仍夕（四库本作反）者，道所闻见，为作《梦仙谣》。乾道三年孟秋几望翼日记。</div></div></div><div id='poem_note_548226_comment'></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1167&endYear=1167')">1167年</a>　在永嘉候缺，研究学术。是年，序赠甄云卿（字龙友）作品：送甄云卿赴西宫学官序。<div id='poem_1273756' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1273756' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1273756?labeling=true' target='_blank'>送甄云卿赴西宫学官序</a><span class='authorDate'>（1167年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 南宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(31376, "南宋", "薛季宣", "poem_title_1273756")'>薛季宣</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1273756_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1273756'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1273756'>道家者流，有金丹之术，走初未之学，谓如汉方士说煮丹砂为黄金则可以致神仙，其语信荒唐。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1273756_comment'></div>问于道学之老人，老人曰：「金丹谓内药也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1273756_comment'></div>鍊神与气，毋以外物伤吾内，则大药可就，而神仙可至，化人之袪可执，老枞之舌可咋，洪崖之肩可拍矣」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1273756_comment'></div>走矍然曰：「是在吾术内，但异名耳。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1273756_comment'></div>孟轲养浩然之气，四十而不动心，上论于古之人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1273756_comment'></div>此仲尼所以告曾参，曾参语单离居者，安得通方之士与之共论此术哉」！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1273756_comment'></div>云卿念八兄以《易》名家，壮岁取科甲，声名籍籍在人耳目间，一时公卿大人见之无不倾挹。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1273756_comment'></div>仕辄不偶，一乡之士类无得而亲疏者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1273756_comment'></div>走罢鄂陵长，始获交于云卿。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1273756_comment'></div>出《原丹》一篇，盖是说也，从此与之友。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1273756_comment'></div>孰知其为人自处之高，风斯在下，道心内切，罔象曷求焉！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1273756_comment'></div>是固云卿所长，要亦为云卿累。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1273756_comment'></div>云卿教国胄子，分职在闽中，腾踏飞黄，必自兹发也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1273756_comment'></div>居贫抗手，曾不能为黄金以赆其行。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1273756_comment'></div>尝闻闽多古书，道家之藏为甚富，云卿尚友，今之君子岂皆不足与于斯乎？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1273756_comment'></div>云卿志抗浮云，气充天地，持其志，无暴其气，日益日损，神气有不冲邪？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1273756_comment'></div>吾意其必且梦周公、骑箕尾矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1273756_comment'></div>以道之腴治己，以土苴治天下，云卿知必进于是也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1273756_comment'></div>走细人也，学不能造乎道，而浑沌之眉，倏忽之窍，所以丧吾真者日勃溪于方寸，辅仁者去，则金丹何冀焉？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1273756_comment'></div>云卿老于诗文，走不可以雷门布鼓。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1273756_comment'></div>序意惜别，又将以己之所甚难者责望吾云卿云。</div><div id='poem_sentence_20_1273756_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1167&endYear=1167')">1167年</a>　在永嘉候缺，研究学术。有书答石宗昭（字应之）作品：答石应之书。<div id='poem_1273722' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1273722' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1273722?labeling=true' target='_blank'>答石应之<span class='inlineComment2'>（宗昭）</span>书</a><span class='authorDate'>（1167年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 南宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(31376, "南宋", "薛季宣", "poem_title_1273722")'>薛季宣</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1273722_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1273722'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1273722'>古人以小学训习童蒙，皆大学之具也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1273722_comment'></div>大学之道，但神而明之尔。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1273722_comment'></div>小学之废久矣，为大学者失其养心之地，流于异教，不过空寂之归。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1273722_comment'></div>开物成务之功，宜无望于贤者，但令良心不泯，天理岂外于人邪？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1273722_comment'></div>反而求之，莫若存其大者，积小以成其大，是又不可忽也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1273722_comment'></div>惟能平其忿懥恐惧，好乐忧患，复六情之未发，心不失正，良知良能其何远之有乎？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1273722_comment'></div>用之读书，用之正身，用之事物与人皆是物也，非能洗濯心源，荡除旧习，涤去小智之凿，全吾天之聪明，尘埽随生，犹未艾也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1273722_comment'></div>孝悌忠恕，无非发吾诚意之中，况小者乎！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1273722_comment'></div>况庶物乎！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1273722_comment'></div>《帝典》以「聪明文思称尧」《洪范》「思睿作圣」，《书》不他道，曰「钦」曰「敬」而已，无小无大，是为得之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1273722_comment'></div>第能用志不分，则精义入神矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1273722_comment'></div>某学虽不足以知此，尝闻诸君子矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1273722_comment'></div>素丝何告，愿无以人废言也。</div><div id='poem_sentence_12_1273722_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1167&endYear=1167')">1167年</a>　在永嘉候缺，研究学术。致书王彦恭。作品：与王彦恭经略。<div id='poem_1273728' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1273728' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1273728?labeling=true' target='_blank'>与王彦恭经略<span class='inlineComment2'>（趯）</span>书</a><span class='authorDate'>（1167年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 南宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(31376, "南宋", "薛季宣", "poem_title_1273728")'>薛季宣</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1273728_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1273728'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1273728'>某顷者试令武昌，伏承持节湖右，名位辽绝，势相万也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1273728_comment'></div>初无蟠木先容之助，又无牖间半面之雅，庭参一见，即蒙礼异，教诏警策，凡可以安全之者无所不至。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1273728_comment'></div>趋事之日虽浅，一邑之庇居多。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1273728_comment'></div>既而台旆行部荆南，遂迁淮甸，道出境上，某适微恙，弗克请违，乃辱台翰抚存，告以方药。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1273728_comment'></div>未几，浙西旋旆，获于东坡江步一瞻台表，悤悤诀去，罙用耿耿。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1273728_comment'></div>继于鄂陵知后吏处领所赐教墨，道左罕便，既不时报谢，于今凡五阅岁，而起居之问，不一通于记史，颜之厚矣，负负何言！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1273728_comment'></div>自惟赋性迂疏，拙于援上，诒怒当路有矣，能见亮者，夫岂无之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1273728_comment'></div>其间亦有同舟遇风，权相成济，利涉之后，势合相忘，独于门墙，初无丝发之补。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1273728_comment'></div>在官则帡幪厦屋，既去则恩意绸缪，非徒此也，又以无似之迹，为延誉于士夫间。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1273728_comment'></div>某非强交之人，台座又非有资于某者，眷顾如此，未之前闻，上论于古之人，或可以一二数耳。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1273728_comment'></div>愚陋何以得此？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1273728_comment'></div>言之增愧。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1273728_comment'></div>然闻媢贤丑正，寔繁有徒，自分无以逾人，虚名适足为累，兼恐上负知人之鉴，不可不察。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1273728_comment'></div>知我足矣，何足为人道哉！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1273728_comment'></div>既沐爱怜，敢布以请。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1273728_comment'></div>昨承开府番禺，倚眷方渥，旋抗章高举，竟获成命。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1273728_comment'></div>请祠之奏，遂能自出机杼，无所蹈袭，其言直而不肆，婉而成章，当有识者知之，众人固不识也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1273728_comment'></div>东坡侍见，尝闻君子馀论，以为进退有义，得失有命，君子赢为君子，小人谬为小人，仰知将以教督其愚，然亦有以卜知我公自处之地。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1273728_comment'></div>独善可矣，如天下何？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1273728_comment'></div>世衰道微，士风骫骳，藩垣使节，其能不为身计，称股肱耳目之寄如台座者，不知其谁？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1273728_comment'></div>适用之才，济时之具，况不秖此。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1273728_comment'></div>此何时也，而犹侍祠于外，得非明镜冤于丑妇，抑厉揭浅深之计固当然邪？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1273728_comment'></div>岳下雅多英隽之游，今无改旧俗否？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1273728_comment'></div>衡镜平皎，所得当日富也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1273728_comment'></div>某里居待次，经涉四年，虽家徒四壁，日忧糊口之不继，而单贫无事，得以料理书学，无当官箠楚患，亦足以为乐。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1273728_comment'></div>然性质凡下，既无简书之畏，而狂躁之态，投闲复作，尤一身之累也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1273728_comment'></div>金华阙期在明夏，决曹虽事省于县，而人命所系，惧非智虑所及。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1273728_comment'></div>矧时有难易，制不在己，每一念此，如负芒刺，益知浮湛州县，今亦良难。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1273728_comment'></div>台座政为吏师，雅辱怜眷，有可见教，愿与闻之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1273728_comment'></div>某虽下材，不敢不勉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1273728_comment'></div>自同众人，敬以幅书通记，伏幸台察！</div><div id='poem_sentence_30_1273728_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1167&endYear=1167')">1167年</a>　在永嘉候缺，研究学术。致书刘朔（复之）作品：与刘复之。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1168&endYear=1168')">1168年</a>　在永嘉候阙。曾与何溥（字商霖）讨论经学。作品：答何商霖书三篇。<div id='poem_1273741' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1273741' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1273741?labeling=true' target='_blank'>答何商霖<span class='inlineComment2'>（溥）</span>书<span style='margin: 0 0.5em'> 其一 </span></a><span class='authorDate'>（1168年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 南宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(31376, "南宋", "薛季宣", "poem_title_1273741")'>薛季宣</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1273741_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1273741'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1273741'>某闻君子之风，为日久矣，声迹之相闻，又两年来矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1273741_comment'></div>小儿获抠衣于讲席之下，于今行复更岁，政缘疏怠，阻造下风，虽未能日接音容，得馀论于文字之间，开发厚矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1273741_comment'></div>比辱临访，言及忠父邶、鄘之论。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1273741_comment'></div>某忠父友也，实相忘于道术之际，有所论辩，各不敢为隐遁之说以相罔，故虽言有当否，然各自其所见。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1273741_comment'></div>窃意要知本末同异，有以订其是非，故敢不蔽愚固之踪，用以求教，非欲自售于下，执事必我察也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1273741_comment'></div>六经载道之器，远矣大矣！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1273741_comment'></div>某既妄有论著，且以荐于洪儒大学之前，明眼难懑，多见其不自量也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1273741_comment'></div>退即所安，知其手足俱露，方此内愧，以为将必大得罪于门墙，札翰之来，则知与其进也，甚幸甚幸！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1273741_comment'></div>示谕六经之说于左右，未能无疑。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1273741_comment'></div>读书欲有所疑，此伊洛先生语也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1273741_comment'></div>吾人于学未能了了于不疑之际，夫不疑者，盖无所自见，不然，则蛙之在井，圣言天远，宁俄而可料哉？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1273741_comment'></div>惟善学者未能无疑，疑者问辩之所由生也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1273741_comment'></div>谆谆之云，何造道之深也！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1273741_comment'></div>至谓疑理之蠹，则某请得一言。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1273741_comment'></div>疑固多端，左右之疑，固将有所决也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1273741_comment'></div>理道必疑而决，则疑未为蠢也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1273741_comment'></div>众咻谁佐之，惑能决焉，则定矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1273741_comment'></div>某学未足以及此，然于众多之说，不敢必以为是。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1273741_comment'></div>此亦得之先生长者之论，馀皆不知而妄作耳。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1273741_comment'></div>谓毕其说，非所敢当，信能有以规之，则亦非所隐也，清论之及，故敢复之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1273741_comment'></div>见交之文，仰荷垂示，非徒属辞命意、无愧前作，论交之际，益足以知君子之不苟也，知感知幸！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1273741_comment'></div>某窃有所见，不敢不荐其说。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1273741_comment'></div>此赋之质美矣，近世才人实未之见，吾曹盖相期于古人不到之地，夫何今之足云。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1273741_comment'></div>讲道之馀，加游息焉于楚骚、汉赋之作，则笔端之力，久之当益有所到，此不可以言尽也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1273741_comment'></div>古人虽曰作文害道，然犹未通于一弛一张之说，有如尽舍他事而专心文墨，则非我所敢知也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1273741_comment'></div>草草脩报，幸恕疏略，不宣。</div><div id='poem_sentence_25_1273741_comment'></div></div></div><div id='poem_1273742' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1273742' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1273742?labeling=true' target='_blank'><span style='margin: 0 0.5em'> 其二 </span></a><span class='authorDate'>（1168年）</span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1273742_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1273742'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1273742'>前书裁答，方惧不韪，荐承教毕，蒙有以警笃之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1273742_comment'></div>其意良厚，有以知君子成人之际，且足以见涵泳于六经之说，不以先儒之故而置圣人之学，知感且羡。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1273742_comment'></div>书辞宜答，请以所闻于古者复之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1273742_comment'></div>《诗》古乐经，其文古之乐章也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1273742_comment'></div>《书》云「诗言志，歌永言，声依永，律和声」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1273742_comment'></div>三百五篇，非主于声而已。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1273742_comment'></div>太史以《国风》系先王之旧俗，二《雅》识其政事，《颂》播郊庙，是皆职在太师。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1273742_comment'></div>盖遒人之官，采之天下，施之当时之用者，先王之盛，教化之美，颂声翕绎，蔼然成章；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1273742_comment'></div>不得于言，固有不能宣之于口，被之声律以供燕享。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1273742_comment'></div>有若《南陔》、《华黍》之诗者，虽有其义，不强为之辞，《仪礼》所谓「笙诗」，先儒以为「亡诗」者也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1273742_comment'></div>王者功成之乐，庶人无所得议，纯一之化加乎四海，比屋皆有可封之俗，四方安有殊风之事？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1273742_comment'></div>召伯、韩侯之盛，一皆见之周诗《甘棠》诸篇，《南》、《雅》所存是也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1273742_comment'></div>四诗之正，恶有所谓变哉！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1273742_comment'></div>观于《诗序》之文，正变为可言矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1273742_comment'></div>《诗序》于先王之诗，皆言朝廷之所施用，其所称叙，不过一诗之指，幽、厉之雅，邶、鄘之风，视前序为何如，正变断可知矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1273742_comment'></div>《豳风》之作，亦以当时之变，豳尝变而终不克变，成王、周公之美也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1273742_comment'></div>变风见录，起于政俗之异，国自为次，固其理也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1273742_comment'></div>邶、鄘之不合于槔，自其邦人之不予，诗章自为篇帙，初非前有其叙。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1273742_comment'></div>圣人删《诗》而为之次第，则因变之后先。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1273742_comment'></div>《国风》起周、召、邶、鄘而迄于豳，见治乱有可易之理，以为序有因改，斯为不可厚诬。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1273742_comment'></div>反鲁所正之诗，止于雅、颂而已。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1273742_comment'></div>来教谓诗之作，起于教化之衰，所引康王晏朝将以为据。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1273742_comment'></div>《鲁诗》所道，可尽信哉？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1273742_comment'></div>求《诗》名于《礼经》，非后世之作也，又安知《关雎》作刺之说，非赋其诗者乎？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1273742_comment'></div>降王而不予卫，是非圣人为之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1273742_comment'></div>邶、鄘灭而音存，故非卫所能乱。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1273742_comment'></div>政不加于天下，则王不可谓雅，所云系于所得之国，与《春秋》之王城，确实而言，惟其理也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1273742_comment'></div>然诸侯之兼并，非独邶、鄘为然，圣人不以灭国系诸侯之风，非为因地而已。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1273742_comment'></div>夫《诗》家之音律，犹《易》家之象数。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1273742_comment'></div>圣人于《易》称君子之道四，则《诗》之声文未可以一偏取。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1273742_comment'></div>孔子固尝弦歌合乐，而亦不为无取于辞，《角弓》、《唐棣》之去留，义之可得而通者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_30_1273742_comment'></div>《诗》、《书》之序，非圣人莫能为之，然其源流岂无所自？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_31_1273742_comment'></div>《易·系》不皆兴于孔氏，则《诗》、《书》可以类知；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_32_1273742_comment'></div>如孔子自己为之，必有不能为之者矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_33_1273742_comment'></div>走于反古《诗》说虽不主于先儒，于其所长不敢废也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_34_1273742_comment'></div>古人尚或采之刍荛之说，况圣人之徒欤！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_35_1273742_comment'></div>务相乖违，非反古之道矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_36_1273742_comment'></div>不能自明六经之学，诚世儒之深病；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_37_1273742_comment'></div>凿空以攻先儒之论，不亦后世之罪人哉？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_38_1273742_comment'></div>观于会通，则古道之去人不远矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_39_1273742_comment'></div>某学不足以知古，乐求古人之意，聊以自诳，非缘垂世而立言。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_40_1273742_comment'></div>执事不以其愚，赐之提诲，此道之不作久矣，何意闻此正音！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_41_1273742_comment'></div>临文者不敢借辞，益重不敏，幸为隐恶。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_42_1273742_comment'></div>本不足以示人，既沐诲言，不敢不既其说，尚为时复教告，以适翘跂之私！</div><div id='poem_sentence_43_1273742_comment'></div></div></div><div id='poem_1273743' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1273743' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1273743?labeling=true' target='_blank'><span style='margin: 0 0.5em'> 其三 </span></a><span class='authorDate'>（1168年）</span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1273743_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1273743'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1273743'>披读枉教，申理前说，辨而不置，真古人之事也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1273743_comment'></div>钦叹三复，敢不敬应！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1273743_comment'></div>《诗》学有二，曰声曰辞，声辞合而成章，乃古之道。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1273743_comment'></div>然尔人之情性，古犹今也，情有哀乐，声文称焉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1273743_comment'></div>听其语可以合其声，闻其音可以知其意，二者不可以毫釐判，于人有不省乎？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1273743_comment'></div>孔子学于操而得文王，识《鸱鹄》之知道，声辞交见，庸有二是，故舍乐论文与释文而言乐，皆非《诗》学之正。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1273743_comment'></div>近世填词之作，始别异于声文，唐固不然，况乎三王之代！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1273743_comment'></div>季子论乐，夫其殊于圣人，其以《小雅》为周之衰，亦汉儒所云，讥小己之得失，有为而发，其可遂泥其言乎？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1273743_comment'></div>文中子不与季子之知乐，近于眉睫之论，然其旨各有在，不可合也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1273743_comment'></div>在《乡饮酒》、《燕礼》、《射礼》已有《二南》诸篇，虽为不必尽出文王之时，要为周公制礼作乐所用，以为思先王而歌其事，则幽王之诗有之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1273743_comment'></div>详而味焉，与《南》、《雅》之古诗，或居然异矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1273743_comment'></div>仲尼归正《雅》、《颂》，岂徒然哉，序之云云，不待言也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1273743_comment'></div>学经而他求于传，不若专意于经；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1273743_comment'></div>传皆不同，则经学之文，不几于或矣？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1273743_comment'></div>序据《左氏》，谓《棠棣》为召公作，《毛传》以为周公，二者莫知适从，则序燕兄弟之文，非其所论拟也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1273743_comment'></div>古学在求其正，不当论出之后先，如惟前出之从，则《书》之古文，不若汉世今文者矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1273743_comment'></div>妄意无似，非执事谁为裁之！</div><div id='poem_sentence_16_1273743_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1168&endYear=1168')">1168年</a>　在永嘉候阙。曾与徐元德论学。作品：答徐元德书。<div id='poem_1273746' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1273746' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1273746?labeling=true' target='_blank'>答徐元德书</a><span class='authorDate'>（1168年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 南宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(31376, "南宋", "薛季宣", "poem_title_1273746")'>薛季宣</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1273746_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1273746'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1273746'>某不肖之迹，见疑于世久矣，兹蒙三兄眷顾特达，然若有不相察者，敢尽底蕴，冀一知之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1273746_comment'></div>某不天，蚤失义方之教，仕缘世荫，以惰，不为科举之习；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1273746_comment'></div>居官无有治迹可以求知上官，心非不欲为众所为，顾不能耳。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1273746_comment'></div>士夫过听，或意其尚古人之学，不知我者遂有众多之论。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1273746_comment'></div>二者于我虽异，其不相知一也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1273746_comment'></div>前某伏蒙轩车见过，不以愚鄙见绌，荐辱名刺，则以学生自居。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1273746_comment'></div>昔者徂徕先生与泰山先生德比名齐，举相似也，徂徕自谓不及，拜泰山而师之，天下方知有师，后世不以为过。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1273746_comment'></div>以二先生道谊之重，天下信之不疑，回既倒之狂澜，故不难也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1273746_comment'></div>执事之举，将无欲效之乎？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1273746_comment'></div>师道不明，此风之不作也久矣，某小丑，其何德以堪之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1273746_comment'></div>在执事自处则贤，为人谋者，不几乎厝诸炉炭之上矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1273746_comment'></div>某虽不学，其自知甚明，非其有而取之，何远于盗？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1273746_comment'></div>此所以逡循退辟，不敢当大礼之盛也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1273746_comment'></div>兹蒙镌谕谆复，敢固以辞。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1273746_comment'></div>且执事之下交，夫岂徒然者也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1273746_comment'></div>某所期于大君子者，端不在是。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1273746_comment'></div>不我瑕弃，固所愿也，尚几以道为度，毋以过礼见加，姑为朋友相从，亦足以讲道为学，无骇俗目，使某不堕于好为人师之诮。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1273746_comment'></div>爱人以德之意，想执事乐为之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1273746_comment'></div>用布腹心，切希财量。</div><div id='poem_sentence_18_1273746_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1168&endYear=1168')">1168年</a>　在永嘉候阙。曾与潘文叔（友文）论学。作品：与潘文叔。<span class='inlineComment2'>（交游者姓名为录入者据张良权点校《薛季宣集》（上海社会科学院出版社2003年版）卷二十五补。系年作品名称为录入者据张良权点校《薛季宣集》（上海社会科学院出版社2003年版）卷二十五补。）</span><div id='poem_1273750' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1273750' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1273750?labeling=true' target='_blank'>与潘文叔<span class='inlineComment2'>（友文）</span>书</a><span class='authorDate'>（1168年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 南宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(31376, "南宋", "薛季宣", "poem_title_1273750")'>薛季宣</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1273750_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1273750'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1273750'>某获从端叔昆季游，愿见之日甚久，驱驰扰扰，恨未承望。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1273750_comment'></div>兹蒙华翰之贶，辱临之以师弟子礼，倥侗自视，何敢当盛意邪！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1273750_comment'></div>继今如不鄙夷，略之是望。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1273750_comment'></div>示谕为学之道，某何足以知之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1273750_comment'></div>过听之求，仰见好问不耻，然而索金贫子，终何以副所欲乎？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1273750_comment'></div>抑某闻之，君子虽极高明，道实中庸，虚受谦持，无有偏颇好恶，自无不得其正之患。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1273750_comment'></div>君臣之义，父子之亲，天理昭昭，不容与易，惟居之以平荡，持之以兢业，终身可以无畔，其至要当有见，必自得而后能安之也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1273750_comment'></div>若以恬漠为进，某恐难乎应事于纷纭耳。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1273750_comment'></div>所恶于知正，谓其凿空无之说于此，不与存焉，承问之廑，聊及尔耳。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1273750_comment'></div>斯道要非语言所及，纤寸笔舌，讵能写方寸哉！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1273750_comment'></div>又蒙于某求师，某学焉不足，顾将何以为献？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1273750_comment'></div>惧涂公之耳目，无以祗复将命，切几照亮！</div><div id='poem_sentence_11_1273750_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1168&endYear=1168')">1168年</a>　在永嘉候阙。曾与潘必胜论学。作品：复潘秀才书。<div id='poem_1273752' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1273752' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1273752?labeling=true' target='_blank'>复潘秀才<span class='inlineComment2'>（必胜）</span>书</a><span class='authorDate'>（1168年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 南宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(31376, "南宋", "薛季宣", "poem_title_1273752")'>薛季宣</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1273752_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1273752'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1273752'>某闻士俯仰以求人，不若修身而约处，侥求而得位，不若守道而安贫。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1273752_comment'></div>是故瓮牖蓬枢，原思弦诵而不辍；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1273752_comment'></div>豆羹箪食，颜子独乐而有馀。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1273752_comment'></div>夫二子之贤，学仲尼之道，是非无意于世，志抗浮云而厉世矫俗者，惟所存者大，固将以有为耳。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1273752_comment'></div>执事乡兄奋布衣之下，怀济时之策，愤匈奴之未灭，将折箠而鞭之，历聘王公，以求得意，其志略亦大矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1273752_comment'></div>抑某尝闻之曰：「四郊多垒，卿大夫之辱也」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1273752_comment'></div>居斯时，履斯位、任斯责者，固当开幕府以下士，辟东阁以礼贤，汲汲营营，惟恐失天下之士，而无与成虑定功，亦何敢傲当世之贤者！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1273752_comment'></div>士无官守，无言责，政当以道自处，待时而动。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1273752_comment'></div>必在上者，不若魏侯之于干木，昭烈之于孔明，降其礼，听其言，亦不屑就之矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1273752_comment'></div>我国家取士之法，不许以它求致，国有庠，乡有贡，茍以叙进青紫，可如芥而拾。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1273752_comment'></div>是虽未足以拟原思、颜子之事，然比之侥求而俯仰者，为有间矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1273752_comment'></div>执事乡兄夫岂无意于此？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1273752_comment'></div>四年仆仆，夫何为哉？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1273752_comment'></div>愿一思乡巷之言，自反之也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1273752_comment'></div>国之鸿儒，有若泰山先生、横渠先生者，弱冠盖尝俱以策略历干边帅，为执事之事矣，得范文正、韩魏王一语，退而学道，遂为当世宗师。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1273752_comment'></div>在圣人之门，将不愧于二子。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1273752_comment'></div>乡使往而不反，果得一官，齿于辕门，厕于赤籍，二人埋没久矣，将何以名于世，而况未可必邪。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1273752_comment'></div>某虽托在里闾，方远官以糊口，瓜期云及，归计茫如，顾且自悔自怜，惧无以当盛意，虽不敢自同先正，犹思所以仰报铿金之语。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1273752_comment'></div>大言无当，执事乡兄其谅之乎？</div><div id='poem_sentence_18_1273752_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1168&endYear=1168')">1168年</a>　在永嘉候阙。曾与程时行论学。作品：复程秀才书。<div id='poem_1273753' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1273753' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1273753?labeling=true' target='_blank'>复程秀才<span class='inlineComment2'>（时行）</span>书</a><span class='authorDate'>（1168年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 南宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(31376, "南宋", "薛季宣", "poem_title_1273753")'>薛季宣</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1273753_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1273753'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1273753'>某闻之：君子以道义为重，爵禄为轻。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1273753_comment'></div>王公大人立乎人之本朝，一嚬呻，一呼吸，足为天下利病，系生民之休戚；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1273753_comment'></div>而韦布之士，穷居约处，乐先王之道，不求闻达于诸侯，其相望为甚殊，而其寔无异道。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1273753_comment'></div>苟在位者不能以身任道，则为士者谊亦不屑求知于人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1273753_comment'></div>何哉？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1273753_comment'></div>道义之在亡而已，穷达何有于我？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1273753_comment'></div>果能此道也，则箪瓢陋巷，青琐玉堂，易地皆然，夫何贵贱之有？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1273753_comment'></div>是则舜之饭糗茹草，与夫居尧之位，又何加焉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1273753_comment'></div>某不才，为贫而仕，每以治无善状，不敢妄求知己。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1273753_comment'></div>间者当路有过听者，与某音容之不接，声闻之不通，不以某之不肖，而为之剡章，且附置以达时俗之礼，通为启谢。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1273753_comment'></div>某不工偶俪，强为数语，而致其意焉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1273753_comment'></div>语前所谓道义之交修者，以周公之贤，惟恐失天下之士，而伊尹之任，何以为王者之师。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1273753_comment'></div>妄意士之所以自任者当然；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1273753_comment'></div>不然，亦不足以为士矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1273753_comment'></div>执事之于某，初非牖间半面之旧，又无研席论交之雅，邂逅一遇，贻我以书。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1273753_comment'></div>某读其文，望其容，窃自知其幸也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1273753_comment'></div>盛意于我良厚，故敢因前书之语，而请复之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1273753_comment'></div>执事谓位卑则道不存焉，又谓贵贱分殊而尊卑势异。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1273753_comment'></div>此言之发，似未之尽。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1273753_comment'></div>虽然，亦前相望甚殊之意，特未言道义之在亡而已。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1273753_comment'></div>在《诗》有必酬之谊，故某即之以相规。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1273753_comment'></div>横渠之诗不云乎「出异归同禹与颜，未分黄阁与青山」，明道亦云「统军百万，曲肱饮水在其中矣」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1273753_comment'></div>此古人道义所在之验，愿执事持之以自广，施之他日，无负于今。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1273753_comment'></div>若夫某之作，斐然之文，胥失道真，何足为执事道？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1273753_comment'></div>若仁与贤，则某岂敢？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1273753_comment'></div>惟执事财察是幸！</div><div id='poem_sentence_25_1273753_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1168&endYear=1168')">1168年</a>　在永嘉候阙。曾与张人杰论学。作品：复张人杰学谕书。<div id='poem_1273754' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1273754' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1273754?labeling=true' target='_blank'>复张人杰学谕书</a><span class='authorDate'>（1168年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 南宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(31376, "南宋", "薛季宣", "poem_title_1273754")'>薛季宣</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1273754_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1273754'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1273754'>某窃尝喜《易》，读之将数百过，而弗知其际也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1273754_comment'></div>夫以先天之卦，见之三画；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1273754_comment'></div>重《易》之象，系之六爻。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1273754_comment'></div>天地之大，昆虫之细，与夫圣人之道，先生之治，君子小人之事，工师卜祝之流，幽而鬼神，远而造化，凡有可推之数，可形之象，可行之事，靡不备在此书。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1273754_comment'></div>微若书不可言，亦求斯得之矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1273754_comment'></div>六经之义，于《易》备焉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1273754_comment'></div>以通为足以尽之，则太极之体未尝动；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1273754_comment'></div>以定为足以周之，则作《易》之道变为占。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1273754_comment'></div>是皆本诸吾身，参诸天地，拟诸变化，可由而不可测者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1273754_comment'></div>某安足以知之！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1273754_comment'></div>不知《易》而施诸民，犹宵行而瞽者也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1273754_comment'></div>思得通儒而与之论，未之能得。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1273754_comment'></div>执事不以某为不肖，惠然辱枉临之，诒我以书，纵言而及于《易》也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1273754_comment'></div>惟学有伦有要，执事其知之矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1273754_comment'></div>善乎《书》之论政体也，曰「当仁明而通变」，舍是则为姑息而苛察矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1273754_comment'></div>《易》曰「通其变，使民不倦」，此黄帝、尧、舜之治，某何德以堪之？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1273754_comment'></div>高山仰止，敢不钦服训诲。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1273754_comment'></div>虽然，窃有必酬之谊，故某谨布其腹心。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1273754_comment'></div>今夫煦煦之仁，察察之明，而后有姑息苛察之事，信能仁并天地，明等日月，则何二弊之能有！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1273754_comment'></div>某学也未造乎此，其能亿二仪二曜之仁明。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1273754_comment'></div>若夫《易》之变通，后世失之远矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1273754_comment'></div>执中无方，犹执一也，苟知变而不知止，则必若晋人之为通。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1273754_comment'></div>《大传》有之，无思也，无为也，寂然不动，感而遂通，天下之故。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1273754_comment'></div>变通之道，尽此赞矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1273754_comment'></div>某区东狂妄人耳，焉知《易》道！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1273754_comment'></div>因执事之有是言也，故敢及之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1273754_comment'></div>至于《易》之为书，圣人晚学以无过，以为仁明而通于《易》也，实非下走之所敢当。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1273754_comment'></div>书不尽言，财察是幸！</div><div id='poem_sentence_27_1273754_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1168&endYear=1168')">1168年</a>　在永嘉候阙。曾与龚秀才论学。作品：复龚秀才书。<div id='poem_1273755' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1273755' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1273755?labeling=true' target='_blank'>复龚秀才书</a><span class='authorDate'>（1168年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 南宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(31376, "南宋", "薛季宣", "poem_title_1273755")'>薛季宣</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1273755_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1273755'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1273755'>子路有言：君子之仕也，行其义也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1273755_comment'></div>行其义，则不俟乎其外者矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1273755_comment'></div>仕而道不行者，近世以为深患，非有他也，不能尽己之道，固无以尽物也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1273755_comment'></div>苟尽己以行道，则凡自外至者有常态，而吾所以应之者有常法，无俟乎其外，而天下之理无不得矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1273755_comment'></div>尽己之道，夫岂它术哉？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1273755_comment'></div>亦在乎熟之而不学墙面。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1273755_comment'></div>盖未之习也，时习焉，则吾固有之者，卓焉而立乎！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1273755_comment'></div>内焕焉而章乎外，纷纭万变，触睫过耳，而吾不为乱，则其于从政也何有？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1273755_comment'></div>此某朝夕之所愿学而未能得者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1273755_comment'></div>昏昏焉，而以施诸事，顾不悖哉！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1273755_comment'></div>伏惟秘省执事好学而知其要，将士而通其理，惠然我顾而无私曲之问，投以长笺而为治民之说，凡某素所愿闻而不可得者，稔闻而熟见之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1273755_comment'></div>如击蒙昧，如发丰蔀，其为赐也，岂兼金之况哉！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1273755_comment'></div>以观其学之所到，知不如斯而已，信能进乎此道，则于异时之政，将见其有及物之惠矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1273755_comment'></div>虽然，仕而学者恒有单闻之患，学而仕者其于人情必得，势使然也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1273755_comment'></div>某不幸而窭仕而未能有学，视执事者学而未仕，其于尽已之道，犹霄壤之为间也，尚惟不已斯道，充其所学，日新达德，而知我之为戒，待时而动，不亦伟乎！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1273755_comment'></div>某不敏，窃慕古人相成之谊，惟执事财察而加励焉，幸甚！</div><div id='poem_sentence_15_1273755_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1168&endYear=1168')">1168年</a>　在永嘉候阙。春，陈傅良谢徒束书，山间屏居。薛季宣又前去访谈，问治何业，傅良竭己所得以对，季宣曰：“吾惧吾子之累于得也。“<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1168&endYear=1168')">1168年2月</a>　在永嘉候阙。二月，王炎除签书枢密院事。薛季宣上书王炎。<br /></div><div class='label1' id='7fdfc613e9c34623b338e6e0c005627d_label'><a href='javascript: DetailSwitch("7fdfc613e9c34623b338e6e0c005627d");'><span id='7fdfc613e9c34623b338e6e0c005627d_link' class='switch'>—</span></a><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1173&endYear=1173')">1173年</a>，40岁</div><div id='7fdfc613e9c34623b338e6e0c005627d' class='detail'><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1173&endYear=1173')">1173年4月</a>　解湖州任，改除知常州，未上任，回到永嘉。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1173&endYear=1173')">1173年7月</a>　七月戊申，卒于家，年四十。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1173&endYear=1173')">1173年12月</a>　十二月壬申，葬于永嘉县吹台乡慈湖之原。<br /></div>
-----end



-----title
江陵（江陵府）
-----detail
<div class='label1' id='49ca4e18891c40f88414401d7fec2c39_label'><a href='javascript: DetailSwitch("49ca4e18891c40f88414401d7fec2c39");'><span id='49ca4e18891c40f88414401d7fec2c39_link' class='switch'>—</span></a><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1140&endYear=1140')">1140年</a>，7岁</div><div id='49ca4e18891c40f88414401d7fec2c39' class='detail'><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1140&endYear=1140')">1140年1月</a>　随伯父薛弼宦游。是年初，薛弼在荆南知府任上。<br /></div><div class='label1' id='b333e070d86a4303af31ec33881b76f4_label'><a href='javascript: DetailSwitch("b333e070d86a4303af31ec33881b76f4");'><span id='b333e070d86a4303af31ec33881b76f4_link' class='switch'>—</span></a><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1150&endYear=1152')">1150-1152年</a>，17-19岁</div><div id='b333e070d86a4303af31ec33881b76f4' class='detail'><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1150&endYear=1150')">1150年</a>　在江陵。与孙氏成婚，岳父荆南安抚使孙汝翼辟为书写机宜文字。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1150&endYear=1150')">1150年</a>　在江陵。从袁溉问学。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1151&endYear=1151')">1151年</a>　任荆南安抚使司书写机宜文字。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1152&endYear=1152')">1152年</a>　任荆南安抚使司书写机宜文字，有志改写《五代史记》，郑伯英知其名。<br /></div>

-----title
杭州
-----detail
<div class='label1' id='1efee2fb14364764b7c89fb0fc98829f_label'><a href='javascript: DetailSwitch("1efee2fb14364764b7c89fb0fc98829f");'><span id='1efee2fb14364764b7c89fb0fc98829f_link' class='switch'>—</span></a><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1140&endYear=1140')">1140年</a>，7岁</div><div id='1efee2fb14364764b7c89fb0fc98829f' class='detail'><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1140&endYear=1140')">1140年2月</a>　随伯父薛弼宦游。二月，薛弼充秘阁修撰、陕西转运使。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1140&endYear=1140')">1140年6月</a>　随伯父薛弼宦游。六月，薛弼为尚书左司郎中。<br /></div><div class='label1' id='9c16522dcce047e4a580f469c00b116a_label'><a href='javascript: DetailSwitch("9c16522dcce047e4a580f469c00b116a");'><span id='9c16522dcce047e4a580f469c00b116a_link' class='switch'>—</span></a><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1163&endYear=1164')">1163-1164年</a>，30-31岁</div><div id='9c16522dcce047e4a580f469c00b116a' class='detail'><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1163&endYear=1163')">1163年10月</a>　胡铨兼权中书舍人、同修国史。薛季宣上书胡铨，论及和战。作品：上胡舍人书。<div id='poem_1273699' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1273699' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1273699?labeling=true' target='_blank'>上胡舍人书</a><span class='authorDate'>（1163年10月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 南宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(31376, "南宋", "薛季宣", "poem_title_1273699")'>薛季宣</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1273699_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1273699'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1273699'>某闻之：盛名之下为难居，天下之望为难副。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1273699_comment'></div>盖士有名斯有德，有德斯有望，名望所在，至德存焉，无其德而有其名，是窃名者也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1273699_comment'></div>名者，天下之美器，造物者之所靳也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1273699_comment'></div>有其德而名从之，犹恐无以充天下之望，盗名孤望，安有不殆者乎？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1273699_comment'></div>执事穷圣学之源，奋百世之下，名德之重，非一日矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1273699_comment'></div>戊午之疏，欲取奸臣而枭之，女子童儿，至今传诵，廉顽立懦，可以风乎。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1273699_comment'></div>百世之后，所谓气充天地，名光日月，其所以得天下之望者岂徒然哉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1273699_comment'></div>皇上付执事以国书，班执事以法从，任寄之意，夫岂无自而然邪？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1273699_comment'></div>上下之情，其所望于执事者可谓至矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1273699_comment'></div>执事以身任天下之重，宜必有以处之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1273699_comment'></div>今天下倒悬矣，上策莫如自治，而自治之道，非小人之所及也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1273699_comment'></div>观乎边鄙则荡而无备，问其粮饷则匮而不给；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1273699_comment'></div>外有强梁不测之虏，日窥觎而弗制；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1273699_comment'></div>四郊多垒，必有当任其辱者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1273699_comment'></div>不思自治之道而论遂及于和，和固多端，然不自强则和不在我，则将靡事不为，而敌人得以制其命矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1273699_comment'></div>虏固贪顽无义之国，我之虚实，已尽知之，而又示弱以和；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1273699_comment'></div>且哀鸣而请命，未见颜色，固将先事而为之，无厌之求，必将纵于我矣，一辞其请，则和不可就；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1273699_comment'></div>举从其命，必将有所不给。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1273699_comment'></div>及有所不给，则彼辞直而动顺，吾圉不固，其将何以拒之？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1273699_comment'></div>然则今日之和，是为坐困之策，谋谟之际，尤不可以不审也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1273699_comment'></div>以愚不肖之见，求之人情，保国之计，和不若守。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1273699_comment'></div>守御备具则和议可成，和议可成，守之必固。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1273699_comment'></div>虽然，守御备矣，纪纲立矣，和战在我，又何敌之畏乎？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1273699_comment'></div>彼寡谋肉食之人，乌知国之深虑？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1273699_comment'></div>议和之始，未尝不为善后之说，所谋一遂，则将歌颂太平，文饰礼乐，居身周公之地，以天下为弗复事矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1273699_comment'></div>善后之说不亦虚乎？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1273699_comment'></div>视前日之所为，则其情状自见，如其详尽，则非累言之所能及也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1273699_comment'></div>伏自执事返国，天下之人谁不拭目以望，延颈以俟，皆曰执事守先王之道，其将正国而以福天下乎？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1273699_comment'></div>寥寥无闻，疑必有所待也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1273699_comment'></div>今国家之事势，断可知矣，以为中原不可复得，强虏不可复破，则先王之道遂为无用，而天下无可治之理。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1273699_comment'></div>此直自欺之论。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_30_1273699_comment'></div>如曰国耻必雪，国雠必报，此万世不易之论，而不可以遽成者，知上策之自治，则恢复之计在其中矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_31_1273699_comment'></div>释此而为和议，又将轻举而妄发；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_32_1273699_comment'></div>和之不就，尚可侥倖而存；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_33_1273699_comment'></div>或至于成，则国命从此倾矣，安危之计，无此为急。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_34_1273699_comment'></div>天下循名而求实，执事固人望之所由归也，直前论辨，必有非外廷所得闻者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_35_1273699_comment'></div>一言决安危之机，用副人望之所属，以全名而保德，则此举其时矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_36_1273699_comment'></div>昔贾谊、刘蕡以治安之策陈于汉、唐之朝，志不克伸，至今遗恨于天下。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_37_1273699_comment'></div>执事戊午之疏，固已书之大典，著之人寰，刘、贾之言，执事盖全而有矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_38_1273699_comment'></div>今日之事，志复可伸，如倡言以为天下先，则天下犹有可为之理；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_39_1273699_comment'></div>置而弗论，或始论而中辍，则天下之望，万世之名，亦有时而替矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_40_1273699_comment'></div>贾、刘之论，从可谓之空言？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_41_1273699_comment'></div>惟执事审图之尔。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_42_1273699_comment'></div>某狂生小子，不知国论之所定，痛念先人不容于和亲之际，抱志以殁，见父之执，则思父道之所在；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_43_1273699_comment'></div>以父之道求父之执，不敢不以全名保德副生民之所望。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_44_1273699_comment'></div>属于执事者之说，陈于执事之前，贽见之诚，先人之志，盖于此焉见矣，惟执事先生财察，幸甚幸甚！</div><div id='poem_sentence_45_1273699_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1163&endYear=1163')">1163年</a>　是年，薛季宣从吏部铨，得婺州司理参军，待次。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1164&endYear=1164')">1164年1月</a>　在杭州。<br /></div><div class='label1' id='8bea37f69190467a849f907c8bcdfcb6_label'><a href='javascript: DetailSwitch("8bea37f69190467a849f907c8bcdfcb6");'><span id='8bea37f69190467a849f907c8bcdfcb6_link' class='switch'>—</span></a><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1168&endYear=1168')">1168年</a>，35岁</div><div id='8bea37f69190467a849f907c8bcdfcb6' class='detail'><span style='margin: 0 0.5em; color: gray;'>▪</span>是年入都，在郑伯熊（景望）之舍得陈亮之文。<br /><span style='margin: 0 0.5em; color: gray;'>▪</span>在临安。上《召对劄子》三则，首论审政本，遴三公之选，进人才，张纪纲；二论冗官冗兵，害政伤财；三论民间疾苦，省虚税，宽民力。作品：召对劄子三则。<br /><span style='margin: 0 0.5em; color: gray;'>▪</span>在临安。召对后改宣义郎，知平江府常熟县。离开临安前，致书王炎告别。作品：与王枢密公明。<br /><span style='margin: 0 0.5em; color: gray;'>▪</span>在临安。召对后改宣义郎，知平江府常熟县。离开临安前，致书刘珙告别。作品：与刘枢密。<div id='poem_1273687' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1273687' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1273687?labeling=true' target='_blank'>与刘枢密书</a><span class='authorDate'>（1168年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 南宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(31376, "南宋", "薛季宣", "poem_title_1273687")'>薛季宣</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1273687_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1273687'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1273687'>某伏蒙钧谕，奏劄副本谨缮写封纳。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1273687_comment'></div>首劄上劘君德，在庙堂无可施行，既不付外，敢乞毋示于人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1273687_comment'></div>某被召而来，蒙朝廷汲引之意良厚，所愧学术浅陋，不能有所感悟，负于鉴裁，惭仄多矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1273687_comment'></div>如某世味澹泊，素无改官之望，冒荣京秩，寔出造化，然而涓埃亡补，谊不当受。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1273687_comment'></div>犹赖第三劄子降出，辞之恐非人情，宁受伤廉之讥，不敢不拜，敢望钧慈鉴念，力为主张行之，勿使尧、舜之民，尚供无业之赋，为施甚大。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1273687_comment'></div>某叨窃不为无名<span class='inlineComment2'>（云云）</span>。</div><div id='poem_sentence_5_1273687_comment'></div></div></div><br /></div><div class='label1' id='e9a6058698b541ecae116e3eab51269f_label'><a href='javascript: DetailSwitch("e9a6058698b541ecae116e3eab51269f");'><span id='e9a6058698b541ecae116e3eab51269f_link' class='switch'>—</span></a><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1171&endYear=1171')">1171年</a>，38岁</div><div id='e9a6058698b541ecae116e3eab51269f' class='detail'><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1171&endYear=1171')">1171年8月</a>　到达临安，上劄子给虞允文，论及君臣关系，反对贪功喜事，轻启边衅。作品：都堂审察劄子。与虞丞相劄子。<div id='poem_1273636' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1273636' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1273636?labeling=true' target='_blank'>都堂审察劄子</a><span class='authorDate'>（1171年8月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 南宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(31376, "南宋", "薛季宣", "poem_title_1273636")'>薛季宣</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1273636_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1273636'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1273636'>某读《史记》，至赵烈侯欲赐歌者田，相国公仲连不与，曰：「求之未有善者」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1273636_comment'></div>番吾君曰：「君实好善，而未有所持。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1273636_comment'></div>今公仲相赵四年矣，亦尝进士乎」？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1273636_comment'></div>曰：「未也」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1273636_comment'></div>番吾君曰：「牛蓄、荀欣、徐越皆可」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1273636_comment'></div>公仲乃进此三人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1273636_comment'></div>牛蓄侍烈侯以仁义，约以王道，烈侯逌然。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1273636_comment'></div>明日，荀欣侍以选练举贤，任官使能。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1273636_comment'></div>明日，徐越侍以节财俭用，察度功德，所与无不充。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1273636_comment'></div>君悦，使使谓相国曰：「歌者之田且止，赐相国衣二袭」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1273636_comment'></div>仆未尝不抚卷而叹，谓公仲连贤相也，不以正义咈君之心；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1273636_comment'></div>番吾君善谋也，乃以贤贤易君之虑。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1273636_comment'></div>公仲用人如己，烈侯改过不吝，贤哉！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1273636_comment'></div>是故大臣格君心之非，惟务引之当道，是虽战国之事，盖三代大臣遗法也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1273636_comment'></div>昔者伊尹、周公所以弥缝君臣之间，盖不于其身而于其左右之臣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1273636_comment'></div>当其未甚相知之时，脱有一人不正，则二公之事去矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1273636_comment'></div>圣人之所以大过人者如此。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1273636_comment'></div>后世大臣喜与人主争事，人主顾以要窃名誉疑之，君臣之间，盖判然离矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1273636_comment'></div>进则孤立而无助，退则洁己以致讥，而欲道行事济，万无是理。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1273636_comment'></div>古人之不可仿佛，非天也，人也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1273636_comment'></div>主上以天纵之圣，笃任同德，凡天下事与相公唯诺可否，无所疑贰，是诚足以有为之时。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1273636_comment'></div>然而间或事与意违，而功成未有端绪者，将由进贤未广，犹无以易君之虑，引义以争，未免身亲之乎？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1273636_comment'></div>虽有至心，谁能谅之？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1273636_comment'></div>伏惟谋谟庙堂，深思远览致君之道，愿专以伊尹、周公之心为心，若公仲连之所为有可备采择者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1273636_comment'></div>某位卑言高，死罪。</div><div id='poem_sentence_24_1273636_comment'></div></div></div><div id='poem_1273637' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1273637' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1273637?labeling=true' target='_blank'>与虞丞相劄子</a><span class='authorDate'>（1171年8月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 南宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(31376, "南宋", "薛季宣", "poem_title_1273637")'>薛季宣</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1273637_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1273637'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1273637'>某小官，不敢辄踰分理，亟请呼召。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1273637_comment'></div>仰蒙希世知遇，有拳拳欲报而不能自已者，其可以遂无言乎！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1273637_comment'></div>兹者伏承丞相以礼为国，主上三加弥尊，虽高祖患失酂侯，柳下惠不以三公易其介，未足多之，天下寔幸！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1273637_comment'></div>抑尝闻之师曰：君土相火，一心也；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1273637_comment'></div>元首股肱，一体也；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1273637_comment'></div>中有毫釐之间，非心体之道也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1273637_comment'></div>共惟君相叶德，宁有毫釐间于其中，然而归柄辞权，似亦不可常也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1273637_comment'></div>今丞相已不得谢，宜益尊所闻，行所知，为人所不能为，以镇服天下，巩固基本。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1273637_comment'></div>格心之道，仆尝陈其略矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1273637_comment'></div>若夫事与意违，而功成未有端绪，请得而毕言之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1273637_comment'></div>大抵喜欲速之功者，昧于宏远之规模，临重事而轻为之，鲜不中道而废，察于二者，则天下无不可为之事，无不可成之功。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1273637_comment'></div>士君子存有为之心，居可为之地，处当为之事，动不先虑，急于有成，往往命出而反汗，政举而事乖，虽其胸次瞭然，中亦未能无沮，而欲一人之信，四国之顺，功业之有成就，万无是理。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1273637_comment'></div>是故规模宏远，功之所以速成也；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1273637_comment'></div>不轻举动，事之所以必济也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1273637_comment'></div>古人所行，皆有节度。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1273637_comment'></div>幕府专治文书，况于一日二日万几而可以轻为之邪？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1273637_comment'></div>天下之事，当与天下之士议之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1273637_comment'></div>碌碌鄙夫，心存得失，而以贪功喜事、自献其身者，要何足以知此。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1273637_comment'></div>丞相愿继自今务恢古人之度，充体国之诚，深察蔽邪以谨奸慝，博求英乂以广聪明，宁受百罔而不替好士之心，勿以一眚而弃人才之用，必得四友之佐，赞帷幄之议者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1273637_comment'></div>临事加之以惧，好谋期于必成，每每敬之于先，俾毋吝之于后，将使人主见可成之效，四方睹难拔之基，图事乡功，安有溃于成者！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1273637_comment'></div>不然，日又一日，谁适与谋？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1273637_comment'></div>作事付之渺茫，近功希于幸会，而有成效，非所闻也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1273637_comment'></div>某思所以补报，不知语之深切，伏惟审听而熟图之，不胜社稷斯人之幸！</div><div id='poem_sentence_22_1273637_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1171&endYear=1171')">1171年8月11日</a>　赴大理寺任主簿。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1171&endYear=1171')">1171年</a>　因看不惯大理寺因循拖沓的办事作风，上书大理寺长贰，要求“奉身而退”作品：上大理寺长贰劄子。<div id='poem_1273629' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1273629' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1273629?labeling=true' target='_blank'>上大理寺长贰劄子</a><span class='authorDate'>（1171年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 南宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(31376, "南宋", "薛季宣", "poem_title_1273629")'>薛季宣</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1273629_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1273629'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1273629'>某兹者叨冒误恩，备数簿领，自十一日赴寺，供职本厅，即无人吏，虽供职文状，亦是自行修写。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1273629_comment'></div>当时惟有胥长二三辈至直舍参谒，并不睹群吏之面。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1273629_comment'></div>本寺之籍，深所未晓，遂求教于判寺莫少卿，伏蒙谕以「本寺之制，左断刑，右治狱，自少卿、丞正、评事而下，皆有分职，独主簿不然，凡文书之期会，簿籍之句考，在两司者悉当兼掌。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1273629_comment'></div>此职不修久矣，可呼问知杂吏」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1273629_comment'></div>某亦询知本厅旧例，差破人吏一名，意者知杂一司，职当关领。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1273629_comment'></div>寻呼知杂司者，问以职，则曰无事；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1273629_comment'></div>问以吏，则曰阙人；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1273629_comment'></div>且言寺簿不治文书，但请十日一至直舍，签押簿历。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1273629_comment'></div>某欲一见簿历，则又泛然不应，竟无一事，不免逡循出局。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1273629_comment'></div>某来自远外，诚不识朝廷事体。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1273629_comment'></div>窃详国朝官制，以长贰综领大纲，不可自治凡目，故设主簿专职句校。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1273629_comment'></div>内之寺监，外之县邑，小大虽异，所掌宜同。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1273629_comment'></div>则凡应干行遣期程及簿书销注之属，其事无不当预，稽违漏落，责有所归。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1273629_comment'></div>簿历有当十日一签，亦有日当考视者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1273629_comment'></div>主簿之职，况不祗此。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1273629_comment'></div>今也不得知其条目，虽废签书可也，张官置吏，恐不为是。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1273629_comment'></div>虚设胥辈，惟恐主簿之得举其职也，故多方壅蔽。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1273629_comment'></div>不示之籍，将使不得辄有所问；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1273629_comment'></div>不与之吏，将使不得辄有所为。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1273629_comment'></div>旨意甚深，察此可见。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1273629_comment'></div>某无状，仕寔为贫，庙堂过听，处以在京职事，期待之意，宁古乘田委吏之比！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1273629_comment'></div>有如本职，不得效其区区，愧于前人多矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1273629_comment'></div>仰惟主上励精为治，尽心庶狱，刑寺之职，所系至重，他官禄仕可也，此岂苟禄地邪？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1273629_comment'></div>综覈之朝，责以名实之效，失职至是，将何辞以对乎？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1273629_comment'></div>长贰勉以职事之修，交游望以职分之内，某所为不能称事，有奉身而退耳。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1273629_comment'></div>伏惟台慈鉴念详思，所以处当其宜。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1273629_comment'></div>某责重位卑，不敢不告，伏乞台察！</div><div id='poem_sentence_26_1273629_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1171&endYear=1171')">1171年</a>　上书枢密使王炎。作品：与王枢使公明。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1171&endYear=1171')">1171年</a>　秋，与周必大、吕祖谦交。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1171&endYear=1171')">1171年</a>　冬，奉使淮西。<br /></div><div class='label1' id='1035b80f46af4c63bde1cbcc2ad79877_label'><a href='javascript: DetailSwitch("1035b80f46af4c63bde1cbcc2ad79877");'><span id='1035b80f46af4c63bde1cbcc2ad79877_link' class='switch'>—</span></a><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1172&endYear=1172')">1172年</a>，39岁</div><div id='1035b80f46af4c63bde1cbcc2ad79877' class='detail'><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1172&endYear=1172')">1172年7月</a>　回到临安复命，进官二等，除大理正（任大理正仅七日）<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1172&endYear=1172')">1172年7月</a>　上奏宋孝宗，首论租税不均，土户包占田地，淮地未得垦辟；次论边田荒芜，劝垦文具，边备不修；三论左右之人欺诳不实，托正以行邪，伪直以售佞，提出“收骨鲠之士，弃软熟之人”的主张。作品：奉使淮西回上殿劄子一、二、三。<div id='poem_1273610' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1273610' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1273610?labeling=true' target='_blank'>奉使淮西回上殿劄子<span style='margin: 0 0.5em'> 其一 </span></a><span class='authorDate'>（1172年7月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 南宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(31376, "南宋", "薛季宣", "poem_title_1273610")'>薛季宣</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1273610_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1273610'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1273610'>臣恭奉圣训，前去淮西措置赈赡安集，覈实诸州垦田二麦等事。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1273610_comment'></div>臣将命亡状，不能仰称使令，初至淮西，岁已云暮，委付虽重，所成至微。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1273610_comment'></div>其庐、黄州所置官庄，并覈到垦田增种麦数，已别具图册，节次进呈外，方惧不逃辱命之责，圣度包荒，恩宠沓至，奖借幺么，以为事功之劝，俯伏战汗，未知展竭之地。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1273610_comment'></div>窃缘置庄、覈实二件事体实相关。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1273610_comment'></div>盖自兵火以还，州县多仍承平垦田旧数，间用貌约顷亩，著为定籍。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1273610_comment'></div>已而人户请佃，类皆包括湖山为界，有一户之产，终日履行不遍，而其输纳不过斗斛。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1273610_comment'></div>以臣循问所历，大抵皆然。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1273610_comment'></div>今者齐安之立官庄，寿春所以分给归正，不免检括冒占，取其荒田。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1273610_comment'></div>初索干照视之，有名田一亩，而占地五七顷者，自耕则无力，刬请则必争。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1273610_comment'></div>诸处之民转徙淮甸者，纵有佃田之请，州县村堡往往惮事，且为土人囊橐，多方沮之，陈诉穷年，了不可得，弊源未涤，乃欲覈知实数，自欺可也，诚不可以告陛下。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1273610_comment'></div>故臣覈垦田，祗是括责税籍，拖照自陈之数，臣不复尽论。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1273610_comment'></div>诸州只如蕲州罗田一县，邑于灊霍诸山之奥，实与五郡十县封境犬牙。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1273610_comment'></div>初申一县垦田若干顷，至覆田，已耕不过一百五十三顷，未耕三十六顷一十五亩。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1273610_comment'></div>又如黄州黄陂一县，初申垦田三千七百一十九顷二亩，覆行诘问，则云垦田一百六十顷四十九亩。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1273610_comment'></div>二邑此其最甚者，其馀大略可知。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1273610_comment'></div>臣尝怪国家经理两淮，朝夕忧念，历岁十馀，迄未有成，及此亲行，乃见其患。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1273610_comment'></div>且夫姑息之爱，惠及倖民。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1273610_comment'></div>包占既多，垦辟实少，非惟官司坐失租入，天产之物皆为此废。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1273610_comment'></div>虽欲聚人保境，其道无繇。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1273610_comment'></div>官庄之立，乃以一时赈赡之故，不无劳费，甚非常行之策。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1273610_comment'></div>臣之所睹，江南转徙人户来淮甸者，东极温、台，南尽福建，西达赣、吉，往往有之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1273610_comment'></div>土人包占既多，无田可以耕佃，以故失所者众，来者甚艰。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1273610_comment'></div>设若此患不除，则虽三数十年，淮南未见充实。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1273610_comment'></div>朝廷常展刬请之限，兹臣所未解也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1273610_comment'></div>有如立法劝耕而开刬请之制，蠲耕牛之税，徕四远之民，来者知佃之必得，居者知包占之无利，驱诱并行，主客皆争垦辟，数年之内，淮南可使地无旷土，足兵足食，以守以战，将无往而不济矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1273610_comment'></div>臣愿陛下深念远览，与宰辅大臣熟议而断行之，不胜宗社大幸！</div><div id='poem_sentence_25_1273610_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1172&endYear=1172')">1172年</a>　赴湖州任知府。行前上劄子一论科折不均、丁绢催扰之弊，二论备边之策，三论下情上达、人主兼听广纳。作品：朝辞劄子一、二、三。<div id='poem_1273613' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1273613' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1273613?labeling=true' target='_blank'>知湖州朝辞劄子<span style='margin: 0 0.5em'> 其一 </span></a><span class='authorDate'>（1172年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 南宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(31376, "南宋", "薛季宣", "poem_title_1273613")'>薛季宣</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1273613_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1273613'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1273613'>臣少长田里，常睹乡民患苦催科之政，九重千里，无路上通。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1273613_comment'></div>兹蒙超擢辅藩，未知称报。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1273613_comment'></div>伏睹陛下无轻民事，寅夕究怀，知而不言，臣则有罪。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1273613_comment'></div>催科之弊，未易单举，敢以其害甚且博者，仰为陛下言之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1273613_comment'></div>凡二事：一曰科折不均，二曰丁绢催扰。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1273613_comment'></div>县官租入有常，科折在所不免。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1273613_comment'></div>使有均一简易之法，民知适从，人吏不得为奸，夫复何患？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1273613_comment'></div>比年州县科折，一切付之乡胥，令长利于速办，而有赢馀，听其抛折虚数，轻重在手，不立堤防，给散人户凭由，不言科折之数，由是出等，上户多缘计弊而免其数，并于贫下，实出强倍之征。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1273613_comment'></div>其尤甚者，正赋既入于官，官司不为销落，抑令重纳科折，而以箠楚临之，逼以威刑，何所申诉！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1273613_comment'></div>及额之后，官亦无所稽考，虚数之入，吏窃有之，民困不均。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1273613_comment'></div>此其大者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1273613_comment'></div>丁绢之赋，古口算之法也，凡有丁则有赋，为绢不过数尺，催科有法，民亦何患？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1273613_comment'></div>然而丈尺既少，不免并合。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1273613_comment'></div>输官掌钞，不过一人，又多揽纳之户，乡司不为销落，未免时复追催。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1273613_comment'></div>掌钞或不在家，或为揽者盗用，无钞呈验，小民惮于出官，绢既不多，不免计会重纳。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1273613_comment'></div>一岁如此，或至再三。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1273613_comment'></div>或到官者，令长多不之恤，禁系瘐死有矣，而其诛求科罚之费，甚于倍蓰之征，岁岁相仍，无有宁日。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1273613_comment'></div>人规避免丁籍，壮岁或不裹头。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1273613_comment'></div>困苦细民，此尤甚且博者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1273613_comment'></div>二事革之有法，可使民安田里，而无追须横纳之赋，不然，比屋受弊，利在猾胥而已。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1273613_comment'></div>愿戒天下县邑，凡承受抛降、科折租赋，并须先期以正数细计分数科折，明出榜示今年某科管催若干数，内科折若干，除下户若干、所管若干不该科折外，今将第几等户已上如何分数科折，明于逐户由子开说某乡合纳某税，仰于数内科纳几分几釐。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1273613_comment'></div>简而易知，奸弊必少。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1273613_comment'></div>丁绢入纳，须令每疋为钞，开具人户单名，各纳若干丈尺，钞外添置飞子一纸，据户数界作几行，明开某年月日某县乡村某人投纳某年丁绢若干丈尺，系钞头某人名下，官以飞子当县户二钞，缝上横使条印，而移团印于上，纳罢随钞给之，责令钞头于三日内剪开，飞子给还人户。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1273613_comment'></div>户钞只今钞头收掌，其飞子并令官司照用。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1273613_comment'></div>如户钞法自非去失飞子，并飞子书印不明与县钞印文不合者，不得追索户钞钞头参验。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1273613_comment'></div>有如官用条印或不圆备，许人户于纳钞之际即时执覆添补，庶几人人有可以执守，可省追催重叠之患。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1273613_comment'></div>臣谓其他应干税赋凡系并合输纳者，二户以上皆可依此添置飞子，施行州县，敢不遵承，科以违制坐之，则凡催科之政，其害甚且博者，可以一日而去矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1273613_comment'></div>一颦呻而利泽天下，于是有足言者，伏惟陛下留神采纳。</div><div id='poem_sentence_27_1273613_comment'></div></div></div><br /></div>
-----end



-----title

-----title
绍兴
-----detail
<div class='label1' id='14685045875a484e94746f1c189f7730_label'><a href='javascript: DetailSwitch("14685045875a484e94746f1c189f7730");'><span id='14685045875a484e94746f1c189f7730_link' class='switch'>—</span></a><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1155&endYear=1155')">1155年</a>，22岁</div><div id='14685045875a484e94746f1c189f7730' class='detail'><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1155&endYear=1155')">1155年</a>　东游会稽，谒禹陵，经过马臻祠下，询问鉴湖所在，则已堙塞为民田，因作诗纪之。作品：乙亥岁东游会稽谒禹陵过马臻祠下询所谓鉴湖者则已堙塞为民田因赋。<div id='poem_548181' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_548181' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/548181?labeling=true' target='_blank'>乙亥岁东游会稽谒禹陵过马臻祠下询所谓鉴湖者则已堙塞为民田因赋</a><span class='authorDate'>（1155年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 南宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(31376, "南宋", "薛季宣", "poem_title_548181")'>薛季宣</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_548181_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_548181'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_548181'>登会稽，瞰长湖，漪涟万顷皆平芜。<div id='poem_sentence_0_548181_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_548181'>桑田变改唯闻说，岂信古今人事殊。<div id='poem_sentence_1_548181_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_548181'>往时夏后禹，道川治水劳驰驱。<div id='poem_sentence_2_548181_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_548181'>四支疲弊跛其足，过门弗视儿呱呱。<div id='poem_sentence_3_548181_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_548181'>众流宗海出平陆，滋人巨浸因卑洿。<div id='poem_sentence_4_548181_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_5_548181'>百神效职来大计，勤民远狩崩于嵞。<div id='poem_sentence_5_548181_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_6_548181'>名山立郡此焉始，明明功与日月俱。<div id='poem_sentence_6_548181_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_7_548181'>马侯有汉二千石，施仁复古苏燋枯。<div id='poem_sentence_7_548181_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_8_548181'>浚深倍薄拂古镜，还使硗埆成膏腴。<div id='poem_sentence_8_548181_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_9_548181'>阴邪丑正富权戚，居肓如鬼捐其躯。<div id='poem_sentence_9_548181_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_10_548181'>大君良吏不复见，茫茫陈迹日就无。<div id='poem_sentence_10_548181_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_11_548181'>玻璃湛湛长芳草，蛟龙窟宅生菰蒲。<div id='poem_sentence_11_548181_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_12_548181'>前功不录倚隳弃，谁何聚敛浮穿窬。<div id='poem_sentence_12_548181_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_13_548181'>庸情非圣决陂泽，迁移膏润为官租。<div id='poem_sentence_13_548181_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_14_548181'>昔人旧事已无在，犹有水则<span class='inlineComment2'>（四库本作识）</span>■<span class='inlineComment2'>（石毚）</span>长途。<div id='poem_sentence_14_548181_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_15_548181'>高田燥仰下沮洳，雨晹无岁均沾濡。<div id='poem_sentence_15_548181_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_16_548181'>咄哉荣利归乃室，是邦黔首其何辜。<div id='poem_sentence_16_548181_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_17_548181'>反令二主神，淫祀烦此都。<div id='poem_sentence_17_548181_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_18_548181'>王陵委积蠹明币，守祠浇酹倾清酤。<div id='poem_sentence_18_548181_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_19_548181'>禳祷两无已，跳梁饱妖巫。<div id='poem_sentence_19_548181_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_20_548181'>享祭缘报诚，嘉猷委泥涂。<div id='poem_sentence_20_548181_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_21_548181'>神灵血食已非分，无为耗黩令人吁。<div id='poem_sentence_21_548181_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_22_548181'>复绩怅何从，我心徒自㥚。</div><div id='poem_sentence_22_548181_comment'></div></div></div><br /></div>
-----end



-----title
常州
-----detail
<div class='label1' id='e2a2f63a2a6b41a183a8a407e50ecb4e_label'><a href='javascript: DetailSwitch("e2a2f63a2a6b41a183a8a407e50ecb4e");'><span id='e2a2f63a2a6b41a183a8a407e50ecb4e_link' class='switch'>—</span></a><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1156&endYear=1158')">1156-1158年</a>，23-25岁</div><div id='e2a2f63a2a6b41a183a8a407e50ecb4e' class='detail'><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1156&endYear=1156')">1156年</a>　孙汝翼以丁忧解荆州任（绍兴二十四年汝翼复知荆南），回到毗陵。季宣自永嘉往毗陵（常州）去看望岳父母。不久，孙汝翼去世。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1156&endYear=1156')">1156年</a>　在毗陵（常州）。作《克斋前记》<div id='poem_1273838' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1273838' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1273838?labeling=true' target='_blank'>克斋前记</a><span class='authorDate'>（1156年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 南宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(31376, "南宋", "薛季宣", "poem_title_1273838")'>薛季宣</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1273838_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1273838'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1273838'>克斋之故名曰「损斋」，损斋，损私之斋也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1273838_comment'></div>仲尼称「克己复礼为仁」，老氏谓「为道日损」，人虽不同，言理不异。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1273838_comment'></div>今夫人之生也，涵虚而无体曰命，通一而无方曰性。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1273838_comment'></div>命不易也，性不远也，物其故有也，道亦其故有也，耳目为闻见夺，心志为利欲移，然后私意萌，公义隐，迷惑失道，贯习为常，其故有尽亡，于是为小人伍；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1273838_comment'></div>往而不返，则将与飞走俱，日远于人，遂不可求诸人域。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1273838_comment'></div>收心正性，故圣人贵焉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1273838_comment'></div>今人病之切身，孰不务亟其去？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1273838_comment'></div>习非害性之为人患，不切于病乎？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1273838_comment'></div>人知病而不知非，圣人于是乎不作。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1273838_comment'></div>仲尼、展蹠其元顾不同邪？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1273838_comment'></div>仲尼明一以贯之道，师表乎万世；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1273838_comment'></div>蹠也违之不悟，天下号名大愚。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1273838_comment'></div>犹之水然，清明自其本性，埃尘浑之以浊。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1273838_comment'></div>本性固存，定而澄之，则为清明也，于其元奚辨？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1273838_comment'></div>人能去恶以复性，又何让于圣人哉！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1273838_comment'></div>皆知弗为者非他，私夺之也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1273838_comment'></div>走生二十有三年矣，日闻道于圣人之书，然临事辄失其情，益知胜私之不可不务，是以考之大《易》，取「损卦」以名书堂曰「损斋」，以为居处，期将斋心窒欲，反本归仁，日革非心，庶乎尽于此生也，损益盛衰之始，敢即之铭之！</div><div id='poem_sentence_16_1273838_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1157&endYear=1157')">1157年</a>　在毗陵（常州）。作《俨若思斋记》<div id='poem_1273839' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1273839' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1273839?labeling=true' target='_blank'>俨若思斋记</a><span class='authorDate'>（1157年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 南宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(31376, "南宋", "薛季宣", "poem_title_1273839")'>薛季宣</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1273839_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1273839'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1273839'>混焉曰太极，形而为两仪，天地位焉，万物育焉，布烈森罗，罔知攸究！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1273839_comment'></div>乡之所谓太极者，宜若亡而故存，故耐化物无迹，触感惟应，孰知其所以然！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1273839_comment'></div>非至静曷能与于此？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1273839_comment'></div>夫人之为物，万物之灵也，头足具天地之象，知识出事物之表，谁使之然？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1273839_comment'></div>有道主于内也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1273839_comment'></div>昧者不固其本，疲精神而它求，滋滋焉，汲汲焉，惟恐或遗，而遗之日多，患于忤物而于物益忤。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1273839_comment'></div>此亡它，不知所以用之，不能尽己以尽物也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1273839_comment'></div>圣人传心之要，岂有它哉，亦惟吾之故有，是归是体而已。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1273839_comment'></div>吾友行父子车子，所谓养其大者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1273839_comment'></div>之人也，以为道不远物，万物岂异于人，必欲周知其情，没齿将恐不既，莫若反求诸己，即圣人「毋不敬」之语行之，自诚而明，将以尽其性，合德于太极。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1273839_comment'></div>安居坏室，寂寂穷年，外则渊如块如，不言不笑，虽《记》云如斋如尸，殆无以异。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1273839_comment'></div>非惟此也，亦能以处众于喧鬨之中，虽挠之万端，卒莫以动其静。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1273839_comment'></div>比其言也，复无远于物情，使遇主而见之施为，将见其有不言而化者矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1273839_comment'></div>尝以其事告曰：「礼始『毋不敬，俨若思，安定辞』，而后『安民哉』，盖本于正心也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1273839_comment'></div>心正乃静，静而定，则浩然之气为吾体，体此则心乌乎动？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1273839_comment'></div>道乌乎加？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1273839_comment'></div>死且不移，况于小屑利害！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1273839_comment'></div>以之穷理，理不吾畔，以之推物，物将焉潜！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1273839_comment'></div>故古人务在至诚，治人其馀事耳。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1273839_comment'></div>我欲事斯语勿失，用名书堂，曰『俨若思斋』，子幸为我志之」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1273839_comment'></div>走于行父为知己，不可以辞，即叙其语而为之记。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1273839_comment'></div>夫斋之为言齐也，谓齐其心志也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1273839_comment'></div>心志一而无适，则太极不远物，动静无或遗，故曰「清明在躬，气志如神」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1273839_comment'></div>无为而为莫能臻，无思而思亦莫造，虽一身至鲜，大而天地不我过，与夫驰神于外，物役其志者，可同年语哉！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1273839_comment'></div>然其状则几是，曰俨若思斋，顾不甚得，如久于其道，则其来者将何如邪？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1273839_comment'></div></div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_25_1273839'>乃躬在是，乃心在彼。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1273839_comment'></div>逐物忘身，乌知天地！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1273839_comment'></div>心君中立，寂如太虚。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1273839_comment'></div>形神不违，齐庄如愚。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1273839_comment'></div>或之其它，或诚于敬。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1273839_comment'></div>望之不分，道有奇正。</div><div id='poem_sentence_30_1273839_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1158&endYear=1158')">1158年2月</a>　在毗陵（常州）。二月戊午，作《书庄绰揲蓍新谱》<div id='poem_1273788' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1273788' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1273788?labeling=true' target='_blank'>书庄绰揲蓍新谱</a><span class='authorDate'>（1158年2月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 南宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(31376, "南宋", "薛季宣", "poem_title_1273788")'>薛季宣</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1273788_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1273788'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1273788'>圣人之道行于古，圣人之法具于经，学者不务穷经，泥夫师说，故圣经法则晦以不明。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1273788_comment'></div>士当以经为据依，断然不惑于习，略去众多之论，以尽其心，夫然后圣典森然，无不得也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1273788_comment'></div>《易》，六经之原委也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1273788_comment'></div>作《易》之道，哉始揲蓍，其法详著《系辞》，可按以考也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1273788_comment'></div>自脱于秦火，师法纷纶，而经闇不通，举世罔知攸定。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1273788_comment'></div>士视先儒为用，久且不疑，旅出一途，而蓍法隐矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1273788_comment'></div>《揲蓍新谱》毅然《易大传》之从，始谓一、三为奇，二、四为偶，得奇偶之正，无偏颇之失，契于经旨，有足多者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1273788_comment'></div>其引徵以张辕揲蓍之法，可以为审矣，而师春氏说，又略与符同。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1273788_comment'></div>其法用蓍四十九茎，总箸把之，以意中分，扐一小指间，四揲之第一指揲，馀一、二足满五，馀三、四足满九，第二、第三指揲，馀一、二足满四，馀三、四足满八，四、五为少，八、九为多，三多老阴分爻，交三少老阳重分，两少一多少阴拆分，两多一少少阳单分，是法最为近古，然而馀二足五，馀三足九，与张氏说皆不与《易》通。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1273788_comment'></div>走尝闻巫山隐者袁道洁先生言，特暗与庄氏会，第以四、八为多为未尽。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1273788_comment'></div>走甚疑而参考之，惟策数几庄氏，何则？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1273788_comment'></div>《乾》之策三十有六，《坤》之策二十有四，庄氏策恒亏二，袁氏则二差而为《乾》矣，以知庄氏之说容有未当，何哉？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1273788_comment'></div>《系辞》之云，盖十八变而成卦，夫爻一、三少变六爻而数通矣，不必皆大变也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1273788_comment'></div>先儒自陈图南、邵尧夫辈，爻之再变已用四十有八，庄氏则尽用四十九，故从先儒则合于策，而四十九之用失矣，从庄氏则合于用，而二篇之策赢矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1273788_comment'></div>惟刘禹锡辩《易》九六，论揲以三指，其法与师春同，既用无四十八之讹，而策复与二篇叶，是则庄氏之奇偶，师春之变卦，既可信，皆可从。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1273788_comment'></div>作《易》之道，其不外是夫！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1273788_comment'></div>学者当自求之，是不必信。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1273788_comment'></div>盖一人之见，非敢谓诚然，如意无疑，则或可信，若犹未也，愿得复正从经，庶偏见之言，无以惑经于永。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1273788_comment'></div>绍兴著雍摄提格之岁如月戊午，读庄季绰《揲蓍新谱》，爱其善而失之变，故书<span class='inlineComment2'>（《浪语集》卷二七。）</span>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1273788_comment'></div></div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_19_1273788'>二差而为乾：四库本作「奇差而为耦」。</div><div id='poem_sentence_19_1273788_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1158&endYear=1158')">1158年3月10日</a>　在毗陵（常州）。葬岳父孙汝翼于尹原。<br /></div><div class='label1' id='6408b954493a446da1195a56f4e72be9_label'><a href='javascript: DetailSwitch("6408b954493a446da1195a56f4e72be9");'><span id='6408b954493a446da1195a56f4e72be9_link' class='switch'>—</span></a><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1158&endYear=1158')">1158年</a>，25岁</div><div id='6408b954493a446da1195a56f4e72be9' class='detail'><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1158&endYear=1158')">1158年</a>　抵永嘉翌日，岳母去世。季宣因贫瘁而不能如期奔丧，赶到毗陵（常州）时岳母已下葬。<br /></div><div class='label1' id='131c1b764b00412b9a20f7b809f6f49a_label'><a href='javascript: DetailSwitch("131c1b764b00412b9a20f7b809f6f49a");'><span id='131c1b764b00412b9a20f7b809f6f49a_link' class='switch'>—</span></a><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1164&endYear=1164')">1164年</a>，31岁</div><div id='131c1b764b00412b9a20f7b809f6f49a' class='detail'><span style='margin: 0 0.5em; color: gray;'>▪</span>稽延武进妻子娘家，墓祭岳母。作品：墓祭外舅姑文。<div id='poem_1273895' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1273895' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1273895?labeling=true' target='_blank'>墓祭外舅姑文</a><span class='authorDate'>（1164年1月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 南宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(31376, "南宋", "薛季宣", "poem_title_1273895")'>薛季宣</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1273895_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1273895'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1273895'>某不天，生六年而亡失怙恃，丈人为子择对，以为无以易吾故人之子。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1273895_comment'></div>居四年，而伯考待制始纳徵礼，又七年，而昏乃克成。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1273895_comment'></div>其年丈人帅荆州，处我记室之任。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1273895_comment'></div>越三年府罢，将我西游于蜀。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1273895_comment'></div>居半年而别，别三年而丈人解荆州。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1273895_comment'></div>某观省自东瓯，时丈人归甫数日，相顾悦怿，乐以忘言。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1273895_comment'></div>不图改月之间，丈人捐弃舍馆。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1273895_comment'></div>后二年，丈人既葬，某哭于尹原之墓，乃复于故家。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1273895_comment'></div>抵家翌日，而恶梦兆祥，丈母以其日即世。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1273895_comment'></div>虽哀伤如割，而贫瘁不办奔丧，临不及掩。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1273895_comment'></div>后六年，始克展哀于墓，又不能与其女偕。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1273895_comment'></div>隐衋于中，辞文曷究，哀哉，言之不可极已！<div class='inline'
