id='poem_sentence_11_1273895_comment'></div>惟自丈人录我舅甥之列，终始将二十年，礼曰宾亲，爱均子姓。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1273895_comment'></div>某繇依舅馆，获奉丈母于堂，爱之亲之，亲加众婿。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1273895_comment'></div>自人而论，盖爱女者之常情。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1273895_comment'></div>生相思，死相远，此德不报，在某则多负矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1273895_comment'></div>然世已相知舅姑于我之厚，而殊不知厚有加于此者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1273895_comment'></div>昔我先大夫右史下世，适在权豪之柄国，妒疾谠正，号称党人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1273895_comment'></div>先人以赵氏而升，死和戎之议，一时契故不克收恤其后者，于理势固宜。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1273895_comment'></div>丈人惇切旧交，相攸我乐，终始教字，望以先人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1273895_comment'></div>此先人感槩交情，见诸先兄将仕之梦者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1273895_comment'></div>斯盖古人相与之义，在丈人固优为之；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1273895_comment'></div>而丈母之心，恩我又母子如也，宁以泉亭假馆。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1273895_comment'></div>不忘我先宜人一日之故，抑亦夫之所厚，固当亲厚之邪？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1273895_comment'></div>呜呼！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1273895_comment'></div>此风不作也久矣，使某微舅姑之教，则今何有所立？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1273895_comment'></div>拊心恳恻，负负何言！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1273895_comment'></div>惟是舅姑念我之深，愿之进学，爱其女子，奇其外孙。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1273895_comment'></div>今独有涵泳六经，尽心于大学之道，和舅姑之爱子而教诲其外孙，庶几雍睦于家，不坠我先人之绪，且以慰舅姑之心于九地之下，或可以无慊。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1273895_comment'></div>虽然，今日之事，固已负初心矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1273895_comment'></div>一杯之奠，悲欲忘生，乌呼哀哉，惟神灵是监飨！</div><div id='poem_sentence_30_1273895_comment'></div></div></div><br /><span style='margin: 0 0.5em; color: gray;'>▪</span>在武进。与妻弟访延陵道士何希全。作品：纪游诗。<br /></div><div class='label1' id='18d3ef95a6104baab5ac34d6678a3a7d_label'><a href='javascript: DetailSwitch("18d3ef95a6104baab5ac34d6678a3a7d");'><span id='18d3ef95a6104baab5ac34d6678a3a7d_link' class='switch'>—</span></a><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1168&endYear=1168')">1168年</a>，35岁</div><div id='18d3ef95a6104baab5ac34d6678a3a7d' class='detail'><span style='margin: 0 0.5em; color: gray;'>▪</span>夏，薛季宣前往婺州赴任。在之官途中，因王炎举荐，被召赴临安审察。季宣派人汇报政府，求终金华之任，未被批准，于是自富春下船，将家眷安排在延陵暂住，然后前往余杭。期间有书达先侄。作品：答象先侄书。<div id='poem_1273745' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1273745' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1273745?labeling=true' target='_blank'>答象先侄书</a><span class='authorDate'>（1168年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 南宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(31376, "南宋", "薛季宣", "poem_title_1273745")'>薛季宣</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1273745_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1273745'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1273745'>某启八五侄上舍：携别浸久，方切悬思。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1273745_comment'></div>仆归，收书，审知即日首夏乡炎，启处佳胜。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1273745_comment'></div>仍闻肄业湖上，挹山泉之清秀，以资涵养，供笔力之助，甚善。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1273745_comment'></div>尚须力自勉励，毋以时学而小之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1273745_comment'></div>得失付之于天，务为深醇盛大，以求经学之正。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1273745_comment'></div>讲明时务，本末利害必周知之，无为空言，无戾于行，则前辈之事何远之有。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1273745_comment'></div>学无今古，适睹时学，益人之大耳，位中上下皆安。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1273745_comment'></div>某以交代，尚欲补填一月，夏中可以即路交事，不出六月上中旬间。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1273745_comment'></div>房下粗安，它亡足道。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1273745_comment'></div>王枢书未欲作，方以州县窃禄自喜，姓名讵可关诸政路？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1273745_comment'></div>悠悠之议，自非众人所谓，人情服习苟且，宜吠所怪。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1273745_comment'></div>然道路籍籍，颇云有兵。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1273745_comment'></div>意良工之不示人以朴，莫无是否，羸病未药，而求孟贲手拼，闻其他日之论，当不如是疏也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1273745_comment'></div>作事若管夷吾可矣，其不切致主，以求欲速之功，令人多恨；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1273745_comment'></div>况侥倖成事，必无是理。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1273745_comment'></div>论者谓晋淝水之役以天幸，议谢文靖公父子。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1273745_comment'></div>每思军中欲害万石，不忍于一处士，所以用众，非一日之积矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1273745_comment'></div>方其命将，内拔诸不经事少年，以韩康伯与玄之疏，固已许之击贼；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1273745_comment'></div>郤诜怨也，知其必辞；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1273745_comment'></div>玄问计而安不应，荆援至而安不喜，方赌墅于王师之出，视捷书如无事。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1273745_comment'></div>有孚盈缶，宁徼天之幸邪？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1273745_comment'></div>身危死外，功弃不卒，其弊安出，亦若夷吾而已。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1273745_comment'></div>张魏公、刘开府望实俱丧，龟鉴不远，要此一著，不容再错。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1273745_comment'></div>前日尚可，如今大事去矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1273745_comment'></div>详思朝中人物，未见其辈。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1273745_comment'></div>观棋静处，每高当局未能忘情于物，故不能不眷眷于若人，因报及之，火之为望。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1273745_comment'></div>开馆相延固善，然公府不易作客，千万审处，无劳轻动。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1273745_comment'></div>景望失得有命，所谓举而不能先者之命欤？</div><div id='poem_sentence_27_1273745_comment'></div></div></div><br /><span style='margin: 0 0.5em; color: gray;'>▪</span>夏，薛季宣前往婺州赴任。在之官途中，因王炎举荐，被召赴临安审察。季宣派人汇报政府，求终金华之任，未被批准，于是自富春下船，将家眷安排在延陵暂住，然后前往余杭。期间有书致汪澈。作品：与汪枢使明远。<br /><span style='margin: 0 0.5em; color: gray;'>▪</span>夏，薛季宣前往婺州赴任。在之官途中，因王炎举荐，被召赴临安审察。季宣派人汇报政府，求终金华之任，未被批准，于是自富春下船，将家眷安排在延陵暂住，然后前往余杭。期间有书致王炎。作品：与王枢密公明。<br /></div><div class='label1' id='cd353a566a8a480b973a40d4e89ef4bc_label'><a href='javascript: DetailSwitch("cd353a566a8a480b973a40d4e89ef4bc");'><span id='cd353a566a8a480b973a40d4e89ef4bc_link' class='switch'>—</span></a><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1168&endYear=1171')">1168-1171年</a>，35-38岁</div><div id='cd353a566a8a480b973a40d4e89ef4bc' class='detail'><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1168&endYear=1168')">1168年</a>　回到毗陵妻子娘家待缺。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1169&endYear=1169')">1169年</a>　是年，在毗陵待缺。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1169&endYear=1169')">1169年3月</a>　在毗陵待缺。三月，王炎任四川宣抚使。薛季宣上书王炎。作品：与四川宣抚使王枢密劄子。与王枢密公明。<div id='poem_1273640' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1273640' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1273640?labeling=true' target='_blank'>与四川宣抚王枢密劄子</a><span class='authorDate'>（1169年3月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 南宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(31376, "南宋", "薛季宣", "poem_title_1273640")'>薛季宣</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1273640_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1273640'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1273640'>某闻之：善治水者必涤其源，善呼卢者必丰其本。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1273640_comment'></div>治水而涤其源，则下流无壅阏之患，滔滔赴海，安行而顺导之耳；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1273640_comment'></div>呼卢而丰其本，则在我之气胜，而为之对者索，十卢随掷，遂可气吞之矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1273640_comment'></div>皇上愤匈奴之未灭，痛神州之陆沈，谓关中中夏之本源，柄政之臣，又本源之所赖以疏涤者，乃眷西顾，辍大参于中极，寄以召伯之任，所以为涤源者，端有本矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1273640_comment'></div>三川之气，待公而振；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1273640_comment'></div>关河之沴，待公而清。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1273640_comment'></div>譬诸呼卢之望赢，非丰其本不可也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1273640_comment'></div>仆，故吏也，间尝从事于蜀，目睹生民之憔悴；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1273640_comment'></div>官于湖外，又尝得其梗概于道途。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1273640_comment'></div>究观规模，稽诸故实，论以成败之法，可得而言。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1273640_comment'></div>今公为万里行，仆方有弱小之累，不能自赞请从革辂之后尘，伏念早蒙特达之知，曾无伦匹于世。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1273640_comment'></div>德之不报，何以自宁？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1273640_comment'></div>夷门一言，愿钧坐安受之而毋忽也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1273640_comment'></div>梁益之地，久苦重征，自承平时固然。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1273640_comment'></div>南渡之初，一切取办，关外之众，仰之而给；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1273640_comment'></div>总领既设，益起上供，郡县苛刻征之，非复名数之见，民之困悴，殆嗷嗷无告矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1273640_comment'></div>朝廷虽时时捐减其数，是皆虚无积累之名，以为实惠及民，但自欺耳。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1273640_comment'></div>疲弊之极，救之良难。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1273640_comment'></div>如无守令之贤，则将何事不有？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1273640_comment'></div>民困若此，谓其本之丰可乎？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1273640_comment'></div>戍兵之众，旧蜀无之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1273640_comment'></div>自失关中，退屯汉沔，西极陇坂，东接商颜南山之阳，谷累数十，带甲不逮十万，而虏不能窥者，良以置帅之法，兵民兼涖，无改陕西之旧，大军堡砦相为首尾，守之得其道尔。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1273640_comment'></div>近自将臣过计，避岐雍而击熙河，顿兵旁角之地，不得展吾所长，挫锋于泾原，弃师于德顺，多刺流散以补亡师之缺，怙权擅地而要姑息于时，因其死而削之权，数当然也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1273640_comment'></div>然今藩臣不典兵马，则有警无以自救；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1273640_comment'></div>官军既难调发，而人心亦复不同。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1273640_comment'></div>风尘之惊，势同呼吸，心待行府之令，则蹈后时之悔矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1273640_comment'></div>兵非素练，帅非旧职，边氓无所依怙，则将折入于北。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1273640_comment'></div>军政若此，谓之丰本可乎？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1273640_comment'></div>二者则然，又有迫于此者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1273640_comment'></div>岷、宕之西，威、茂以北，杂蕃之境，近接成都，盗假之涂，信宿可至；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1273640_comment'></div>均、房，南出夔，直其冲。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_30_1273640_comment'></div>太祖之师尝入此道，言边备者曾莫之虞。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_31_1273640_comment'></div>变起腹心，盍先备豫，丰本之计，又当谋之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_32_1273640_comment'></div>为元戎忧，仆窃以为此数者，尤所当先者也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_33_1273640_comment'></div>参相识造几微，雅意人物，补苴罅漏，夫何足言！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_34_1273640_comment'></div>中州削平，当在兹举，千疮百痏，谓之何哉？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_35_1273640_comment'></div>处内护前，宁得无虑？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_36_1273640_comment'></div>必也为之有道，使人不疑，监往者坏之之由，思来者救之之计，为此一著，不容再错。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_37_1273640_comment'></div>譬之丰本之博，将安往而不胜乎？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_38_1273640_comment'></div>虽然，起羸瘵者不可以力加人，大有为者不可见形于敌。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_39_1273640_comment'></div>第丰吾本，无为兵先，机会之来，何容穷尽！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_40_1273640_comment'></div>扼其吭领之地，则形格而势禁，三秦平定，盖此术耳。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_41_1273640_comment'></div>持此上报明天子，涤源之计，顾不伟欤！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_42_1273640_comment'></div>至于姜维覆败之道，往固不可追，于今尚多有之，惟行府终始念之也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_43_1273640_comment'></div>某私忧过计，欲补千虑之一得，不佞不敏，然之却之，惟所命！</div><div id='poem_sentence_44_1273640_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1169&endYear=1169')">1169年</a>　在毗陵待缺。春，致书汪澈。作品：与汪枢密明远。<div id='poem_1273639' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1273639' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1273639?labeling=true' target='_blank'>又与王枢密劄子</a><span class='authorDate'>（1169年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 南宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(31376, "南宋", "薛季宣", "poem_title_1273639")'>薛季宣</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1273639_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1273639'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1273639'>初二日、初九日两被呼召，侍坐函席，诲以话言，遂及边计。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1273639_comment'></div>忧众之所不忧，又将为人所不能为，以为当及虏无事时，大为边防，事至图之，无及于事，非以身任天下之责者，其谁知之？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1273639_comment'></div>岂特门生故吏忻幸之私，实宗社苍生之望。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1273639_comment'></div>仆后生妄庸，既被恩奖，当时不避狂斐，随问辄对，言不尽意，退而惘然。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1273639_comment'></div>今当远去钧屏，思报万一，不知所出，愿效一言，敢疏管窥，庶有山海涓尘之补，伏惟钧慈采察而审图之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1273639_comment'></div>比年人情苟且，类少深远之谋，众人幸于偷安，狂妄则希生事。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1273639_comment'></div>偷安固一切不问，生事则轻议伐人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1273639_comment'></div>且不备不虞，不可以师；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1273639_comment'></div>不知彼己而轻易用兵者，百战百殆而已。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1273639_comment'></div>虏人之情，传闻常多失实。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1273639_comment'></div>其在兵法，用间号为尤难。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1273639_comment'></div>古人譬水之能载舟覆舟，不轻信之如此。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1273639_comment'></div>圣人内求诸己，无取于物，我自能而何敌之问焉？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1273639_comment'></div>国家上当同君臣之心，明忠邪之辨，众贤登进，百度自举，感神格天，何求不获？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1273639_comment'></div>区区夷虏，夫何足道！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1273639_comment'></div>其次淮堧之地，当施罗落；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1273639_comment'></div>江流海道，合置水军。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1273639_comment'></div>昨闻山阳、合肥之谋，规模既已略尽，江海之备，则殊未闻。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1273639_comment'></div>其间间道所行，我之素不讲者，天长可以入维扬，清流可以向六合，肥水可以下合肥；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1273639_comment'></div>北峡之隘，庐江之径，与武昌之近，新息、秭归之比；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1273639_comment'></div>商于、贾堑、三关直趋荆、鄂，子午南达梁、洋，洮、岷东近威、茂。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1273639_comment'></div>前人用兵所经，斥候又当明远，忽而不备，则邓艾江油之事，不可便谓无之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1273639_comment'></div>冲要虽有重兵之屯，坚城之守，中无民力，且乏粮械之资，则亦未可谓之万全。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1273639_comment'></div>人情苟安，不知为备之说，欲为守御，固当力施行之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1273639_comment'></div>言议悠悠，何益于事！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1273639_comment'></div>至如用兵一事，起于喜事之臣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1273639_comment'></div>窃尝论以孙子始计之书，盖未知其可也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1273639_comment'></div>方今人人异意，不可谓道；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1273639_comment'></div>灾变数起，不可谓天；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1273639_comment'></div>以江左而争中原，不可谓地；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1273639_comment'></div>以贪戾而帅骄卒，不可谓将；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_30_1273639_comment'></div>将士不相安习，不可谓法。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_31_1273639_comment'></div>于斯五者，曾莫之计，又不可谓知之也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_32_1273639_comment'></div>恭惟主上天纵之圣，曾非龙荒所得伦拟，则主孰有道，在所不论。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_33_1273639_comment'></div>至于将孰有能，天地孰得，法令孰行，兵众孰强，士卒孰练，赏罚孰明，彼固不容尽知，其在我者亦可以知之矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_34_1273639_comment'></div>虏能包藏隐忍以成鸣镝之事，未可以无能视之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_35_1273639_comment'></div>捕盗之军、归卧之帅，又安知非彼之谋？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_36_1273639_comment'></div>前虏方易主时，我以全师临制其后，尚无尺寸之效，则今未易图也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_37_1273639_comment'></div>我自隆兴、乾道之后，星文屡变，水潦荐臻，流离之民充满道路，骄悍之卒气凌州府；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_38_1273639_comment'></div>或悖而辱长吏，或起而为盗贼，皆有形验，安可谓加于虏？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_39_1273639_comment'></div>且以区区江左，经纬中夏，以一图九，古人固已寒心，求之时贤，恐不易办，虽以恩地之重，仆犹以为未可必也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_40_1273639_comment'></div>方今兵力既弱，财力空匮，所恃以战者不过三衙、御前之众，旧人既已垂尽，江南白丁未可望以持久。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_41_1273639_comment'></div>所仰以济者，不过常平钱米，应在虚数，州县尽然，问之甚多，求实无有，赈济已自不给，必将上误军计。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_42_1273639_comment'></div>以此用众，其能济乎？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_43_1273639_comment'></div>兵交于前，人困于后，安知卢循之盗，寄奴、霸先之将，不又起于萧墙之内？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_44_1273639_comment'></div>事至而悔，将何及哉！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_45_1273639_comment'></div>昔宋文帝河南之谋，其算殆无遗策，终无成济，胡马饮江而治遂衰；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_46_1273639_comment'></div>太祖皇帝谋取幽州，赵普以为必得，问将谁守，因不复言。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_47_1273639_comment'></div>今之治功与一时之将帅，未能贤于元嘉之世，其望太祖固已辽绝，不监不法，将恐辱甚于饮江；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_48_1273639_comment'></div>即幸胜之，仆窃意其方劳庙算也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_49_1273639_comment'></div>主上用兵之意，每形天语，空言挑虏，兵计固当然乎？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_50_1273639_comment'></div>有谋人之心而使敌人疑之，殆矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_51_1273639_comment'></div>枢密忠诚体国，愿垂深念。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_52_1273639_comment'></div>致君尧舜，望惟以仁义纲纪为本；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_53_1273639_comment'></div>备边之计，幸勿为浮议摇动。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_54_1273639_comment'></div>至于用兵，则请留待十年之后，必以机会而举。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_55_1273639_comment'></div>人才既富，彝伦既叙，虏之世世淫暴，必将有颉利之功矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_56_1273639_comment'></div>且自古未有寄任不专，孤立无助，小人不去，而能成功立事者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_57_1273639_comment'></div>诚能和同君臣之际固善，如曰事出九重，制不在己，则当以义进退，不可身坐庙堂而叹志之不伸也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_58_1273639_comment'></div>仆受恩深厚，不知言之妄发，万死未足以谢，惟幸察之！</div><div id='poem_sentence_59_1273639_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1169&endYear=1169')">1169年</a>　在毗陵待缺。秋，写信给陈傅良。作品：答君举书二。<div id='poem_1273721' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1273721' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1273721?labeling=true' target='_blank'>答陈同父<span class='inlineComment2'>（亮）</span>书</a><span class='authorDate'>（1169年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 南宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(31376, "南宋", "薛季宣", "poem_title_1273721")'>薛季宣</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1273721_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1273721'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1273721'>某自戊子入都，得左右之文于景望四三哥之舍，于四三哥、王枢使闻宾从之学业气志，每以未及识面，聆謦欬之音为歉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1273721_comment'></div>及趋召道宛陵，四三哥寄朋友书二，其一左右，一君举也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1273721_comment'></div>洎访旧知于学，则闻二陈之名籍甚。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1273721_comment'></div>京师旋沐，从者访临，获亲名理之益，从知名下之无虚士。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1273721_comment'></div>谚非虚语，私以得与从游为喜。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1273721_comment'></div>已辱开怀倾写，临途要无可道，然而别不及面，宁无惘惘。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1273721_comment'></div>被教敬审，即日冬序正寒，温侍有相，尊候万福。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1273721_comment'></div>学官秋试，遂遗贤者，士夫不能无恨，得失有命，时运故应然邪？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1273721_comment'></div>乡使举无留才，则何以为造化？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1273721_comment'></div>但在我本无患得之意，未始低头就之，则吾同父之失，较之君举之得，亦复何愧。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1273721_comment'></div>冲天惊人之<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_10_1273721", 1273721, "Clauses/37/Comments/0")'>轩奋</span>，岂有迟速间哉！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1273721_comment'></div>体用之诲，备认高旨，某何足知此，然不敢以不敏而罢。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1273721_comment'></div>夫道之不可迩，未遽以体用论。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1273721_comment'></div>见之时措，体用疑若可识，卒之何者为体，何者为用，即以徒善徒法为体用之别，体用固如是邪？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1273721_comment'></div>上形下形，曰道曰器，道无形埒，舍器将安适哉？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1273721_comment'></div>且道非器可名，然不远物，则常存乎<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_15_1273721", 1273721, "Clauses/57/Comments/0")'>形器</span>之内，昧者离器于道，以为非道遗之，非但不能知器，亦不知道矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1273721_comment'></div>下学上达，惟天知之，知天而后可以得天之知，决非学异端、遗<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_16_1273721", 1273721, "Clauses/65/Comments/1")'>形器</span>者之求之见。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1273721_comment'></div>礼仪威仪，待夫人而后行耳，苟不至德，谁能知味？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1273721_comment'></div>日用自知之谓，其切当矣乎！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1273721_comment'></div>曾子日且三省其身，吾曹安可辄废检察？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1273721_comment'></div>且不识不知、顺帝之则者，古人事业，学不至此，恐至道之不凝。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1273721_comment'></div>此事自得，则当深知，殆未可以言言之也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1273721_comment'></div>以同父天资之高，检察之至，信如有见，必能自隐诸心；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1273721_comment'></div>如曰未然，则凡平日上论古人，下观当世，举而措之于事者，无非小知謏闻之累，未可认以为实。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1273721_comment'></div>弟于事物之上，习于心无适莫，则将天理自见，持之以久，会当知之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1273721_comment'></div>《洪范》「无党无偏」，《大学》「不能其正」，真万病之针石，独无意于斯乎？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1273721_comment'></div>某非曰能之，冀共事斯语耳。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1273721_comment'></div>葬议甚韪，近过伯恭不遇，尚须续报，志铭某岂敢？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1273721_comment'></div>何故舍四三哥，发<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_28_1273721", 1273721, "Clauses/107/Comments/0")'>潜德</span>之幽光？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1273721_comment'></div>某愧焉多矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1273721_comment'></div>妥齐铭文本欲相名如周公之与《君奭》，君举以为《君奭》王事；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_30_1273721_comment'></div>表德，朋友之谊也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_31_1273721_comment'></div>名近师道，有所不可，不然，何惜一换？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_32_1273721_comment'></div>试更思之，某碌碌素餐，强颜留处，于朝家亡毫发补，未能决去为愧。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_33_1273721_comment'></div>同父望以世道，譬如觅金于窭者，何不知我之深邪！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_34_1273721_comment'></div>轮对当在来春，只等一见后，求外补州县，差可及物。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_35_1273721_comment'></div>尸素欲何为哉！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_36_1273721_comment'></div>不足为人言之，恐欲知何所向尔。</div><div id='poem_sentence_37_1273721_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1169&endYear=1169')">1169年</a>　在毗陵待缺。叶适上书薛季宣问学，薛季宣有书作答。作品：答叶适书。<div id='poem_1273744' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1273744' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1273744?labeling=true' target='_blank'>答叶适书</a><span class='authorDate'>（1169年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 南宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(31376, "南宋", "薛季宣", "poem_title_1273744")'>薛季宣</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1273744_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1273744'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1273744'>某闻之：务博学者必自约，乐教人者必自修。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1273744_comment'></div>执事通百氏诸子之书，可以为博矣；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1273744_comment'></div>为人师而学不厌，又知所谓约矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1273744_comment'></div>听于涂说，不以某之不肖，惠然肯顾，投以尺书，望我以急难，扣我以学问，以诸葛武乡之英特，谓我闻风而慕之；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1273744_comment'></div>以王梅溪、郑著作一乡之善士，许以雁行而肩随。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1273744_comment'></div>某虽至愚，自知甚悉，未能为己，何以为人，未克自明，于何明物？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1273744_comment'></div>若武乡则吾岂敢，王梅溪之方正，郑著作之冲养，是皆吾党之望，愿学焉而未能者，其又何可拟邪！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1273744_comment'></div>读诵腼颜，不知何自而得此也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1273744_comment'></div>范文正公镇陕右，孙泰山、张横渠初以游客干之，公能资以读书，告之名教之乐，二先生赖以有立，卒为天下大儒。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1273744_comment'></div>范公得位时任大，非吾事也，名教之乐，愿与执事同之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1273744_comment'></div>执事秀发妙龄，多闻多识，通于古，明于文，行不自贤，不耻下问，一日千里，吾知方发轫焉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1273744_comment'></div>及于八陈为邦，将无著鞭之太蚤，而某庸敢当也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1273744_comment'></div>约文以礼，颜氏所以立于仲尼之门，执事方以教人，敢请从事于此。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1273744_comment'></div>若夫夏时、商辂、周冕、韶乐，四代损益，孔子非亚圣弗之告。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1273744_comment'></div>先王寓兵丘井，建之邦国，舞之行缀，教民后战，不以军容入国，有本有末，躐等之学难矣乎！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1273744_comment'></div>言志而贤舞雩，问陈而称俎豆，为学自有次第，仲尼岂欺我哉！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1273744_comment'></div>故欲执事先之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1273744_comment'></div>军旅为邦，愿执事之姑舍是也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1273744_comment'></div>抑某又尝闻之，子夏曰「君子敬而无失，与人恭而有礼」，「四海之内皆兄弟也」，士患敬恭之不立，夫不容奚病焉？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1273744_comment'></div>修道教人，执事其从容于是矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1273744_comment'></div>执事有亲之奉，日虞甘旨之弗给，不抵人而抵我，其所望于我者甚厚且深，某方空腹而游，独行踽踽，不足相为轩轾，以孤从来之意。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1273744_comment'></div>甚恐，姑诵所闻于博约之说者，复之将命，执事之不我弃，庶几能谅之乎？</div><div id='poem_sentence_21_1273744_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1169&endYear=1169')">1169年</a>　在毗陵待缺。冬，陈傅良前往毗陵，学于薛季宣门下。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1170&endYear=1170')">1170年</a>　在毗陵。春，因刘朔之荐，朝廷召薛季宣赴临安审察。薛季宣固辞不就，刘朔以君命相讽励。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1170&endYear=1170')">1170年</a>　在毗陵。上书陈左相，力求终常熟县令之任，不被批准。作品：与陈左相。<span class='inlineComment2'>（交游者姓名为录入者据史所补。）</span><div id='poem_1273680' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1273680' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1273680?labeling=true' target='_blank'>与陈左相书</a><span class='authorDate'>（1170年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 南宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(31376, "南宋", "薛季宣", "poem_title_1273680")'>薛季宣</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1273680_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1273680'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1273680'>即日首夏清和，恭惟燮调元化，尊主庇民，天寔相之，钧候动止万福。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1273680_comment'></div>某荐蒙命召，非望所及，此惟造化甄陶之内，都无弃物，虽如樗散，亦有瘿壶之用，落落难合，终不忍捐。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1273680_comment'></div>某乡也未尝扫门一拜，亦无牖间半面之雅，得之知识，已蒙钧慈眷眄之旨厚甚，收召亡补，重惜其去。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1273680_comment'></div>行不旋踵，而弓旌之赐已及门矣，求之于古名德之相，所以进豪杰之士者如此，某小丑，其何足以当之？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1273680_comment'></div>顾今英豪未闻尽用，虽曰昭王致士，先自隗始，旌显卜式，风示天下，某人非隗、式之贤，独蒙眷眷如许。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1273680_comment'></div>《缁衣》之好，将无示人之不宏乎？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1273680_comment'></div>窃恐不肖之进，贤者怠矣，愿回兹施推之贤于某者，庶几周士济济，上格圣心，以兴底平极治之功，天下幸甚，天下幸甚！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1273680_comment'></div>某敢沥肝胆，仰干钧听。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1273680_comment'></div>某曩尝蒙赐对矣，学术浅陋，不能有所裨益，改秩不谢，大为人士所非。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1273680_comment'></div>今犹乡者之人，才不加进，贪冒荣利，深畏友朋之非议己也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1273680_comment'></div>已具劄目，仰告庙堂，得蒙敷奏许之，莫大之幸。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1273680_comment'></div>君子爱人以德，钧慈念之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1273680_comment'></div>某前诣阙庭，伏蒙礼遇甚宠，请违主客，已涉二年，虽依仰黄扉，如川流百折之未尝不东，以为閒居小官，不当奏记相府，两闻册拜，只与有识之士相庆于下，而函笺贺悃，顾不复陈，素蒙知眷之隆，必当不以虚文督过之也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1273680_comment'></div>鳞番诇诇，不敢自同众人，幅纸通勤，敢乞钧照！</div><div id='poem_sentence_13_1273680_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1170&endYear=1170')">1170年</a>　在毗陵。上书虞允文，力求终常熟县令之任，不被批准。作品：与虞右相。<div id='poem_1273681' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1273681' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1273681?labeling=true' target='_blank'>与虞右相书</a><span class='authorDate'>（1162年2月1日）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 南宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(31376, "南宋", "薛季宣", "poem_title_1273681")'>薛季宣</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1273681_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1273681'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1273681'>某岁在辛巳、癸未间，试鄂之武昌令，伏遇元戎督视关陕，道出境上，初与齐安郡官旅谒律步，夙仰声谊，遂获一觇钧表，已剧私幸。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1273681_comment'></div>既而螭舫东返，又率戍县诸将迎见于大江中流。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1273681_comment'></div>伏蒙略去等威，席艕而坐，酌以卮酒，出示地图，虽悤悤拜违，接馀论之不款，然蒙钧慈礼遇之意，盖不与常人等矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1273681_comment'></div>当时戎行之士同泛而归，论公之贤，至有加手于额者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1273681_comment'></div>仰窥所以制服诸将、式遏乱略、参功微管者，岂徒然哉！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1273681_comment'></div>感叹之私，中藏亡已。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1273681_comment'></div>嗣以名位悬隔，道路阻修，诇问之函从不复贡，虽聆大拜，亦不敢修贺主书。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1273681_comment'></div>然而每与士夫共论当世王公，未尝不及鄂陵之所亲见，莫不吁嗟称叹，以为近世之所无也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1273681_comment'></div>敢谓精意人物，不遗菅蒯。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1273681_comment'></div>兹者荐蒙命召，寔出造化炉锤之力。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1273681_comment'></div>收之既去，诚出过恩；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1273681_comment'></div>非分得之，秪深愧仄。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1273681_comment'></div>顾今异昔，伏念之，某既蒙特达之知，诇候之仪，不敢自同疏远之士，赤纸奏记，敢冀钧察<span class='inlineComment2'>（云云）</span>。</div><div id='poem_sentence_12_1273681_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1170&endYear=1170')">1170年</a>　在毗陵。上书梁克家，力求终常熟县令之任，不被批准。作品：与梁枢密。<div id='poem_1273682' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1273682' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1273682?labeling=true' target='_blank'>与梁枢密书</a><span class='authorDate'>（1170年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 南宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(31376, "南宋", "薛季宣", "poem_title_1273682")'>薛季宣</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1273682_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1273682'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1273682'>某一介寒远，前此虽仰斗山之望，未尝趋谒下风；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1273682_comment'></div>曾无寸长，非有左右先容之助，已蒙论荐于上。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1273682_comment'></div>特达之知，近所未有。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1273682_comment'></div>此风之不作也久矣，贤人在上，引其类者岂曰无之，然多有求而后及也；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1273682_comment'></div>至于精意人物，不欲恩出私门。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1273682_comment'></div>人非识面，不俟有求而举，初不之告，自非王公大人以天下为度者，未有是事，求之前辈，政可一二数耳。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1273682_comment'></div>是在古人所以收召豪杰之士，某小丑，其何德以堪之？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1273682_comment'></div>乃者荐被弓招，又出造化财成之赐，眷言感愧，铭在心府<span class='inlineComment2'>（馀同二相。）</span>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1273682_comment'></div>某间者入都，才得再谒门下，仰詹钧表，以慰生平敬仰之私。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1273682_comment'></div>迫行虽一告违，适当谢客。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1273682_comment'></div>属朝辞已越日，不克留名，远去门墙，每怀怏罔。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1273682_comment'></div>自以閒居远外，不当通记辇下达官，故虽恩门，亦废承问之礼，仄闻贰公之拜。</div><div id='poem_sentence_11_1273682_comment'></div></div><div class='poemNote' id='poem_note_1273682'><span class='label'>按：</span>同左相。<br /></div><div id='poem_note_1273682_comment'></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1170&endYear=1170')">1170年</a>　在毗陵。上书王炎，力求终常熟县令之任，不被批准。作品：与王枢密公明。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1170&endYear=1170')">1170年</a>　在毗陵。上书张枢密，力求终常熟县令之任，不被批准。作品：张枢密劄子别纸。<div id='poem_1273684' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1273684' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1273684?labeling=true' target='_blank'>张枢密劄子别纸<sup class='reference inlineComment2'>①</sup></a><span class='authorDate'>（1170年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 南宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(31376, "南宋", "薛季宣", "poem_title_1273684")'>薛季宣</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1273684_comment'></div><div class='titleComment'><div class='inline1'><div id='poem_title_1273684_0'>① 不克上，明年复用，卒以前章抵之。</div></div></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1273684'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1273684'>某窃以南风之不竞也久矣，卿士大夫安故玩常，不以为辱。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1273684_comment'></div>往坐论流品，猎取高位，事业无见，为世嗤鄙。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1273684_comment'></div>陛下拨去晚唐数百年颓靡之习，举枢密而任之政，固已四方耸动，想闻风采。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1273684_comment'></div>恭惟盛德大业，时措之宜，所以上当王心，下副物望者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1273684_comment'></div>在规摹中自有次第，诚非晚生寒远之所侧知，然此任为不轻矣，宜当大有以填服天下，非为人所不能为者不可也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1273684_comment'></div>某尝谓今日之事，纪纲为急，不庭为后。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1273684_comment'></div>天下大务不过数端，振而起之，在执政大臣反掌顷耳。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1273684_comment'></div>王伯之道，安强之术，固无如此者，枢密其图之！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1273684_comment'></div></div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_8_1273684'>某狂易僭率，敢以迫切之恳，仰干钧重。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1273684_comment'></div>某昨以馀论吹嘘之赐，荐蒙审察之命。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1273684_comment'></div>自顾学术浅陋，曩尝荐对无补，秪冒宠章，欲进趑趄，娄伸终任之请，仰荷庙堂惇促数四，所求迄未听许。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1273684_comment'></div>窃念某家贫累重，前年被召于之官道中，因客毗陵，困不能返。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1273684_comment'></div>待阙十岁，贫病交攻，趣召且乏桂玉之资，穷处固无糊口之计，困瘁之状，不敢缕缕渎尊。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1273684_comment'></div>今常熟县见任人代期只在夏间，某以有上项恩旨，难以专辄交政，已具朝廷公状，丐一祠庙差遣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1273684_comment'></div>或许且令之任，得蒙借重九鼎，特赐敷奏，俯遂鄙志，得获少沾寸禄，一家免于倒垂之急，不胜大幸！</div><div id='poem_sentence_14_1273684_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1170&endYear=1170')">1170年</a>　在毗陵。上书参宰，力求终常熟县令之任，不被批准。作品：参宰禀目。<div id='poem_1273683' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1273683' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1273683?labeling=true' target='_blank'>参宰禀目</a><span class='authorDate'>（1170年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 南宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(31376, "南宋", "薛季宣", "poem_title_1273683")'>薛季宣</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1273683_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1273683'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1273683'>绝不奏记隔年矣，斗山之仰，徒切下情。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1273683_comment'></div>伏蒙希世特达之知，必不以苛礼督过之也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1273683_comment'></div>即日春晚暄妍，恭惟论道调元，寅亮贰公，夷夏邕睦，百神显相，钧候动止万福。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1273683_comment'></div>某仰恃帡幪，敢有诚恳。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1273683_comment'></div>某属者伏蒙甄陶引拔，猥有审察之命，一时同召，类被不次超擢，独某顾惭群彦，娄伸终任之请，仰荷眷怜，敦促数四。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1273683_comment'></div>三公之贵，降意下士之末列，兹事行之远古，为德之盛，寂寥久矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1273683_comment'></div>斐然狂简，何幸亲闻正始之音！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1273683_comment'></div>内顾凡庸，何可当也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1273683_comment'></div>矧士之求达，人情所同，如某厌于宰县之难，宁不愿为时用，而复逡循逊避，岂有他哉？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1273683_comment'></div>自惟所以处己未诚，苦乏感物之动。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1273683_comment'></div>曩者盖尝赐对，蔑有补于聪明；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1273683_comment'></div>虽蒙采录豪末之言，又为有司折言沮格。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1273683_comment'></div>惧涉崖异，受爵不辞，每一思之，泚焉背汗。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1273683_comment'></div>上念圣主有作，名宰辅方相与收揽天下豪英之士以备使令，俊乂如林，固不乏用。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1273683_comment'></div>某腹背之毳，无与重轻，进备一官，竟亦何补。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1273683_comment'></div>惟有修其进退廉隅之节，或可微动九重。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1273683_comment'></div>有如少感听闻，谓亦可为贤大臣致君一助。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1273683_comment'></div>某虽退而穷处，所获已多，况未为当世弃材，不为无补于政。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1273683_comment'></div>此古之君子爱人以德，所为动心者也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1273683_comment'></div>不与其退，直得前辈进贤不进不已之意。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1273683_comment'></div>某褊迫之见，尚愿取其一端，况某久次食乡，贫于之官，道中被召，因客异县，困不能归，其视古人妇儿无禈不袜之穷，不过是矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1273683_comment'></div>常熟当上以有前命，未可以行，远念在武昌时，以罢羸数千户，外应营筑、馈输之繁，内事战船、军戍、批支百役，虽幸不以罪斥，愧负已深。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1273683_comment'></div>代还十年，又苦多病。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1273683_comment'></div>今此京辅剧县，其可以虚愚妄处之邪？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1273683_comment'></div>自知百不如人，百念久已灰冷，徒以世仕，未能退耕而食，室家蛰蛰，所不免者，尚仰禄耳。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1273683_comment'></div>已具状申朝廷，丐陶铸一祠，或且许令之任，得蒙借重九鼎，一赐敷奏，获如鄙志，其为终始成就大矣！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1273683_comment'></div>干渎钧听，某不任栗栗末阶<span class='inlineComment2'>（云云）</span>。</div><div id='poem_sentence_26_1273683_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1170&endYear=1170')">1170年</a>　在毗陵。上书请祠，不被答复。作品：再召辞免劄子。请祠申省状。再辞召命申省状。劄子。又状。<div id='poem_1273628' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1273628' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1273628?labeling=true' target='_blank'>再召辞免劄子</a><span class='authorDate'>（1170年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 南宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(31376, "南宋", "薛季宣", "poem_title_1273628")'>薛季宣</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1273628_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1273628'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1273628'>某准尚书省劄子，奉圣旨令赴都堂审察。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1273628_comment'></div>窃以间年再召，殊异乎常伦；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1273628_comment'></div>顾影多惭，岂加于曩日？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1273628_comment'></div>祗可循墙以走，难从不驾之行。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1273628_comment'></div>伏念某才不踰人，学非适用，仕之藉荫，禄以代耕，曾微一善之可称，已得九重之过听。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1273628_comment'></div>弓招下逮，取诸选调之中；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1273628_comment'></div>扆座为前，擢视王官之列。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1273628_comment'></div>顾雨露草木之恩甚溥，如海岳涓尘之补则亡，下拜腼颜，迄今汗背。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1273628_comment'></div>敢谓下才之樗散，旋蒙命召之鼎来，得之若惊，眷前增愧。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1273628_comment'></div>在进退而惟谷，诚若古人之言；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1273628_comment'></div>不往来之惮烦，窃怀友朋之畏。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1273628_comment'></div>所愿庙堂之俯察，许迟县邑之终更。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1273628_comment'></div>尚冀修为，以图报称。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1273628_comment'></div>某下情无任皇惧战栗、俯伏俟命之至。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1273628_comment'></div>伏乞钧慈，特赐敷奏施行。</div><div id='poem_sentence_14_1273628_comment'></div></div></div><div id='poem_1273630' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1273630' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1273630?labeling=true' target='_blank'>请祠申省状</a><span class='authorDate'>（1170年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 南宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(31376, "南宋", "薛季宣", "poem_title_1273630")'>薛季宣</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1273630_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1273630'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1273630'>准敕授前件差遣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1273630_comment'></div>续准尚书省劄子，三省同奉圣旨，令赴都堂审察。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1273630_comment'></div>某窃伏自念，嵬琐之质，术业浅陋，已尝赐对亡补，徒冒宠荣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1273630_comment'></div>材能不异于前人，问学无加于往日，而复容容昧进，非心所安，辄敢上干堂陛之严，屡伸终任之请。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1273630_comment'></div>仰蒙庙堂眷私，敦促至于数四。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1273630_comment'></div>恐孤所以期遇，每欲进而趑趄。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1273630_comment'></div>虽卷卷之诚，久之颇见幸察；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1273630_comment'></div>而由衷之恳，弥年尚未听从。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1273630_comment'></div>今常熟县见任人赵善括去替在一两月间，某以有上项恩旨，未敢专辄前去之任，更合申取朝廷指挥。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1273630_comment'></div>窃缘某比岁以来，得疾异甚，精华日耗，大惧损生，所授号剧繁难，必不胜任。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1273630_comment'></div>况又家贫累重，待阙十年，久客他州，非禄无以糊口。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1273630_comment'></div>伏望仆射相公参政钧慈矜悯，特赐陶铸祠庙差遣一次。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1273630_comment'></div>庶几少安微分，养痾之外，得以尽意学业，或备异时器使之列。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1273630_comment'></div>须至申闻者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1273630_comment'></div></div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_14_1273630'>右，谨具状申尚书省，伏望检会累申劄状，特赐敷奏，所有作降审察指挥，欲乞更不施行。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1273630_comment'></div>谨状。</div><div id='poem_sentence_15_1273630_comment'></div></div></div><div id='poem_1273631' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1273631' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1273631?labeling=true' target='_blank'>再辞召命申省状</a><span class='authorDate'>（1170年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 南宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(31376, "南宋", "薛季宣", "poem_title_1273631")'>薛季宣</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1273631_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1273631'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1273631'>准尚书省劄子，奉圣旨令赴都堂审察。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1273631_comment'></div>某寻具劄子申仆射相公、参政府，乞终常熟新任，未蒙施行。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1273631_comment'></div>再准尚书省劄子，催某疾速起发前来，须至申禀者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1273631_comment'></div></div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_1273631'>右，某伏闻人有常言，小官不当辞命。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1273631_comment'></div>窃谓心之辞逊，不在官之崇庳。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1273631_comment'></div>当辞而不辞者贪也，可进而不进者伪也，惟贪与伪，何以事君！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1273631_comment'></div>其有谊或可辞，礼未容进，均之失也，宁伪无贪。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1273631_comment'></div>伏念某素乏技能，蚤蒙荐对，备尝罄竭，无益聪明，沓冒宠荣，祗深愧腼，方期下邑，少效秋毫。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1273631_comment'></div>何贤于人，弓招荐及；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1273631_comment'></div>庸敢为伪，请固以辞。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1273631_comment'></div>且某才不加长，学非至到。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1273631_comment'></div>强揠其智，则固何堪，迁就其言，又所不敢，纵蒙审察，岂过前时？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1273631_comment'></div>如某之流，世固不乏，进为贪也，孰与虽贤？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1273631_comment'></div>使某得为天下知退之人，寔可仰副朝廷励俗之意。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1273631_comment'></div>此某所以不避小官之嫌，辄冒尊严而进再三之渎也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1273631_comment'></div>谨具状申尚书省，伏乞检会某前此呈劄，特赐敷奏，俯从所请施行。</div><div id='poem_sentence_15_1273631_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1170&endYear=1170')">1170年</a>　在毗陵。夏，写信给喻樗，请他述录赵鼎遗事，以补史载之缺。作品：与喻郎中。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1170&endYear=1170')">1170年</a>　在毗陵。又作《与沈应先书》<div id='poem_1273726' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1273726' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1273726?labeling=true' target='_blank'>与沈应先<span class='inlineComment2'>（有开）</span>书</a><span class='authorDate'>（1170年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 南宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(31376, "南宋", "薛季宣", "poem_title_1273726")'>薛季宣</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1273726_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1273726'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1273726'>君举相见所谈，谓何得无多过其实。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1273726_comment'></div>大抵爱之不知其恶，何容尽信？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1273726_comment'></div>谆谆之谕，何敢当也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1273726_comment'></div>某所行天下，阅士多矣，好善笃，信道深，求如吾应先者曾未之见。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1273726_comment'></div>然而以此见望，近乎不知而作。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1273726_comment'></div>夫人未能为己，安能为人？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1273726_comment'></div>某之自为若何，其何以承盛意？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1273726_comment'></div>然闻责善朋友之道，于此不当有隐，又不知野芹辽豕，不见笑于大方之家乎？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1273726_comment'></div>自大学之不明，其道散在天下，得其小者往往自名一家，高者沦入虚无，下者凝滞于物，狂狷异俗，要非中庸先王大经，遂皆指为无用，滔滔皆是，未易夺也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1273726_comment'></div>故须拔萃豪杰，超然远见，道揆法守，浑为一途，蒙养本根，源泉时出，使人心说诚服，得之观感而化乃可为耳。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1273726_comment'></div>此事甚大，既非一日之积，又非尽智穷力所到，故圣人难言之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1273726_comment'></div>后世昧于诚明明诚之分，遂谓有不学而能者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1273726_comment'></div>彼天之道，何与于人之道？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1273726_comment'></div>致曲未尽，何以能有诚哉？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1273726_comment'></div>孟氏「必有事焉，而勿正，心勿忘、勿助长也」之说，虽非圣人优之柔之，使自求之之意，学者于此从事，思过半矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1273726_comment'></div>颜氏之子，其过与怒，宁与人异？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1273726_comment'></div>不可及处，正在不以怒迁，不以过贰，一节法守之事。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1273726_comment'></div>此吾圣人所以异于贰本者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1273726_comment'></div>空无之家，不可谓无所见，迄无所用，不知所谓不贰者尔。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1273726_comment'></div>未明道揆通于法守之务，要终为无用。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1273726_comment'></div>洒扫进退，虽为威仪之一，古人以谓道无本末者，其视任心而作，居然有间然。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1273726_comment'></div>云「文、武之道，具在方册」，「其人存，其政举」，「苟非其人，道不虚行」，要须自得之也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1273726_comment'></div>学不至于「不识不知，顺帝之则」，竟亦何用？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1273726_comment'></div>有如未办澡心藏密，莫若去故去智。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1273726_comment'></div>古人言「读书百遍，其义自见」，未易以浅近夺信；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1273726_comment'></div>能反复涵泳，会当有得，得之小大，则系乎精诚所至。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1273726_comment'></div>时文称于一经之内，有一言之悟，则六经之义灿然矣，不可以人废言也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1273726_comment'></div>事非笔舌可道，而言之不无罗缕，遐不谓矣，政须体悉，不足为它人道也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1273726_comment'></div>喻丈书承寄示，甚感。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1273726_comment'></div>遂能不废刍荛之论，尤见前辈忠厚之风，前事赖以有传，非小补也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1273726_comment'></div>乡闻彼知旧闻有《方舆记》，望为经营一借，如不可则已。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_30_1273726_comment'></div>之君举，见告藏室中有《越绝书》，未之见，曩得其一二事，未详始末，辄欲求假，一寻绎之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_31_1273726_comment'></div>师友之目，乡来朋友间尝有见被者，其知非是则亦已矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_32_1273726_comment'></div>相知不在相奉，置人于炉炭上，非所以爱之也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_33_1273726_comment'></div>毋以惊世骇俗。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_34_1273726_comment'></div>嗣音尚尔，敬当回纳，勿讶。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_35_1273726_comment'></div>某比以莆阳荐召，虽辞不得命，今不可复去矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_36_1273726_comment'></div>尚迟报罢，专图一见，既所欲言。</div><div id='poem_sentence_37_1273726_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1170&endYear=1170')">1170年6月</a>　在毗陵。六月，刘朔卒。薛季宣有《刘复之哀辞》<div id='poem_548255' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_548255' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/548255?labeling=true' target='_blank'>刘复之哀辞</a><span class='authorDate'>（1170年6月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 南宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(31376, "南宋", "薛季宣", "poem_title_548255")'>薛季宣</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_548255_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_548255'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_548255'>天胡不仁兮，瘼此下民。<div id='poem_sentence_0_548255_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_548255'>良苦乏贤兮，贤人名去而仙。<div id='poem_sentence_1_548255_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_548255'>繄世途之好径兮，正路榛塞。<div id='poem_sentence_2_548255_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_548255'>阊阖重重有栗阶而进兮，不崇朝而折翼。<div id='poem_sentence_3_548255_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_548255'>鸱鹗司政兮，蝙蝠之晨。<div id='poem_sentence_4_548255_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_5_548255'>猿仁何咎兮，摈自王孙。<div id='poem_sentence_5_548255_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_6_548255'>宁是不畏<span class='inlineComment2'>（四库本作思）</span>兮，天实为之。<div id='poem_sentence_6_548255_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_7_548255'>皇浩浩之充天兮，岂其已而。<div id='poem_sentence_7_548255_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_8_548255'>鸿翱翔而遵逵兮，退飞者再。<div id='poem_sentence_8_548255_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_9_548255'>抟扶摇之直上兮，竟翷翩而长逝。<div id='poem_sentence_9_548255_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_10_548255'>夫岂人为兮，呼天不闻。<div id='poem_sentence_10_548255_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_11_548255'>人莫不死兮，不亡者存。<div id='poem_sentence_11_548255_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_12_548255'>小官之不卑兮，贤声载路。<div id='poem_sentence_12_548255_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_13_548255'>视彭铿其犹夭兮，后昆有裕。<div id='poem_sentence_13_548255_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_14_548255'>楙实双而一瘁兮，哀哀者母。<div id='poem_sentence_14_548255_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_15_548255'>纷孺弱之呱前兮，苍天太苦。<div id='poem_sentence_15_548255_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_16_548255'>生者作德兮，死者有仁。<div id='poem_sentence_16_548255_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_17_548255'>呜呼哀哉，家国无人非余患兮，余悲夫抱志之不伸。</div><div id='poem_sentence_17_548255_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1170&endYear=1170')">1170年8月</a>　在毗陵。作《叙焦氏易林》<div id='poem_1273777' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1273777' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1273777?labeling=true' target='_blank'>叙焦氏易林</a><span class='authorDate'>（1170年8月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 南宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(31376, "南宋", "薛季宣", "poem_title_1273777")'>薛季宣</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1273777_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1273777'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1273777'>汉焦赣《易林》十六卷，卷有四林，林六十有四繇，凡六十四卦之变四千九十有六。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1273777_comment'></div>以所传中秘书、孙氏藏书参校，中书，繇多亡佚，以孙氏书诠补圆备。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1273777_comment'></div>故书屡经传写，字多舛误，以「羊」为「缶」，以「快」为「决」，若此者众，为是正其晓然者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1273777_comment'></div>其不可知，以「喜」为「嘉」，以「鹊」为「观」，以「乌」为「鸟」，一卦两占之类，并两存之，无所去取。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1273777_comment'></div>具已刊定，可缮写。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1273777_comment'></div>汉儒传《易》，明于占候者如赣、费直、许峻、崔篆、管辂数家。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1273777_comment'></div>《易》俱有林，惟焦氏林今传于世。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1273777_comment'></div>《东观汉记》：孝明帝永平五年少雨，上御云台自卦，遇《蹇》，以《京氏易林》占之，繇曰：「蚁封穴户，天将下雨」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1273777_comment'></div>沛献王辅用体说卦，谓「蚁穴居知雨」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1273777_comment'></div>京房，延寿弟子，今书「蹇」繇实在《震》林，林为焦氏可不疑赣，延寿字也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1273777_comment'></div>其学本以六十四卦，更直日用事，以风雨寒温为候。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1273777_comment'></div>《易林》用之卜筮，尚其占与变者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1273777_comment'></div>政和间，校书郎黄伯思校中秘书，论林自林、直日灾祥自直日灾祥之法，虽同出于赣，初未尝一其用。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1273777_comment'></div>昧者弗晤，乃合而一之，于直日卦中求所得卦，谬托燕蓟士之秘。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1273777_comment'></div>本朝王佖于雍熙二年春，遇异人为筮，得《观》之《贲》，其占乃《观》中《贲》林。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1273777_comment'></div>《观》、《贲》皆白露之卦，非春所宜用，不当于《观》中求之，异人之占，固不应误，是知直日之说，非可用之占筮。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1273777_comment'></div>伯思言若简易，其实非也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1273777_comment'></div>筮法固于直日林中求所遇卦，于遇卦林中求变所之观，从初决从终，则雍熙异僧之占，初未尝与术戾。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1273777_comment'></div>僧论「一幕掀天，一同扫地」，自有得之繇林之外者，未可以一术齐也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1273777_comment'></div>直卦之法，略在汉京房、郎顗传，《天朝班历》尚取其象。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1273777_comment'></div>或者直以《周易》卦爻占数，犹屡有符效，至用林筮，颇多不合，伯思之说，未易循也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1273777_comment'></div>京氏学以卦爻分配期日，《坎》、《离》、《震》、《兑》用事，自分至之首，皆得八十分日之七十三；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1273777_comment'></div>《颐》、《晋》、《井》、《大畜》，皆五日十四分，馀皆六日七分。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1273777_comment'></div>岁既有之，日亦宜然，于直日卦中分卦直时，如日之次，日凡十卦，一时八刻三分，刻之一卦配时，有一刻二分。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1273777_comment'></div>《颐》、《晋》、《井》、《大畜》，皆五刻二分，《坎》、《离》、《震》、《兑》用事于日卦贞悔初爻之首。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1273777_comment'></div>中爻之中，皆四刻一分，是又卜数一法，不待筮而占者自可通用。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1273777_comment'></div>《易经》并论风雨阴阳占候，不必专取诸林。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1273777_comment'></div>《汉·儒林传》：孟喜受《易》于田王孙，得《易》家候阴阳灾变书，诈言田生且死时枕喜膝，独传喜。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1273777_comment'></div>同门梁丘贺疏通證明之，曰：田生绝于施雠手中。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1273777_comment'></div>时喜归东海，安得此事？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1273777_comment'></div>延寿尝从孟喜问《易》，京房以为延寿即孟氏学，翟牧、白生不肯，皆曰非也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_30_1273777_comment'></div>刘向校书，以为诸《易》学说皆祖田何、杨叔、丁将军，大谊略同，唯京氏为异党，延寿独得隐士之说，托之孟氏，不与相同。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_31_1273777_comment'></div>《<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_32_1273777", 1273777, "Clauses/132/Comments/2")'>艺文志</span>》：《易》有孟氏、京房诸篇，无复分异。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_32_1273777_comment'></div>京氏书世尚有之，虽阴阳家，不特灾变之候，论以《汉·儒林传》、《<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_33_1273777", 1273777, "Clauses/138/Comments/4")'>艺文志</span>》自有不可诬者，诸儒党同伐异，可尽信邪！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_33_1273777_comment'></div>延寿行事略在《京房传》中，举最小黄诏听留增秩矣，其曰「得我道以亡身者，京生也」，知人见事，未可以明经学士视之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_34_1273777_comment'></div>《易林》近古，占书既自可尚，缀辞引类，尤尔雅可喜。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_35_1273777_comment'></div>尚其辞者，于汉氏西京文字又可忽诸！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_36_1273777_comment'></div>略抄《卦气图法》著左，乾道六年八月丁巳鹊林书。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_37_1273777_comment'></div></div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_38_1273777'>冬至坎<span class='inlineComment2'>（上）</span>公中孚<span class='inlineComment2'>（四世）</span>辟复<span class='inlineComment2'>（十一月，初）</span>侯屯<span class='inlineComment2'>（二）</span>大夫谦<span class='inlineComment2'>（五）</span>卿睽<span class='inlineComment2'>（四）</span>公升<span class='inlineComment2'>（四）</span>辟临<span class='inlineComment2'>（十二月，二）</span>侯小过<span class='inlineComment2'>（四）</span>大夫蒙<span class='inlineComment2'>（四）</span>卿益<span class='inlineComment2'>（三）</span>公渐<span class='inlineComment2'>（三）</span>辟泰<span class='inlineComment2'>（正月，三）</span>侯需<span class='inlineComment2'>（四）</span>大夫随<span class='inlineComment2'>（三）</span>卿晋/<span class='inlineComment2'>（四）</span>春分震<span class='inlineComment2'>（上）</span>公解<span class='inlineComment2'>（二）</span>辟大壮<span class='inlineComment2'>（二月，四）</span>侯豫<span class='inlineComment2'>（初）</span>大夫讼<span class='inlineComment2'>（四）</span>卿蛊<span class='inlineComment2'>（三）</span>公革<span class='inlineComment2'>（四）</span>辟夬<span class='inlineComment2'>（三月，五）</span>侯旅<span class='inlineComment2'>（初）</span>大夫师<span class='inlineComment2'>（三）</span>卿比<span class='inlineComment2'>（三）</span>公小畜<span class='inlineComment2'>（初）</span>辟乾<span class='inlineComment2'>（四月，上）</span>侯大有<span class='inlineComment2'>（三）</span>大夫家人<span class='inlineComment2'>（二）</span>卿井<span class='inlineComment2'>（五）</span>/夏至离<span class='inlineComment2'>（上）</span>公咸<span class='inlineComment2'>（三）</span>辟姤<span class='inlineComment2'>（五月，初）</span>侯鼎<span class='inlineComment2'>（二，）</span>大夫丰<span class='inlineComment2'>（五）</span>卿涣<span class='inlineComment2'>（五）</span>公履<span class='inlineComment2'>（五）</span>辟遁<span class='inlineComment2'>（六月，二）</span>侯恒<span class='inlineComment2'>（三）</span>大夫节<span class='inlineComment2'>（初）</span>卿同人<span class='inlineComment2'>（三）</span>公损<span class='inlineComment2'>（三）</span>辟否<span class='inlineComment2'>（七月，三）</span>侯巽<span class='inlineComment2'>（上）</span>大夫萃<span class='inlineComment2'>（二）</span>卿大畜<span class='inlineComment2'>（二）</span>/秋分兑<span class='inlineComment2'>（上）</span>公贲<span class='inlineComment2'>（初）</span>辟观<span class='inlineComment2'>（八月，六）</span>侯归妹<span class='inlineComment2'>（二）</span>大夫旡妄<span class='inlineComment2'>（四）</span>卿明夷<span class='inlineComment2'>（四）</span>公困<span class='inlineComment2'>（初）</span>辟剥<span class='inlineComment2'>（九月，五）</span>侯艮<span class='inlineComment2'>（上）</span>大夫既济<span class='inlineComment2'>（三）</span>卿噬嗑<span class='inlineComment2'>（五）</span>公大过<span class='inlineComment2'>（四）</span>辟坤<span class='inlineComment2'>（十月，上）</span>侯未济<span class='inlineComment2'>（三）</span>大夫蹇<span class='inlineComment2'>（四）</span>卿颐/<span class='inlineComment2'>（四）</span>唐僧一行云：《易》孟氏章句、京房本旨、《七略》、郎顗所传卦气，皆六日七分，不以初爻相次用事。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_38_1273777_comment'></div>惟齐《天保历》依《易通统轨图》，自十有二节，五卦初爻相次用事，及上爻与中气偕终；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_39_1273777_comment'></div>又京氏减七十三分为四正之候，其说皆不经。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_40_1273777_comment'></div>据孟氏，自冬至初《中孚》用事，一月之策九六七八，是为三十卦，以地六候以天五，五六相乘，消息一变，十有二变而岁复初。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_41_1273777_comment'></div>《坎》、《震》、《离》、《兑》二十四气次主一爻，其初则二至二分也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_42_1273777_comment'></div>《易》爻当日十有二中，直全卦之初；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_43_1273777_comment'></div>十有二节，直全卦之中。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_44_1273777_comment'></div>《齐历》又以节在贞、气在悔非是。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_45_1273777_comment'></div>近世大儒司马文正推《太玄历》，邵康节谱《太玄图》，《坎》、《离》、《震》、《兑》气节直卦，皆同一行，惟以五卦初爻相次用事从《易轨》云。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_46_1273777_comment'></div>今术专本京氏，用六为法，以辟卦为局；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_47_1273777_comment'></div>六时一卦，日法以直卦为局；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_48_1273777_comment'></div>二刻一爻，《坎》、《震》、《离》、《兑》《、颐》、《晋》、《井》、《大畜》以分数除减半之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_49_1273777_comment'></div>盖三十日、三百六十时、六日、六百刻皆周，而与《易》象俱终，悔吝吉凶，亦可直以经卦世爻为断。</div><div id='poem_sentence_50_1273777_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1170&endYear=1170')">1170年</a>　在毗陵。秋，陈傅良入太学。薛季宣写信给他。作品：答君举书三。<span class='inlineComment2'>（系年作品名称为录入者据张良权点校《薛季宣集》（上海社会科学院出版社2003年版）卷二十四补。）</span><div id='poem_1273734' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1273734' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1273734?labeling=true' target='_blank'>答君举书<span style='margin: 0 0.5em'> 其二 </span></a><span class='authorDate'>（1170年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 南宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(31376, "南宋", "薛季宣", "poem_title_1273734")'>薛季宣</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1273734_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1273734'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1273734'>顷者远勤访，喜有渐磨之益。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1273734_comment'></div>事乖人欲，辄复暌违，卧病分携，宁无怏怏。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1273734_comment'></div>自被无锡由拳教札之后，杳不知车旆何之？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1273734_comment'></div>非徒怀无从修记之恨，翘跂可想知也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1273734_comment'></div>兹承就试行都，猥蒙遣信，恍若天降，慰怿如何！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1273734_comment'></div>即日秋暑乡微，伏惟客舍舂容，尊候动止万福。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1273734_comment'></div>某自作别之后，疾病相仍，幼累复然，而贱妇所苦，特异就医，役役死生，尚未可知。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1273734_comment'></div>廷陵岁又水荒，重之螟蟘、马迹，薄田既无遗种，县官科率草料，倍常赋而加多，憔悴煎熬，分为沟中之断。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1273734_comment'></div>书策相忘固已久矣，区区之迹，前此所以不欲进者，君举既知之矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1273734_comment'></div>正名之说，吾敢乎哉！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1273734_comment'></div>当路前极相知，自莆田之行，尝一得书三被催劄，而某所求以达闻听者，却不将上。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1273734_comment'></div>舅氏去国之未行也，又尝诿以专人，见问所以不来之意，喻以别议所以处我，其意诚厚，吾人去就当何如邪？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1273734_comment'></div>惜也君举已行辞命，颇伤深切，前已失之于左，今复不能得之于右，亦运而已矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1273734_comment'></div>之任请祠，足得熟议，谆谆之喻，中心不忘。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1273734_comment'></div>张、吕之贤，皆愿见而未能者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1273734_comment'></div>言称先师，要为有法；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1273734_comment'></div>理敬之说，进学之指南也，可与立者权多，不足九流之合，须得通方之士议之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1273734_comment'></div>康节固谓之：学未至武侯，武侯未可轻议；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1273734_comment'></div>考叔太真而谓之诡正道，于何而行乎？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1273734_comment'></div>立论常苦执中，有不可不察者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1273734_comment'></div>气禀言性，自是南方之学，近于功利，其又何言！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1273734_comment'></div>乡论贤人之聚，犹或可忧，真见事之谈也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1273734_comment'></div>文不逮于作者，而好诋诃前人，此最吾人大病。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1273734_comment'></div>语人要识深浅，亦欲自今勉之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1273734_comment'></div>四三哥书荷封示闽事，既难隃度，不当相讶。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1273734_comment'></div>乡来去就，尝面论之已详。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1273734_comment'></div>五三哥之云云，将有为为之尔。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1273734_comment'></div>刘复之、真显道相继云亡，真大苦事，天不相道，为善者何劝邪？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1273734_comment'></div>居厚罹忧，可与伤怆。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1273734_comment'></div>其当大事，宜必有以处之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1273734_comment'></div>洪道人学本异端，不足深论，但未知其死何自，尚当察之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_30_1273734_comment'></div>旁谱《春秋地名》固宜，恨未知见《书训》，得刊其误，尤所望者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_31_1273734_comment'></div>《国风》十二变皆有叙，小国不详其世，则附见之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_32_1273734_comment'></div>邶、魏之先，卫、唐二邦之所兼者，二南、豳国，为之先后，旨哉反古说！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_33_1273734_comment'></div>曩闻已有传本，后窜改亦不多，稿纸不精，脱烂不可将出。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_34_1273734_comment'></div>《春秋》敬纳，得与《书训》俱付象先，语以看毕蚤寻端便见还，毋令污败为祝。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_35_1273734_comment'></div>顷用《礼》学相勉，可不朝夕于斯！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_36_1273734_comment'></div>已而思之，及观张文子诏洒扫应对进退之解，异乎所谓法而不说。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_37_1273734_comment'></div>《曲礼》乡党却不如此。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_38_1273734_comment'></div>《仪礼》之记殊略，先王自有深意，虽复将亡可畏，先儒之记，要近于凿，此非笔舌可道，幸详复之可矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_39_1273734_comment'></div>《经考》漫呈一看，《八州地图》别后都不暇料理；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_40_1273734_comment'></div>《阵图》方居外匆扰，不能便为写去。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_41_1273734_comment'></div>下问车徒之阵，一车介士三甲，一为前拒，左右挟毂，矩以车徒，赤步方阵势瞭然矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_42_1273734_comment'></div>新出之图必有新意，后生可畏，未可全非而是古也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_43_1273734_comment'></div>时事日益纷扰，某尚未知存身之地，千里相望，岂不动心！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_44_1273734_comment'></div>所谓不敢因循，冀吾人共事、斯于日用，小学纯全，大体具焉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_45_1273734_comment'></div>持头觅头，佛氏能笑人矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_46_1273734_comment'></div>但能去智去故，乃可默而识之，无知不多，非欺我也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_47_1273734_comment'></div>穷迫少佳意绪，而蒙每事索报，黾勉承命，可无涯略。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_48_1273734_comment'></div>所欲言者尚不能宣之于口，千里书札乌能写方寸哉！</div><div id='poem_sentence_49_1273734_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1170&endYear=1170')">1170年</a>　在毗陵。致书杨简。作品：抵杨敬仲。<div id='poem_1273747' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1273747' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1273747?labeling=true' target='_blank'>抵杨敬仲<span class='inlineComment2'>（简）</span>书</a><span class='authorDate'>（1170年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 南宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(31376, "南宋", "薛季宣", "poem_title_1273747")'>薛季宣</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1273747_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1273747'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1273747'>某景向有年矣，侄子每自庠序归省，辄能具道问学之妙，行谊之美，及所以提诲之甚宠，顾以未尝识面为恨。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1273747_comment'></div>乡来幸会，获合并于武林，虽承教匆匆，弗及详款，拳拳之至。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1273747_comment'></div>然一面而悔吝释，接奉而群疑亡，所得固已多矣，幸甚幸甚！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1273747_comment'></div>分决之后，窃审擢荣上第，虽为宏材本分内事，然而蕴畜之富，可以次第见诸施为，未能绝意于时，尤为善类喜也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1273747_comment'></div>占贺方阻，乃蒙尺书下问，情亲意厚，愧荷兼之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1273747_comment'></div>宠谕不可晓知之言，足验天有显道义命之重，非仁贤恶所望之！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1273747_comment'></div>雨晦鸡鸣，乃今见其人矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1273747_comment'></div>世道渐迫，不尚勉旃。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1273747_comment'></div>某辱誉过，情非所当，有不知何以取此，令人愧汗。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1273747_comment'></div>因论之及，请得一言。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1273747_comment'></div>灭学以来，言行判为两途，旧矣其矫情之过者，语道乃不及事，论以「天何言哉」之意，其为不知等尔。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1273747_comment'></div>某虽不敏，于此窃有所好，而清谈脱俗之论，诚未能无恶焉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1273747_comment'></div>前此对人未尝言之，间因当路纵谈，不免加之针砭，非得已也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1273747_comment'></div>反求未为无累，惭颜厚于重甲，良工之不示人以朴，吾罪大矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1273747_comment'></div>察人伦而明庶物，几吾曹共勉之尔，不贰于物，非所敢知。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1273747_comment'></div>侨居荒僻，新除尚未知何地，何日之官？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1273747_comment'></div>有家侄便可寄声，时蒙发药是幸！</div><div id='poem_sentence_16_1273747_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1170&endYear=1170')">1170年</a>　在毗陵。致书沈焕。作品：抵沈叔晦。<div id='poem_1273748' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1273748' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1273748?labeling=true' target='_blank'>抵沈叔晦<span class='inlineComment2'>（映）</span>书</a><span class='authorDate'>（1170年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 南宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(31376, "南宋", "薛季宣", "poem_title_1273748")'>薛季宣</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1273748_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1273748'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1273748'>某侨止他州，未办旋返，陆陆亡可言者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1273748_comment'></div>窃知调尉上虞，良便仙里。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1273748_comment'></div>戍期不大远否？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1273748_comment'></div>人情咸以久次为苦，而兄承有投閒讲学之喜，漆雕子若之善，而今为兄有之，骋骐骥以御长途，知其莫之御也，甚甚善善！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1273748_comment'></div>某学问未之有见，仕本为禄，而诸公过相拂拭，出应事物之变，触目疏谬，咎皆自取，士夫望之又过，何可当也！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1273748_comment'></div>加意之诲，非甚怜爱我者，俦肯及此！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1273748_comment'></div>已事不足复为兄语，所为诚畔中道，然而拯溺救焚之计，有不暇顾拖泥烂额之患者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1273748_comment'></div>伤廉一事，宁无多馁于中，忍而不辞，无怪乎人士之纷纷也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1273748_comment'></div>强颜处此，负负何言。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1273748_comment'></div>蒙警策之，其敢不勉！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1273748_comment'></div>他有可以鞭其后者，非左右焉取哉！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1273748_comment'></div>勿鄙夷之，万万加赐为祝。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1273748_comment'></div>承谕学不躐等之说，某与家侄曾何足与知之！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1273748_comment'></div>察兄所安，端不愧斯言也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1273748_comment'></div>既蒙镌诲。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1273748_comment'></div>敢索言之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1273748_comment'></div>以某所闻于不躐等者，自明明德以至于知所止，齐家治国而天下平，其序端如贯珠，不可易也，唐氏时邕之化，盖由此作焉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1273748_comment'></div>古人以为洒埽应对进退之于圣人，道无本末之辨，中庸曲能有诚之论，岂外是邪？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1273748_comment'></div>学者眩于「诚明」、「明诚」之文，遂有殊途之见。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1273748_comment'></div>且诚之者人之道，安有不由此而能至于天之道哉？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1273748_comment'></div>今之异端，言道而不及物；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1273748_comment'></div>躬行君子，又多昧于一贯，不行之叹，圣人既知之矣，可与学者，未可适道，所以旷百世而莫之明也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1273748_comment'></div>信言果行，夫子谓之小人之事，以为礼仪威仪待人而行，道不虚行，存乎德行，不知何者为等，又将何者为躐邪？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1273748_comment'></div>必以小学、大学为之等差，则吾属异于成童，而下孟氏之欲自得之也，果何物乎？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1273748_comment'></div>某于此不敢自谓知之，然愿学焉者也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1273748_comment'></div>所识如此，未尝敢以告，人明难瞒，一掊击之幸也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1273748_comment'></div>输写以复来教，将无甚类衒鬻之为乎？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1273748_comment'></div>一眄丙之，毋重吾过！</div><div id='poem_sentence_27_1273748_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1171&endYear=1171')">1171年</a>　在毗陵。春，写信给郑伯熊。作品：与郑景望二。<div id='poem_1273729' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1273729' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1273729?labeling=true' target='_blank'>与郑景望书<span style='margin: 0 0.5em'> 其一 </span></a><span class='authorDate'>（1171年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 南宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(31376, "南宋", "薛季宣", "poem_title_1273729")'>薛季宣</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1273729_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1273729'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1273729'>自闻拜佐著作之命，尝一领教毕，并蒙递示刘复之书，似非仲举家奴台翰，恐未之得便。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1273729_comment'></div>还又拜手札，尉感良甚。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1273729_comment'></div>启沃微意，略蒙见教，多感。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1273729_comment'></div>思之，诚切时病。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1273729_comment'></div>十寒一暴，何以哉？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1273729_comment'></div>愿勿以未听而惜吾告猷之心，成所谓远者大者；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1273729_comment'></div>必不可进，乃谋鸿鹄举耳。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1273729_comment'></div>复之眷眷吾属，此意良厚。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1273729_comment'></div>某何物，滥吹竽于其间，似未之思，近于目听而耳视也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1273729_comment'></div>梦叟方在艰棘，不可得而进退，忠父已决不为赴调之计，然其才力可惜，弃之无用，有可致力，为求试县亦可，若使其人少得自见，虽未可以语通方，中道以临民，事当有实益，剸治繁剧，宁能碌碌如我辈邪？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1273729_comment'></div>祠禄彼固不屑取之，犹可与计资考，别难插手，则乞自为图之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1273729_comment'></div>岩老既熟其人，能为之前却否？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1273729_comment'></div>某告毋复寘之牙颊，必恐上累知人之明，中心岂不自知，何当诖误师友。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1273729_comment'></div>胡氏表侄，一蒙与进，不能嗣造几格，此其好善未笃，甚乖乃父所望。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1273729_comment'></div>后复相见，丐以此意语之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1273729_comment'></div>彼家甚贫，颇劳应接。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1273729_comment'></div>如有可就宾馆，得为宛转经营为幸。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1273729_comment'></div>陈颐刚比相会，云曾屡拜书，都不挥答，何故？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1273729_comment'></div>便閒望报以一二字，戒以事勿轻举，凡百宽裕沈审，必令内外无间为贵。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1273729_comment'></div>君举已罢茶院之会，见与其徒一二十辈聚课仙岩。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1273729_comment'></div>尝与之言，似乎成己工夫全未著力。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1273729_comment'></div>勉之甚相领略，此亦乐事，但未知向去如何尔？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1273729_comment'></div>下问淮壖设险之说，某知之未详。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1273729_comment'></div>《地网》所未之闻，张师言《瓦梁堰记》闻而未见。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1273729_comment'></div>然闻孙氏割据，作涂中东兴塘以淹北道；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1273729_comment'></div>南朝瓦梁城塞后湖为渊，障蔽长江，号称北海。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1273729_comment'></div>大抵淮东之地，沮泽多而丘陵少；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1273729_comment'></div>淮西山泽相半，无水隔者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1273729_comment'></div>独邾城、白沙戍入武昌，及六安、舒城走南硖二路耳。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1273729_comment'></div>古人多于川泽之地立塘鄢以遏水溉田，在孙氏时尽罢县邑，治以屯田都尉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1273729_comment'></div>魏自刘馥、邓艾之后，大田淮南，迨南北朝增饬弥皖。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_30_1273729_comment'></div>今舒州有吴陂堰<sup class='reference inlineComment2'>⑴</sup>，庐江有七门堰<span class='inlineComment2'>（刘馥断龙舒水作。）</span>，巢县有东兴塘<span class='inlineComment2'>（诸葛恪作，遏巢湖水。）</span>，滁、和州、六合间有涂塘、<sup class='reference inlineComment2'>⑵</sup>瓦梁堰<sup class='reference inlineComment2'>⑶</sup>，天长有石梁堰<sup class='reference inlineComment2'>⑷</sup>，高邮有白马塘<sup class='reference inlineComment2'>⑸</sup>，扬州有召伯埭、<sup class='reference inlineComment2'>⑹</sup>裘塘屯<span class='inlineComment2'>（齐高帝建武五年遏艾陵湖立。）</span>，楚州有石鳖塘<sup class='reference inlineComment2'>⑺</sup>、射陂、<span class='inlineComment2'>（汉旧陂。）</span>洪泽屯<sup class='reference inlineComment2'>⑻</sup>，淮阴有白水屯，盱眙有破釜塘<sup class='reference inlineComment2'>⑼</sup>，安丰有芍陂<sup class='reference inlineComment2'>⑽</sup>，固始有茹陂<span class='inlineComment2'>（刘馥作。）</span>，是皆古人屯田遏水之迹，其馀不可详记。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_31_1273729_comment'></div>大要六安以东有芍陂之险，钟离以东无非湖浊之地；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_32_1273729_comment'></div>西自皖<sup class='reference inlineComment2'>⑾</sup>，最为险要。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_33_1273729_comment'></div>然闻芍陂可以灌寿，淝水可以灌庐。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_34_1273729_comment'></div>南唐何敬洙尝复诸塘，不克而罢，其间必有利害，尚当详考。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_35_1273729_comment'></div>前闻面对及此，心知其是。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_36_1273729_comment'></div>窃思如此力量，能办如许事邪？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_37_1273729_comment'></div>如合、复之所上民兵之策，专以刺举兵权还付方镇，使之自治财用，多置水砦，以屯田民兵守之，有警得以发兵助护，如唐故事；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_38_1273729_comment'></div>民兵蠲复制度，略依陕西弓箭手法，秋田既穫，因就籴以实边，始虽暂失少少赋入，数稔之后，利当百倍于今。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_39_1273729_comment'></div>责任不专，则无可成之理。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_40_1273729_comment'></div>方今经制西蜀，以夺帅权为是，此等议论，定空言耳。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_41_1273729_comment'></div>因问之及，谩详及之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_42_1273729_comment'></div>创水虎翼军国，然似非国力所办。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_43_1273729_comment'></div>淮南民屯若就，又于松江肄习水手，为之重险，虽无水军亦得，事不难集，在乎断不断耳。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_44_1273729_comment'></div>论经总制钱减额，竟是如何？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_45_1273729_comment'></div>舅氏方在版曹，可致力否？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_46_1273729_comment'></div>立后事久不报，众甚苦之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_47_1273729_comment'></div>近乐清县括水死家田，不以葬送立后，皆欲官收，一岁州郡仿之而行。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_48_1273729_comment'></div>前日所陈，能为营使之必下否？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_49_1273729_comment'></div>官政略皆如此，无廉耻者争以𣀮敚相尚，思昨所以语刘正夫者言，今验矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_50_1273729_comment'></div>无端好与人事，亦吾人一病也。</div><div id='poem_sentence_51_1273729_comment'></div></div><div class='poemNote' id='poem_note_1273729'><div class='inline1'><div id='poem_sentence_31_1273729_0'>⑴ 朱光、吕蒙所争皖屯也。陂堰，皖水。</div></div><div class='inline1'><div id='poem_sentence_31_1273729_2'>⑵ 吴赤乌中遣兵十万断滁作塘于其上源。今梁县界至滁扬城，晋以为南梁郡，南唐于滁水上立清流关。</div></div><div class='inline1'><div id='poem_sentence_31_1273729_4'>⑶ 有东西瓦梁城。晋置秦郡，而治六合。周显德三年，南唐何延锡建言堰五十四，流不止，鱼三州氓，海四百里，其实据天经、绝地纬，功未就而罢。景德元年毁之。</div></div><div class='inline1'><div id='poem_sentence_31_1273729_0'>⑷ 源出滁州，入高邮，为樊梁溪。梁置泾州。</div></div><div class='inline1'><div id='poem_sentence_31_1273729_0'>⑸ 塘阻三何溪。谢玄破都颜、俱难，李孝逸破李敬业处。</div></div><div class='inline1'><div id='poem_sentence_31_1273729_0'>⑹ 谢安堰艾陵湖作新城在其上。</div></div><div class='inline1'><div id='poem_sentence_31_1273729_1'>⑺ 邓艾作荀羡复屯。</div></div><div class='inline1'><div id='poem_sentence_31_1273729_4'>⑻ 唐大历二年与射阳湖并置官屯。射阳湖即射陂也。</div></div><div class='inline1'><div id='poem_sentence_31_1273729_0'>⑼ 邓艾立白水塘，与破釜相连，开八水门。大业末破釜塘坏，水入淮，白水亦涸。</div></div><div class='inline1'><div id='poem_sentence_31_1273729_0'>⑽ 即孙叔敖所作期思陂，汉王景、魏刘馥、邓艾、齐桓崇祖皆脩复之，首受渒水，西道六安北界驺虞石，东自濠州之南横石，水皆入焉，灌田万顷。</div></div><div class='inline1'><div id='poem_sentence_33_1273729_0'>⑾ 东至扬则多断流为阻。故自前世征役舟师，皆出东道。如吴邗沟、魏广陵、周鹳河等，率资鄢水之利，南北所通行也。惟庐、寿一路，陆有东关、濡须、硖石之阨，重以陂水之限，东关恃东兴塘，濡须恃濡须水，硖石蔽皖。淮南有两硖石。此桐城南硖也。寿春硖石在淮水上。</div></div></div><div id='poem_note_1273729_comment'></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1171&endYear=1171')">1171年</a>　在毗陵。春，回信陈傅良。作品：答君举书。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1171&endYear=1171')">1171年</a>　在毗陵。夏，又与郑伯熊书，告知夏秋之际将趋朝赴召。作品：郑景望三。<br /></div><div class='label1' id='ea4fae91a1594e51affc616506a6bfbe_label'><a href='javascript: DetailSwitch("ea4fae91a1594e51affc616506a6bfbe");'><span id='ea4fae91a1594e51affc616506a6bfbe_link' class='switch'>—</span></a><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1171&endYear=1171')">1171年</a>，38岁</div><div id='ea4fae91a1594e51affc616506a6bfbe' class='detail'><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1171&endYear=1171')">1171年</a>　回毗陵。<br /></div>
-----end



-----title
鄂城（武昌）
-----detail
<div class='label1' id='1ad16dce718d43649b84aaeef9edc8a9_label'><a href='javascript: DetailSwitch("1ad16dce718d43649b84aaeef9edc8a9");'><span id='1ad16dce718d43649b84aaeef9edc8a9_link' class='switch'>—</span></a><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1160&endYear=1163')">1160-1163年</a>，27-30岁</div><div id='1ad16dce718d43649b84aaeef9edc8a9' class='detail'><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1160&endYear=1160')">1160年</a>　以恩荫试武昌令。时刘锜知荆南府，镇守鄂州。季宣论武昌形势，陈屯田、分戍、保伍以宽民力之策。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1160&endYear=1160')">1160年7月</a>　在武昌令任上。七月，推行保伍法。作品：喻保伍文。<div id='poem_1273619' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1273619' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1273619?labeling=true' target='_blank'>谕保伍文</a><span class='authorDate'>（1160年7月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 南宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(31376, "南宋", "薛季宣", "poem_title_1273619")'>薛季宣</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1273619_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1273619'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1273619'>惟绍兴二十有七年，盗生自鄂邑，剽杀人于昼，涂炭延于军市，民莫适莫居。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1273619_comment'></div>守侯博爱以其仁，惟死刑匪杀。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1273619_comment'></div>寇曹昌炽，爰假力于屯兵，荼毒元灵，是浮凶盗。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1273619_comment'></div>逮三十年既三祀，生肇命行鄂长，仍革新贯，政厥纪纲，始共命于泰皇，定民联于保伍。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1273619_comment'></div>井闾骇愕，惧弗溃于成。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1273619_comment'></div>惟七月，生肃众于庭，越以诚告。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1273619_comment'></div>生若曰：「乌呼有众！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1273619_comment'></div>其悃愊无哗，余誓告汝。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1273619_comment'></div>汝不闻曰：谋有小大，见有浅深。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1273619_comment'></div>厥有大谋，不愆于小见。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1273619_comment'></div>矇于浅，惟究于深。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1273619_comment'></div>人无以浅见遗深，毋以小谋大作。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1273619_comment'></div>尔罔不孝乃父母，慈乃妻孥；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1273619_comment'></div>尔有孝慈，宜其卫。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1273619_comment'></div>尔罔不安乃室家，宁乃乡闾；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1273619_comment'></div>尔有安宁，宜其卫。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1273619_comment'></div>卫之不至，惟奸宄之萌心。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1273619_comment'></div>盗贼公行，将不宁于尔室，老弗克孝，幼弗克慈，犹乡邑之沸腾。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1273619_comment'></div>矧乃在昔，先王在上，寄军赋于农田，时未有黥，师惟严惟卫。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1273619_comment'></div>今其尔卫谓之何？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1273619_comment'></div>其惊吴国之屠牛，夫岂不戒！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1273619_comment'></div>今惟我谋我见，不知其大为深，视尔不臧，既其浅小。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1273619_comment'></div>尔毋回遹，慢我大谋。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1273619_comment'></div>尔惟人乃知兵，盗何自作？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1273619_comment'></div>饬躬缮甲，惟永逸于微劳，将诲盗以慢藏，兹其可保。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1273619_comment'></div>自昔淮甸，惟寇之区，由保伍之有成，用不取遗于道，瞭然大可见，矧惟王命之从」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1273619_comment'></div>生若曰：「乌呼有众！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1273619_comment'></div>尔尚一乃志，比乃联，砺乃戈兵，敩乃击刺。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1273619_comment'></div>非徒井闾尔赖，尔惟怙众以宁家。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1273619_comment'></div>刘侯作牧于庐江，由保甲安身报国，焉知不自于来今」！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1273619_comment'></div>浃旬，民豫以成军。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_30_1273619_comment'></div>惟甲午。</div><div id='poem_sentence_31_1273619_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a
