href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1160&endYear=1160')">1160年12月</a>　在武昌令任上。十二月，州命和籴。季宣认为此举伤农，请求罢籴。并以去官相争。作品：自释赋。与赵漕书。白郡劄子。再白郡劄子。<div id='poem_1273594' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1273594' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1273594?labeling=true' target='_blank'>自释赋</a><span class='authorDate'>（1160年12月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 南宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(31376, "南宋", "薛季宣", "poem_title_1273594")'>薛季宣</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1273594_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1273594'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1273594'>太岁贞于执徐兮，涂月季惟方癸。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1273594_comment'></div>农事毕余揆其成兮，秕忼阳与襄水。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1273594_comment'></div>飞符命之坌纷兮，郡府号余曰有敕。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1273594_comment'></div>纸泉货惟四千兮，五千粳其以籴。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1273594_comment'></div>越土性而谓余求兮，郡命违其曷可？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1273594_comment'></div>蚤夜民之饲糠籺兮，又掇攘之有叵。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1273594_comment'></div>方千里而为畿甸兮，茅莩居其百九。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1273594_comment'></div>人景希兮，欲多求之孰有？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1273594_comment'></div>荪榷右而左陂兮，复前堤而后堰。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1273594_comment'></div>万斛舟兮，望悠扬而罔见。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1273594_comment'></div>苞苴昌兮，根微蠹以弗充君门。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1273594_comment'></div>狗之吠狺狺兮，圆月曀于云雾。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1273594_comment'></div>足余进而趑趄兮，矢嗫嚅之靡入。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1273594_comment'></div>思昌倘而归印绶兮，啜哀伤而雨泣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1273594_comment'></div>谓何求之喧泯浑兮，知此忧云实鲜。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1273594_comment'></div>余中切而深虑兮，羌谓之回远。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1273594_comment'></div>亶忧民于以为国兮，胡国忧为毋害。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1273594_comment'></div>敢称民而自佚兮，以求其安泰。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1273594_comment'></div>侥天命之毕罢休兮，余心之有得。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1273594_comment'></div>聊迟留兮，陈词而自释。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1273594_comment'></div></div><div id='poem_sentence_20_1273594_comment'></div></div></div><div id='poem_1273727' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1273727' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1273727?labeling=true' target='_blank'>与赵漕书</a><span class='authorDate'>（1160年12月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 南宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(31376, "南宋", "薛季宣", "poem_title_1273727")'>薛季宣</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1273727_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1273727'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1273727'>某闻一言之道，不以人之无言而废其所当言，亦不以身讷于言而默其所难言，在人之为言无所苟而已；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1273727_comment'></div>矧兹民之休戚利病结于下而弗达于上。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1273727_comment'></div>有真儒当道，宣王化以风风俗，言之者无罪，而又能救其灾，若居令之职，以身讷于言而默其所难言，废其所当言而从人之无言，使民之疾苦不得一闻于上，而求息肩于下，是亦何假于令？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1273727_comment'></div>为之令者不亦名教之罪人乎？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1273727_comment'></div>斯某所以窃不自量，而敢言于执事者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1273727_comment'></div>湖右疮痍甚矣，武昌又其甚者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1273727_comment'></div>遗民千户，非流移转徙，则兵荒盗贼之馀，偷生一时，鲜知本业。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1273727_comment'></div>田莱不辟，何财之聚？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1273727_comment'></div>旱乾水溢之患仍岁有之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1273727_comment'></div>令失职而行者踵相接于途，知安集劳来以称明天子之德意者，兹邑所罕见。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1273727_comment'></div>比年戍兵屡勤，蹂践弗堪，重以大治战船，作屯营于二千里之外，耕男远役，红女下机，二稔于兹，不少休息。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1273727_comment'></div>而又鼠偷侵寇，生发不时，居草莽间、无聊生者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1273727_comment'></div>民羸若此，为邑奈何？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1273727_comment'></div>礼法政刑，所不暇及。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1273727_comment'></div>某嵬琐之质，于民事本非所长，方此效官，敢不自尽。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1273727_comment'></div>而当凋弊窘急之次，束于简书；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1273727_comment'></div>抚字之心，废为残暴；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1273727_comment'></div>礼德之道，迁为苛虐。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1273727_comment'></div>民失依赖，夫奚告哉？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1273727_comment'></div>兹幸自天，恭遇某官执事以忧民之心，副裕民之寄；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1273727_comment'></div>施不忍人之政，充博爱之仁。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1273727_comment'></div>弭节之初，究求民瘼，归仁美德，谅人皆有之，告病以民，恐未有陈于执事之前者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1273727_comment'></div>虽执事之贤，下车伊始，民之困弊，何自得焉？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1273727_comment'></div>可以言而不言，某惧不自逃于咎，不敢自默，废所当言，惟执事推爱物之心，为民深虑，药其彫瘵，使之休息，固执事爱人之实，非有待于猥吏之言。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1273727_comment'></div>至于自快其私，取容于上，攘人之大利，以给公家之小利，存人臣之小节，而忘其大节，是近时浅丈夫之所为事，在某非敢为，亦不敢烦执事者之虑。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1273727_comment'></div>瞽言冒进，惟执事幸察其心！</div><div id='poem_sentence_25_1273727_comment'></div></div></div><div id='poem_1273626' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1273626' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1273626?labeling=true' target='_blank'>再白郡劄子</a><span class='authorDate'>（1160年12月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 南宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(31376, "南宋", "薛季宣", "poem_title_1273626")'>薛季宣</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1273626_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1273626'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1273626'>某十五日以心气惝恍，不计僭差，狂率有请，日虞何谴之至，俯伏以俟。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1273626_comment'></div>今数日矣，迄未蒙府之报命，岂眷怜素厚，而难其请邪？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1273626_comment'></div>将以为诈而不足听邪？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1273626_comment'></div>某之所以朝夕狂悸，而不避再三之渎也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1273626_comment'></div>伏念某赋才谫薄，仕宦固非本心，始欲一试所闻，庶几少有所济，力微而废，谓之何哉！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1273626_comment'></div>诚非敢犯台严，亦非干百姓之誉，一身之计，端有在焉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1273626_comment'></div>盖某爰自之官，非惟身自废学，一儿一侄，皆失从师。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1273626_comment'></div>眷先人之遗书，久贮箱箧，郁蒸蟫鼠之患，惟日忧之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1273626_comment'></div>矧樗散之姿，雅多闲放，读书之外，问不及家。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1273626_comment'></div>托庇于兹，遂有官守之责，事亡巨细，不敢不尽其诚。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1273626_comment'></div>以此劳心，殆成糜溃。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1273626_comment'></div>屯营之役一起，归思乳柑政黄，不能自已。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1273626_comment'></div>以《周易》筮，遇《遁》之《旅》，以为此意可以质诸天地神明，故断之不疑，请辞而去。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1273626_comment'></div>亦尝妄有所作，不敢冒昧投陈，而此及之，丐察其非诈耳。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1273626_comment'></div>窃念某故乡尚远，贫乏为甚，坐食于外，饥寒且将及之，如蒙蚤赐备申，得遂其志，啜菽饮水，皆执事之赐也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1273626_comment'></div>云云。</div><div id='poem_sentence_15_1273626_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1160&endYear=1160')">1160年</a>　在武昌令任上。作文多篇。作品：弦歌堂记。松风阁记。新作殊亭记。诚台记。寒溪堂记。胜亭记。正己堂记。艮止亭记。梅庑记。<div id='poem_1273841' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1273841' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1273841?labeling=true' target='_blank'>弦歌堂记</a><span class='authorDate'>（1160年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 南宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(31376, "南宋", "薛季宣", "poem_title_1273841")'>薛季宣</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1273841_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1273841'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1273841'>狂生之治武昌，有堂以休其燕处，命之曰「弦歌」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1273841_comment'></div>或徇其名，以丝声问者曰：「吾不识操缦，安知琴瑟」？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1273841_comment'></div>「然则永言将何若」？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1273841_comment'></div>曰：「吾不分清浊，安知声调」？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1273841_comment'></div>「是则此堂何以」？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1273841_comment'></div>曰：「以临官」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1273841_comment'></div>「临官古之道与」？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1273841_comment'></div>曰：「吾不知其今古，居斯可得矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1273841_comment'></div>居而视其实，则其邑之所为设，无非世俗之政，胥徒皂隶充乎闼，傅别质剂盈乎前，条教在门，赋财在帑，所听者狱讼，所闻者催科，汩汩营营，无或弦歌之事」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1273841_comment'></div>或者愀然不悦曰：「异哉！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1273841_comment'></div>子之政，斯亦妄人而已矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1273841_comment'></div>虽然，犹有说也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1273841_comment'></div>之子曾不是闻乎？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1273841_comment'></div>太古之治，有乐而无声，琴而无弦者，以身为器，以心为律，建之以太极，制之以中和，翕而作之，皦而纯之，绎而成之，八音克谐，律吕斯应，动天地，感鬼神，有生之类无不获者矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1273841_comment'></div>夫如是也，弦歌之事可得而略也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1273841_comment'></div>中古患不得乎此，于是乎有《乐经》之教，中和以节其内，音律以宣其外，弄之以器，听之以声，琴以禁之，歌以讹之，非辟之心，无自而入矣，仁民而爱物，未有学非是道者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1273841_comment'></div>今子上无得乎彼，而又此之略，疲精神于刑政，不求诸内而于簿书期会之间役役焉，谓其堂曰『弦歌』，吾不知之矣」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1273841_comment'></div>狂生曰：「吾过矣！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1273841_comment'></div>吾过矣！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1273841_comment'></div>所求于太古之道，则吾未能也；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1273841_comment'></div>中古之事，吾何足与闻之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1273841_comment'></div>苟居今之世，不变今之俗，诚其意，正其身，爱其民，律其吏，明其期会，察其簿书，谨其货财，时其徭役。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1273841_comment'></div>上无沈蠹之失，下无非横之征。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1273841_comment'></div>无情者不得尽其辞，穷民为有所赴愬。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1273841_comment'></div>耕而食，织而衣，用不犯于有司。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1273841_comment'></div>礼义兴行于下，四封之内，民吏各安其所居，一堂之上而民弗吾罪。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1273841_comment'></div>仰不愧，俯不怍，忧不患乎失职。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1273841_comment'></div>则弦歌之事，其或庶几乎。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1273841_comment'></div>若夫兴礼乐、制田赋、一风教、致和平，吾无事焉，有天子之职官在。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1273841_comment'></div>所求于太古之道，吾未能也，中古之事，则吾岂敢！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1273841_comment'></div>吾过矣！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_30_1273841_comment'></div>吾过矣」！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_31_1273841_comment'></div>由书为之堂记。</div><div id='poem_sentence_32_1273841_comment'></div></div></div><div id='poem_1273842' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1273842' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1273842?labeling=true' target='_blank'>松风阁记</a><span class='authorDate'>（1160年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 南宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(31376, "南宋", "薛季宣", "poem_title_1273842")'>薛季宣</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1273842_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1273842'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1273842'>郊坛冈阴郎亭之麓，精庐左阙，松风之故阁在焉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1273842_comment'></div>初，涪翁复自巴中，访坡公之逸迹，裴徊九曲，信宿松下，啸歌成韵，因风名阁。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1273842_comment'></div>阁磐箬谷，俯寒溪，临洗敛之渊，睨万松之岭。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1273842_comment'></div>江山浩渺，吞吐风云，引领而东，缥缈万象，故虽空谷之内，远瞻无不届焉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1273842_comment'></div>西山多奇，此景为最。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1273842_comment'></div>日者松林茂密，中烬于劫灰，松风之名，犹以人著。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1273842_comment'></div>主僧作新轩槛，请走记而题之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1273842_comment'></div>惟翁学行文章，固已播人耳目，颂述其事，非所敢为，聊叙阁之废兴，与其得名所自。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1273842_comment'></div>登斯阁者，咏涪翁之句，眄西山之景，指顾斯得，自应不改其旧，召棠孔柏，曾何剪伐之有哉！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1273842_comment'></div>松风飕飗，当蓬然起矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1273842_comment'></div>夫然，则苍髯之木，安在乎阁之成坏？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1273842_comment'></div>信能种松木万本，来万壑之清风，追旧观于来今，亦西山一胜事也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1273842_comment'></div>好古博雅之君子，将有意于斯文。</div><div id='poem_sentence_12_1273842_comment'></div></div></div><div id='poem_1273843' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1273843' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1273843?labeling=true' target='_blank'>新作殊亭记</a><span class='authorDate'>（1160年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 南宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(31376, "南宋", "薛季宣", "poem_title_1273843")'>薛季宣</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1273843_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1273843'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1273843'>武昌之西，郎亭之首，有亭岿然而高，超然而迥者，县大夫孟士元之殊亭也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1273843_comment'></div>士元为令武昌，才兼政迹，作亭殊异，有聱叟之漫记焉，唐之刻文磨于俗令。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1273843_comment'></div>亭高记古，同永空山，其所以为不亡者，抑有其道。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1273843_comment'></div>武昌古都也，游观之迹往往而在，山川秀异，触处皆有。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1273843_comment'></div>走初易殊亭之迩，未之尝问，泛然一投足。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1273843_comment'></div>虽湖山江沔顾见古人，俛首内观，则亦有未能见殊于世者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1273843_comment'></div>尝谓为政法古，犹宜继古人之志。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1273843_comment'></div>当其事任，漫不加理，使奇人旧迹堙没自我，其政为可知矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1273843_comment'></div>庾公南楼，犹虚成于江鄂之郡，殊亭伟观，故不可堙诸草莽也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1273843_comment'></div>以亭居涧饮寺后，爰命主僧作而新之，斥广旧基，粗为宽大。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1273843_comment'></div>建以九月甲子，以十月甲子落之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1273843_comment'></div>聊记载其岁时，用见废兴之自，至山川之殊状，游眺之殊极，则次山之记在。</div><div id='poem_sentence_11_1273843_comment'></div></div></div><div id='poem_1273844' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1273844' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1273844?labeling=true' target='_blank'>诚台记</a><span class='authorDate'>（1160年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 南宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(31376, "南宋", "薛季宣", "poem_title_1273844")'>薛季宣</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1273844_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1273844'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1273844'>武昌牙堂之后架，有隙地数亩，自更世俶扰，废为污莱，虫蛇糜鹿之与居，莫有一顾睇者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1273844_comment'></div>走尸县数月，始命疏而辟之，树之以修篁焉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1273844_comment'></div>诛茅薙草，恍若有得。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1273844_comment'></div>邑堧之下，披陇如台，矗然天成，不畚不筑。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1273844_comment'></div>下顾城邑居掌鞅间，林山苍苍，环绕三面，青葱醮碧，非图画可拟，寒溪辟暑之台殿，累累然堕吾目中，真吴楚之奇观也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1273844_comment'></div>武昌鄂故地，在魏为吴孙氏别都，东晋为江州刺史治，有隋徙郡而县。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1273844_comment'></div>英豪隽伟之士居是邦者，不知其几人也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1273844_comment'></div>以仲谋之雄杰，元规之清尚，次山之文翰，而犹无得于此，予何人哉，于斯有见，则天之所赋于我者不薄矣，可不敬之！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1273844_comment'></div>记曰：诚者，自成也，而道，自道也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1273844_comment'></div>故夫斯台之作，岂人为哉！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1273844_comment'></div>命之曰「诚台」焉，明自成之义也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1273844_comment'></div>其铭曰：</div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_11_1273844'>淩云已颓，严濑殊贞。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1273844_comment'></div>如何此台，天乎自成！</div><div id='poem_sentence_12_1273844_comment'></div></div></div><div id='poem_1273845' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1273845' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1273845?labeling=true' target='_blank'>寒溪堂记</a><span class='authorDate'>（1160年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 南宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(31376, "南宋", "薛季宣", "poem_title_1273845")'>薛季宣</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1273845_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1273845'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1273845'>寒溪堂旧址，在今堂西北二十步之路隅，面莽依山，环为墙壁，草茅翳塞，仅给将迎，游衍登临，盖无足尚。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1273845_comment'></div>走到官之始，亭朽而颠，会要之途，送迎无所，于是鸠工命役，更作新亭。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1273845_comment'></div>以为寒溪之名为斯邑望，而堂不称，不亦虚乎！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1273845_comment'></div>乃从主簿亳黄君邦俊、尉番阳王君楠躬行相宅，踪步溪干，旋反求之，得堂基于高冈之上，火茅杀竹，不筑而成。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1273845_comment'></div>东望崇丘，逶逦相属，嵚崟岭岫，耸翠周遭，避暑之宫，九曲之岭，高低隐显，如点缀其西南，江水重湖，西北时见。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1273845_comment'></div>寒溪在下，樊山处西，肇建此堂，适当其会。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1273845_comment'></div>四周曲槛，不设门墉，制矩从中，弗侈弗陋。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1273845_comment'></div>劳来送往，眺望遨游，凡今之人，惟意所适。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1273845_comment'></div>盖已西则就下，秋夏或沦于水，稍北有地可辟，春冬取道又迂，则夫斯堂之为基，后来当不可易。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1273845_comment'></div>赠行折柳，雨雪来思，如得其人，安知不为它日武昌一胜赏也！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1273845_comment'></div>绍兴上章执徐岁孟余之月记。</div><div id='poem_sentence_10_1273845_comment'></div></div></div><div id='poem_1273846' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1273846' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1273846?labeling=true' target='_blank'>胜亭记</a><span class='authorDate'>（1160年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 南宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(31376, "南宋", "薛季宣", "poem_title_1273846")'>薛季宣</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1273846_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1273846'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1273846'>江出岷山，沿流束于三峡，放于云梦之泽，吞洞庭之水，纳湘沔而东之，至樊山而少折。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1273846_comment'></div>樊山之趾，得古鄂城，为吴孙氏之故都。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1273846_comment'></div>其地前左水泽，右背山陵，青嶂澄流，映带环合，如屏如画，触处清阴，荆山而南一奇观也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1273846_comment'></div>由县而北，有亭峙于冈阜，不知谁何氏所作，世目之以胜亭焉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1273846_comment'></div>游武昌者入境而改视，入邑而改观，其山川之秀丽，原田之沃衍，固已甲于荆楚，或不可以名状，至于登胜亭，穷远境，观江流之汗漫，望淮甸之平夷，右西塞而左东坡，泛中原而涵大泽。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1273846_comment'></div>淮山如拱，蹲踞参差，郎岑西来，重冈数叠。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1273846_comment'></div>龙蟠酾水，声如佩环，旦夜阴晴，云霞万状。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1273846_comment'></div>自冬徂暑，葭苇黄苍，雪月之明光，景物之变见，纷纷扰扰，有不可得而齐者，内观其邑，已觉天壤之为间，天下江山之胜，其孰能尚之！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1273846_comment'></div>走始欲更其名而不可，闻摄令程鹏举尝请书于杨退翁运属，于是取榜悬之，且为之记。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1273846_comment'></div>昔孔子登东山而小鲁，登泰山而小天下，游胜亭者，不几于是乎！</div><div id='poem_sentence_9_1273846_comment'></div></div></div><div id='poem_1273847' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1273847' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1273847?labeling=true' target='_blank'>正己堂记</a><span class='authorDate'>（1160年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 南宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(31376, "南宋", "薛季宣", "poem_title_1273847")'>薛季宣</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1273847_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1273847'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1273847'>诚台以北，得射圃之旧地，带江面岭，据冈阜而极坦夷，真武昌之形胜也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1273847_comment'></div>自中兴偃武彻备，诸城汩没苞萧，非复往意。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1273847_comment'></div>乃绍兴己卯，诏书阅弓兵武事，于是邑尉番阳董君经之营之，番阳王君踵而成之，张设射侯，创新堂陛。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1273847_comment'></div>适走行保伍之政，因命同僚落焉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1273847_comment'></div>王君为堂请名，走命之曰「正己」，以为大人正己而物正，射法于是乎取。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1273847_comment'></div>故正己而后发，失诸正鹄则反求诸己。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1273847_comment'></div>至于升降步武，揖逊威仪，一本诸躬，用能不争。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1273847_comment'></div>古之观德者以是，厥有旨哉！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1273847_comment'></div>孔子曰：「吾何执，执御乎？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1273847_comment'></div>执射乎？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1273847_comment'></div>吾执御矣」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1273847_comment'></div>是则射御之旨，艺宁足以周之！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1273847_comment'></div>古者寓兵于农，非徒教战而已，射御之法，使人知之，知正己以成身，则天下无事矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1273847_comment'></div>武昌当天下孔道，南邻大冶、豫章，北而申、蔡、蕲、黄，为奸人盗贼之渊薮，有文事者必有武备，今亦阔矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1273847_comment'></div>王君与走之为此，盖将发政于弓兵，联保伍之民，游于此，学于此，阅习于此，以自成于此，由正己而格物，其庶矣哉！</div><div id='poem_sentence_14_1273847_comment'></div></div></div><div id='poem_1273848' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1273848' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1273848?labeling=true' target='_blank'>艮止亭记</a><span class='authorDate'>（1160年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 南宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(31376, "南宋", "薛季宣", "poem_title_1273848")'>薛季宣</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1273848_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1273848'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1273848'>《说卦》：「艮为山为门」，取象不同，同归于止，故曰：艮，止也，万物之所成终而成始也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1273848_comment'></div>是以大学之道，在止于至善。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1273848_comment'></div>禹曰：「安汝止」、「惟动丕应」、「徯志」，止之为义亦大矣！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1273848_comment'></div>天不止则不清，地不止则不宁，人不止则不行，物不止则不成，天地万物必有止而后诚也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1273848_comment'></div>知止斯静，静斯安，安斯应，安身应物，万世不易之道，其惟止之云乎！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1273848_comment'></div>法像门山，不几于是？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1273848_comment'></div>鄂，岩邑也，枕山而县郎亭。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1273848_comment'></div>樊阜西南而来，西北而止，重冈复磴，曲折委蛇，自下而高，不知其几叠也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1273848_comment'></div>翔飞之势，萃于牙庭，止于诚台之所，旧通径路，为之闬，曰「山门」，下直诚台，趣乎射圃，徘徊转眄无限，青山修竹，苍苍映带。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1273848_comment'></div>官柳废而不治，茅茨塞矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1273848_comment'></div>走为危亭四础，弗侈弗庳，小径依然，其门不改，周遭设槛，以适登临。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1273848_comment'></div>即之可以关去来、闭出入，居之可以极游眺、共赋歌。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1273848_comment'></div>景物风光，今后庭之极止也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1273848_comment'></div>中外有适，何莫由斯！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1273848_comment'></div>惟天地万物之生成，未始非出入于《艮》，邦畿千里，固惟民之所止也，县成天子始终之政，可不知其止乎！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1273848_comment'></div>乩经卦而命之名，故亭名曰「艮止」，庶几厚终于敦艮，不为外物而迁，抑止躬之谊也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1273848_comment'></div>后之君子，信能不改斯度以观象乎？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1273848_comment'></div>兼山动静，惟时思止其位，用光明于是道，不亦善乎！</div><div id='poem_sentence_17_1273848_comment'></div></div></div><div id='poem_1273849' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1273849' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1273849?labeling=true' target='_blank'>梅庑记</a><span class='authorDate'>（1160年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 南宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(31376, "南宋", "薛季宣", "poem_title_1273849")'>薛季宣</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1273849_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1273849'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1273849'>武昌尉寺旧无憩息之地，退食之次，燕伸无所。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1273849_comment'></div>番阳王彦材作尉此邑，始即其堂之中庑，少加葺垩，辟其夹砌，树梅焉，命之曰「梅轩」，以便安其退省，而请记于走，曰：「梅，嘉果也，吾取其实，珍其味；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1273849_comment'></div>其花芳洁雅淡，吾高其致，裛其馨香，故名。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1273849_comment'></div>尉之德称者，宜莫若梅子真，吾慕其为人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1273849_comment'></div>楠，吾名也，又梅之别。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1273849_comment'></div>则夫花树之植吾庭砌者，惟梅为宜，名轩以梅，其谁曰不可」！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1273849_comment'></div>走曰：「公言得矣，而未之尽也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1273849_comment'></div>夫梅之为物，非其果之尚也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1273849_comment'></div>穷冬凛寒，怒风号雪，凋零百物，竹柏犹瘁，此木之常也，而梅花于是，则其操为可称也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1273849_comment'></div>芳香婀娜，斗䌽淩霞，以艳相高，以荂相轧，此花之态也，而梅幽香洁白之为素，则其德为可贵也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1273849_comment'></div>木无不实，无实于果，甘酸异味，适口一时，此果之材也，而梅有鼎羹之和，则其用为可重也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1273849_comment'></div>德纯而不贰，恬素而弗矜，四时一是，华实相当，古之人有合于是、见览于后者，非子真而谁欤？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1273849_comment'></div>斯焉取斯，公比德于是矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1273849_comment'></div>斯廊也而谓之轩，斯名之未正，正名『梅庑』，昭示后人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1273849_comment'></div>与公临庑之梅，名德俱称，茇居剪伐之戒，非甘棠比矣」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1273849_comment'></div>彦材唯唯，因书榜而为之记。</div><div id='poem_sentence_15_1273849_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1161&endYear=1161')">1161年</a>　在武昌令任上。春，作《哀白鹇赋》<div id='poem_1273600' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1273600' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1273600?labeling=true' target='_blank'>哀白鹇赋</a><span class='authorDate'>（1161年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 南宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(31376, "南宋", "薛季宣", "poem_title_1273600")'>薛季宣</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1273600_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1273600'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1273600'>辛巳春，武昌酒官修岁事，植秋千于次，有鹇西飞，触之以死，为恻然赋之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1273600_comment'></div></div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_1273600'>哀白鹇之贞特，亦性天于纯德。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1273600_comment'></div>冠蓉砂之峨峨，素涛翻兮有服。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1273600_comment'></div>林樾居兮幽绝，行有常兮时出。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1273600_comment'></div>不鸡仰乎刍豢，雉有惭其高洁。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1273600_comment'></div>岁曰改兮王春，百卉芳兮物新。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1273600_comment'></div>藏浅草之亡几，而奚为乎迩人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1273600_comment'></div>伤人乐之及时，仙半戏兮轻飞。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1273600_comment'></div>鞦韆建兮蹴蹙，聊翱翔兮嬉嬉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1273600_comment'></div>有来者鹇，自彼荒苑。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1273600_comment'></div>疾溯风而西翥，昧人为之辗转。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1273600_comment'></div>惟奋焉之靡顾，触会遭其东柱。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1273600_comment'></div>碎緌首于倏忽，飙而舞羽。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1273600_comment'></div>有飘有零，涣血流缨。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1273600_comment'></div>降离龙之无首，霞烁雾兮丹翎。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1273600_comment'></div>神不及知，声不及举，俄而毙焉，曷其有所！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1273600_comment'></div>我心恻其生远，过城市而非宜。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1273600_comment'></div>昧有进而弗视，飞灾是以罹之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1273600_comment'></div>信始安其故处，羌高飞而远举。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1273600_comment'></div>矰弋纵其何施，寄哀思兮鄙语。</div><div id='poem_sentence_19_1273600_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1161&endYear=1161')">1161年5月</a>　在武昌令任上。五月，朝廷下令屯田。季宣致书鄂守宋似孙，论屯田利害。作品：与宋守论屯田利害。<div id='poem_1273694' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1273694' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1273694?labeling=true' target='_blank'>与宋守论屯田利害</a><span class='authorDate'>（1161年5月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 南宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(31376, "南宋", "薛季宣", "poem_title_1273694")'>薛季宣</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1273694_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1273694'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1273694'>某准牒备奉朝旨措置屯田事宜。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1273694_comment'></div>县令卑官，固论议所不及，咨询所不到，惟当遵禀成算，以即事功，不当可否其间，上评国论。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1273694_comment'></div>然而愚者千虑，小已未能一得。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1273694_comment'></div>思欲退就循默，则恐利少害多，无补公私，失箴规官守之意，内愧无益，不若言而不用，故敢辄以小见仰进一言。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1273694_comment'></div>窃意议者之及于屯田，盖知其一而不知其二，睹其利而未睹其害，是故及此言也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1273694_comment'></div>今夫国家之务，莫重于军食。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1273694_comment'></div>飞刍挽粟，率百户而奉一军。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1273694_comment'></div>散军就田，所耕足以赡众，军无惰卒，国无劳民；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1273694_comment'></div>此历古屯田之利，赵充国、诸葛亮之所赖以成功者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1273694_comment'></div>至于彍骑、民兵之辨，则恐议者有所未达。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1273694_comment'></div>且亮、充国所将之卒，类皆调之于民，使民就田，何所不可。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1273694_comment'></div>彍骑则四方游手，不堪田亩之事，侥求逸便，是以从军，习击刺于射场，尚苦其事，驱之畎亩，虑非所长。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1273694_comment'></div>获利而共享之，彼将犹有所惮，专有其利，必非乐为。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1273694_comment'></div>贱吏家居，尝识田里之故，上农数口，妇子毕耕，不能数十亩田，力犹不足，一卒营五十亩，其何以堪？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1273694_comment'></div>且古之所以屯田，多缘宿兵塞上，饟馈不给，姑即弃地耕之，所求便事宽民，非以为利，不过自足军用，省馈运之劳，不闻悉使之耕，倍为程督。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1273694_comment'></div>使能垦地如许，宁能弃乡井而隶籍于军？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1273694_comment'></div>又况国之屯田，本缘捍御关隘，今求辟地，利不两全。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1273694_comment'></div>自然扼塞，无田可耕，固非要害。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1273694_comment'></div>散之则不可复聚，聚之则奔命徒劳，一往于田，不可复教，积年阅习，一日废之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1273694_comment'></div>流移之民，仅能复业，良田便于水利，固己耕耨于中，环以屯田，宁不争利？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1273694_comment'></div>便民则军无可耕之地，扰之则民必流亡。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1273694_comment'></div>在今少少营田，其害已见，侵渔豪夺之事，无日无之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1273694_comment'></div>重以屯田，民有流移而已。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1273694_comment'></div>况本县介居大冶，乌能强挽之？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1273694_comment'></div>留屯田之兵，其患有不可胜言者，跂立而待，尚或见之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1273694_comment'></div>言利之臣，恐未尝过计及此。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1273694_comment'></div>第观汉蜀用之以济，思不及于萧铣；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1273694_comment'></div>南唐墨守一隅，未知其可也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1273694_comment'></div>先伯考之经略湖外，实代王彦守边，闻彦使二十将卒营田，溃者十有八将。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1273694_comment'></div>兹某耳目之所接，惟执事明处而熟图之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1273694_comment'></div>堂下之言，未足深过。</div><div id='poem_sentence_30_1273694_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1161&endYear=1161')">1161年6月</a>　在武昌令任上。六月，御史中丞汪澈为湖北、京西宣谕使。时宋金关系紧张，金海陵王完颜亮正筹划南侵。季宣多次上书汪澈，论内政与边事。作品：上宣谕汪中丞书。论民力。论盗贼。论营田。<div id='poem_1273695' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1273695' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1273695?labeling=true' target='_blank'>上宣谕汪中丞书</a><span class='authorDate'>（1161年6月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 南宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(31376, "南宋", "薛季宣", "poem_title_1273695")'>薛季宣</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1273695_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1273695'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1273695'>某闻强国以人，作人以气，士气振而众材用。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1273695_comment'></div>君子乐得其道，小人乐得其利，雄杰狙诈皆得而用，则其国家靡不振。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1273695_comment'></div>不然反是，明哲保身而已，所与为国，非小人而谁哉？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1273695_comment'></div>自非上知之人，安有不化？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1273695_comment'></div>理乱之判，由此而决。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1273695_comment'></div>国家承祖宗积累之厚，教化之美，涵养士气，作成人材，嘉祐、元祐之间，名士辈出，一时之盛，可以追配唐虞，唐、汉以还，未足伦拟。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1273695_comment'></div>党锢之过，贤知放逐；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1273695_comment'></div>趋时之士，媕婀相竞。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1273695_comment'></div>二宫播越，职此之由。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1273695_comment'></div>绍兴始元，皇上恢祖宗之略，士气稍奋，江东以兴，权臣柄朝，媢贤丑正，岳侯之死，世绝功名之望，赵、张之放，人莫敢有贤德。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1273695_comment'></div>四方士气，至于今索然。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1273695_comment'></div>今日朝廷，视祖宗为何似？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1273695_comment'></div>是知士气振者国必盛，士气索则人心亦从而衰。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1273695_comment'></div>其谁为之？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1273695_comment'></div>在时政之所行已尔。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1273695_comment'></div>今天下文武之士，知气节者谁欤？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1273695_comment'></div>居官以谠正为村，刚方谓之暴露；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1273695_comment'></div>脂韦循默，以为官样得体；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1273695_comment'></div>贪婪狠愎，世且才之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1273695_comment'></div>天下滔滔，安于邪行，诬蒙苟且，上下相承，郡县朝堂，会为一律。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1273695_comment'></div>论至于此，而求士气之振，邦家之兴，不戛乎难哉！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1273695_comment'></div>卒有意外之虞，士安所习，孰肯寘其官体，仿其村暴，捐躯效命，以为社稷之卫，易其妻子、禄位、素心之所保乎？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1273695_comment'></div>纵有斯志，其中无有，徒为强死，何补于事？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1273695_comment'></div>夫为待敌之计，所务乎盛气而已。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1273695_comment'></div>求盛而不作，日为循缩之计，气不振，下将愒然而休，以图恢复之功，固未知其或可也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1273695_comment'></div>执事以名德系人望，以忠信结主知，综辖台纲，大明国论，朝廷为之一正，奸回为之胆落。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1273695_comment'></div>今持节以护诸将，真裴度征淮西举也，中兴圣业，当由此致。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1273695_comment'></div>而区区之所为执事虑者，不在乎敌之强大，而患吾气之犹索也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1273695_comment'></div>执事居今之世，行古之道，施诸首政，必也动人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1273695_comment'></div>邪正昭明，会与前反，气无有不振，人无有不奋，则功何有不就？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1273695_comment'></div>是执事所优为者，端不俟小夫之论。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_30_1273695_comment'></div>至于朝廷公辅，未闻庙胜之略，边鄙之将，或恐长城斯坏，士卒云惰，民久告劳，风化所行，人无一怀固志者，以求免复之效，是由斗而身尪，刖而争途，岂直不能，且速败而成偾。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_31_1273695_comment'></div>振而起之，莫如自进道途之论，谓旦暮且将有豳岐之举。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_32_1273695_comment'></div>士气骫骳，御侮其谁？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_33_1273695_comment'></div>行留之间，何所不有？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_34_1273695_comment'></div>公卿弗救，争臣弗言，杞人之忧，宁得不过。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_35_1273695_comment'></div>绳愆纠缪，真执事之事也，弛张国势，系于一言。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_36_1273695_comment'></div>谠论回天，士气增壮，人人有乡功之志，则贤者不敢隐其智，勇者不敢爱其力，太平可指日而俟，夫何有于寇雠。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_37_1273695_comment'></div>康、宣中兴之臣，盖用此道。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_38_1273695_comment'></div>今身任天下之重，非执事其谁宜为？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_39_1273695_comment'></div>惟执事奋其精忠，以身为天下倡始，则士气亦从而靡，安有不亡之寇！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_40_1273695_comment'></div>此先务也，惟执事急焉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_41_1273695_comment'></div>某位卑言高，死罪死罪！</div><div id='poem_sentence_42_1273695_comment'></div></div></div><div id='poem_1273697' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1273697' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1273697?labeling=true' target='_blank'>论民力书</a><span class='authorDate'>（1161年6月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 南宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(31376, "南宋", "薛季宣", "poem_title_1273697")'>薛季宣</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1273697_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1273697'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1273697'>某鲰生晚进，安知国体！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1273697_comment'></div>然尝侍诸父官守，得接士夫馀论。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1273697_comment'></div>窃闻民惟邦本，本固邦宁，为国劳民，未有能固其国者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1273697_comment'></div>今兹假令东鄂，获亲民事。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1273697_comment'></div>到任之始，适当多事之秋，窃禄旷官，仅能书考可以。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1273697_comment'></div>羸民千有馀户，当兵荒水旱之馀，大治战船，治屯营于荆渚，林木尽伐，役且馀年，上溯江流，将二千里。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1273697_comment'></div>方幸少休数月，民获治其私家，俄被军书，夏口有屯营之役。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1273697_comment'></div>基巩未立，旋令迎候大军，奔命疲劳，不胜其弊。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1273697_comment'></div>不知继此之后，果然奈何？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1273697_comment'></div>湖右之民，况又非浙江比。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1273697_comment'></div>一钱粒粟，即名税户，尚不供仰食俯育之费，何有于官？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1273697_comment'></div>比年以来，虚乏甚矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1273697_comment'></div>谓朝廷待敌之计，莫若爱抚边民，使其民愿为我氓，安有不济。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1273697_comment'></div>今日之事，反为先困边民，困而流离，何所不至。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1273697_comment'></div>昔南唐以屯田之役侵扰淮南，周师南征，民或负刍迎奉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1273697_comment'></div>今之科扰，有甚屯田。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1273697_comment'></div>愚瞽之心，未知其可。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1273697_comment'></div>惟某官至诚体国，循问重湖，荆襄之民，引领以承德意。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1273697_comment'></div>嘉谟启沃，莫急告劳，冒献瞽言，惟所裁择。</div><div id='poem_sentence_18_1273697_comment'></div></div></div><div id='poem_1273673' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1273673' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1273673?labeling=true' target='_blank'>论营田劄</a><span class='authorDate'>（1161年6月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 南宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(31376, "南宋", "薛季宣", "poem_title_1273673")'>薛季宣</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1273673_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1273673'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1273673'>某昨者伏遇行台循问及境，思有所献而不敢越其职分，辄请金牛置尉以销南乡之盗，纵论及于营田，仰荷采纳，不以为过。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1273673_comment'></div>退思营田部吏豪横之迹，为民显患，州县犹无得而制，则虽置尉无益。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1273673_comment'></div>以为营田不罢，不可以立尉司。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1273673_comment'></div>盖县不能统营田，则其为盗贼渊薮。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1273673_comment'></div>自若营田幸罢，然后尉职可修，军罢而归，置尉乃为急务。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1273673_comment'></div>顾此军务方冗，事若难行，此来未敢复言，乃蒙询问下及，辄敢条其利病，列于左方。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1273673_comment'></div></div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_6_1273673'>一、古者宿兵绝徼，多为营田，所以省馈连之劳，而勤士卒之惰也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1273673_comment'></div>然而古之调卒，盖取诸农，且战且耕，犹易为力。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1273673_comment'></div>今之营田异于古之营田也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1273673_comment'></div>强士以所不能，弃之而不复教，耕者犹不足自赡，何有于一军？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1273673_comment'></div>废战而赡之，耕非其理矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1273673_comment'></div></div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_11_1273673'>一、营田之卒，一人垦地约二十亩，岁得谷六十硕。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1273673_comment'></div>其奉钱月三贯，米七㪷五升，岁计钱三十六贯，米九硕，而衣赐不与。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1273673_comment'></div>管辖官校大约什置一人，请奉或十倍于兵，则是二十兵营田二顷，得谷岁六百硕，费钱七百二十贯，米一百八十硕，而衣赐不与，牛种农器不在焉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1273673_comment'></div>此营田利害之晓然者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1273673_comment'></div></div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_15_1273673'>一、湖外谷价低昂不等，约其中数，硕谷为钱五百。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1273673_comment'></div>营田庄寨去军远者数百里，以马运谷，骑士从之，往复数程，负谷二硕，校之中直，为钱一千；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1273673_comment'></div>人马在途，其费相若。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1273673_comment'></div>近时士卒弃谷而归者有之，质之人情，未足深过。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1273673_comment'></div></div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_19_1273673'>一、营田之在诸邑，类皆夺民膏腴，稍有良田，民颇耕，营田辄掩而取，州县无得谁何。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1273673_comment'></div>或有水源，营田皆擅其利，民田灌溉非复可得。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1273673_comment'></div>有如放水，则决诸民田之中。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1273673_comment'></div>民以其田归之，为之佃户，非惟可庇赋役，始可保有其田。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1273673_comment'></div>又有无良之人，乐于放纵，一为佃户，遂可横行于乡。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1273673_comment'></div>而无知之民复有平托军校，窜名佃户以避追须。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1273673_comment'></div>虽有盗贼寄迹其间，州县已不敢问，巡尉保伍何从得之！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1273673_comment'></div></div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_26_1273673'>一、营田官校往往不恤其军，科配茶盐日有定计，比及打请，举而取之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1273673_comment'></div>营田之额有增无减，岁有荒歉，皆于军士名下剋除，死损牛车，亦令均备。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1273673_comment'></div>窝藏剽掠，盖非得已而然，自非部校容之，何自而骋？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1273673_comment'></div>部校家自为盗，尤不可容。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1273673_comment'></div></div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_30_1273673'>一、营田部辖下至军兵，往往因公为私，多招佃户，侵耕冒种，不知纪极。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_30_1273673_comment'></div>州县不相统属，故难稽考。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_31_1273673_comment'></div>一户岁失苗米数硕，过百则已及千，一县之间，不知失几百户！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_32_1273673_comment'></div>营田增羡无几，实何补于军中！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_33_1273673_comment'></div></div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_34_1273673'>一、营田军兵，固有老而不可复战者，久于田亩，稍知其趣，又有佃户实供官租，如罢营田，必恐失业。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_34_1273673_comment'></div>如因见耕之产，使为佃户，营田牛具皆以给之，军兵所弃之田因而召人耕佃，阅岁无几，租入必羡于今。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_35_1273673_comment'></div></div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_36_1273673'>一、窃闻营田马料在总所岁计之数，今来军马调发马料系诸路应副。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_36_1273673_comment'></div>若因此时权罢，召民耕佃其田，宽以数年，自可及额；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_37_1273673_comment'></div>若便责之县邑，窃恐未易出办。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_38_1273673_comment'></div></div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_39_1273673'>一、营田之在诸乡，为害虽大，而营寨棋布，舍烟颇为翕集，一旦罢军而返马，或恐人烟空窎，盗贼因兹窃发。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_39_1273673_comment'></div>若第罢遣士卒，其佃客及附庄户并令安业，宽之如旧，自可以无此患。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_40_1273673_comment'></div></div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_41_1273673'>一、伏见诸路营田官庄，皆以县尉兼掌。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_41_1273673_comment'></div>本县官兵营田若罢，尤宜置尉南乡分掌官庄，辖其佃户。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_42_1273673_comment'></div>它县视地广狭，措置大略仿此。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_43_1273673_comment'></div>非惟可销盗贼，兼免失陷官租。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_44_1273673_comment'></div></div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_45_1273673'>某似闻营田马料，每硕破总所般运钱壹贯文。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_45_1273673_comment'></div>其实使士卒般运，不曾支给，却作营田上供金银起发。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_46_1273673_comment'></div>只此一事，虚耗已多。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_47_1273673_comment'></div>某不能知总所支钱之详，更乞询究其实。</div><div id='poem_sentence_48_1273673_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1161&endYear=1161')">1161年8月</a>　在武昌令任上。成闵为湖北、京西制置使，分兵屯夏口。是月，金兵分三路大举南侵。薛季宣上书成闵、汪澈，认为武昌形势险要，关系淮、蔡安全，宜屯重兵驻防。作品：上成马帅论屯军。论屯戍。<div id='poem_1273693' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1273693' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1273693?labeling=true' target='_blank'>上成马帅论屯军</a><span class='authorDate'>（1161年8月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 南宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(31376, "南宋", "薛季宣", "poem_title_1273693")'>薛季宣</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1273693_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1273693'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1273693'>某读《吴志》，至汉居许而吴都鄂，传于魏则徙金陵，得孙氏之所为废兴，从而知仲谋之本志。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1273693_comment'></div>武昌，古鄂县也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1273693_comment'></div>其地四达，襟带江、淮，许、蔡、申、陈相望五百里而近。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1273693_comment'></div>绝江以北，莫捷此途，袭以轻兵，信宿可至。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1273693_comment'></div>以斯谋许，诚无济矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1273693_comment'></div>汉祚移而鼎国分，武昌密尔于魏鄙，建邺之徙端在于斯。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1273693_comment'></div>今之江南，旧为吴地，以钱塘为都邑，则衢、信、洪、抚为之冲。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1273693_comment'></div>乡来金人南牧之兵掩自武昌南渡，是时鄂州兵十三万，闻而蹑之，已不能及。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1273693_comment'></div>自县之西有马桥湖四十里，武昌有变，救之实难。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1273693_comment'></div>北望黄州，去淮才四百里。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1273693_comment'></div>淮流可涉，绝无关津，毁拆黄民之居以为牌筏，顺流而下，不劳舟楫而通。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1273693_comment'></div>今议不此之虞，徒益兵于江夏。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1273693_comment'></div>江夏背山阻水，汉阳以北背陂湖，以进则难，无往而可。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1273693_comment'></div>万一虏人渡汉，由间道以袭豫章，不数日而下江西，因进军以倾衢、信，吾军悉在其后，宁不为都邑虑乎？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1273693_comment'></div>江夏之屯，乃岳飞所以制湖贼。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1273693_comment'></div>西临襄汉，阻水实多，进退江淮以全制虏之后，取道神速，远不逮于武昌。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1273693_comment'></div>吴蜀之冲，固已无急于此。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1273693_comment'></div>东晋之世，陶侃都督江南，其治在于武昌，足以明其险要。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1273693_comment'></div>某官按行边徼，在所当言，某备数长官，不敢不告。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1273693_comment'></div>僭越之罪，死不敢逃。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1273693_comment'></div>留军以屯，惟太尉命。</div><div id='poem_sentence_20_1273693_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1161&endYear=1161')">1161年8月</a>　在武昌令任上。宋金开战以后，江、淮一带地方官纷纷遣还家眷，准备逃走。薛季宣却积极筹划死守，组织军力防御敌人。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1161&endYear=1161')">1161年9月</a>　在武昌令任上。九月，金兵困蒋州。汪澈向薛季宣询问对策。季宣上劄子，建议先取蔡州，“蔡州已平，蒋当自溃。蔡平则虏失要镇，大功易立”作品：上宣谕论淮西事宜之二。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1161&endYear=1161')">1161年10月</a>　在武昌令任上。十月，成闵部将赵撙攻克蔡州，蒋州围解。是时淮西形势紧张，都统制王权闻金兵大至，自庐州逃到采石，刘锜退守镇江。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1161&endYear=1161')">1161年11月</a>　在武昌令任上。十一月，成闵自应城引兵东援淮西。季宣上书汪澈，认为我军既得蔡州，有破竹之势，宜留重兵防守，令成闵乘虚攻下颖昌，取道陈、汝，直取汴都，敌人有内顾之忧，自然溃逃。又论朝廷御将之术未尽其道。作品：上宣谕论淮西事宜。答宣谕范机宜。<div id='poem_1273669' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1273669' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1273669?labeling=true' target='_blank'>答宣谕范机宜书</a><span class='authorDate'>（1161年11月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 南宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(31376, "南宋", "薛季宣", "poem_title_1273669")'>薛季宣</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1273669_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1273669'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1273669'>下喻陈蔡之事，今留屯者赵樽耳。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1273669_comment'></div>深入虏界，其军至为孤弱，二郡势不相及，窃恐为累反大。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1273669_comment'></div>适得黄冈许簿报，前日秦、陈二统制自上蔡赴援，州人皆遮道而泣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1273669_comment'></div>夫蔡为重镇，虏之喉襟也，幸而得之，乃委之而去。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1273669_comment'></div>事已至是，故不当复论。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1273669_comment'></div>但蔡人开门迎纳之事，虏帅复来，必遭屠戮，不唯误一方生灵之命，实恐绝中原归向之心。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1273669_comment'></div>就使虏全而用之，乘其愤愤不平之气，其锋有不可当者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1273669_comment'></div>且今舒、蕲以西绝无兵马，复蔡之军又去强半，则数千里间空虚甚矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1273669_comment'></div>淮东之寇或为诸将所破，势必西走，苟得一航之渡，则吾事有不可胜言者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1273669_comment'></div>今之施为大谬如此。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1273669_comment'></div>某不敢喋喋干渎宣谕，议论之次，告以此及之。</div><div id='poem_sentence_10_1273669_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1161&endYear=1161')">1161年11月</a>　在武昌令任上。是月，判潭州张浚改判建康府。薛季宣于江边拜见张浚。作品：与张左司书。<div id='poem_1273715' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1273715' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1273715?labeling=true' target='_blank'>与张左司<span class='inlineComment2'>（栻）</span>书</a><span class='authorDate'>（1161年11月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 南宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(31376, "南宋", "薛季宣", "poem_title_1273715")'>薛季宣</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1273715_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1273715'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1273715'>即日秋气澄肃，伏惟徜徉闾闬，台候神相万福。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1273715_comment'></div>某先君右史、先伯待制皆受知于先正忠献，致位从班。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1273715_comment'></div>辛巳岁，某备县鄂陵，伏遇元戎即镇金陵，得迎拜于芦洲江步，时已昏暮，伏蒙略去贵贱等威，赐之坐席，温言慰藉，详问存没，区区感戴，鉴寐不忘。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1273715_comment'></div>伏自忠献薨背，某僻在海滨，都失奔问，徒切慊然。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1273715_comment'></div>比年待次毗陵，日闻左司以道学为诸儒唱，告猷悟主，几振吾道，非独为先世私喜，实为善类公庆。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1273715_comment'></div>某方辞审察之召，虽恨不得抠衣几席，而友朋陈君举辈仰荷予进，获闻至正大中之论，所幸已多，且蒙不察其愚，乃欲力相汲引。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1273715_comment'></div>某自顾触藩之久，惧涉其怪，又贪承教，去夏遂谋入都，以欲一见。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1273715_comment'></div>郑景望吏部取道宛陵，忽闻出镇宜春，行次苕水，亟与林择之秀才疾走吴兴郡下，至则鹢舫已西到都，乃知谋过义兴，枉道临访，差池至此，弥更惘然。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1273715_comment'></div>合并之难，一至于是。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1273715_comment'></div>然而千里明月，奚远近之拘邪？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1273715_comment'></div>某自去秋中备数京辇，虽与伯恭子充亲洽，然以人情益薄，不敢显白相从。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1273715_comment'></div>到官之初，一谒当路，是后弗敢复见。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1273715_comment'></div>至前忽蒙假节淮西，悤悤径行，以腊月中旬至部。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1273715_comment'></div>江饶流移，既已赈之无及，而淮北归正，无非守将之欺，小人党与强盛，不敢顾身，三以实闻，仅能寘之于理。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1273715_comment'></div>过元夕至江浦，始与赵帅俊民收流移之未业者，为官庄以处之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1273715_comment'></div>齐安二十二区、合肥复三十六圩之旧，各不过三百四五十户；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1273715_comment'></div>其馀土人招为客户，无虑数千。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1273715_comment'></div>人情不欲闻，官所籍止三千五百户，主惠至渥，不能有所推广，不学无术，临事乃知其累。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1273715_comment'></div>所甚为朝廷叹者，荒田芜于包占，经理害于无谋，归节之际，不敢一毫隐也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1273715_comment'></div>圣恩过厚，职秩皆蒙超次之除，还都百绪一新，进退方谷，偶吴兴阙守，骤蒙中旨之授。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1273715_comment'></div>用踰其分。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1273715_comment'></div>诚剧畏悚。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1273715_comment'></div>而在一身出处私计，虽自为谋，不过如此，然而近圻名郡，千疮百痏，甚非绵薄之所宜居；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1273715_comment'></div>况又踪迹见目于人，危如秋叶，吹竽鼓瑟，孰非孤露？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1273715_comment'></div>未知所以善后，惟在我者不敢不勉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1273715_comment'></div>是外付之造物，人事讵易必邪？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1273715_comment'></div>念未参识，宜当道术相忘，窃思记问不通，人情有所不可，辄尽底蕴，庶几有以察之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1273715_comment'></div>复念古今异时，变态万状，谓非在己无恶，无必于人，用能观感，化服异端，会将有济。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1273715_comment'></div>腾口无益于事，祇招谤訾，适以害道甚矣，要当深思密用退藏，是乃待时之计。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1273715_comment'></div>鄙见如此，不识有取于斯乎？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1273715_comment'></div>辱以声气相求，无惜鞭其不逮，至恳至祝。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_30_1273715_comment'></div>某复有少禀，先正幕府所绘被边形势，颇得表里之要，辄欲就乞传本，以广未闻，人旋得蒙垂示，甚幸！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_31_1273715_comment'></div>台眷上下均受如山之祉，浙中有可委者，无巨细辱示。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_32_1273715_comment'></div>某去就之谊，未知当作何处，且欲为卒岁计，不识可乎？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_33_1273715_comment'></div>可以警其愚，万乞疏示。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_34_1273715_comment'></div>承晤邈未有日，敢祝加餐进业，行以大学，光明于时！</div><div id='poem_sentence_35_1273715_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1161&endYear=1161')">1161年12月</a>　在武昌令任上。十二月，淮南金军全部北撤。季宣作《平狄颂》<div id='poem_1273879' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1273879' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1273879?labeling=true' target='_blank'>平狄颂<span class='inlineComment2'>（秦体）</span></a><span class='authorDate'>（1161年12月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 南宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(31376, "南宋", "薛季宣", "poem_title_1273879")'>薛季宣</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'>四言诗</div></div><div id='poem_title_1273879_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1273879'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1273879'>皇帝绍兴卅有一年，聿修文德。<div id='poem_sentence_0_1273879_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_1273879'>礼制修明，山川鬼神，罔不昭假。<div id='poem_sentence_1_1273879_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_1273879'>乐天含垢，惠康有民，施及蛮貊。<div id='poem_sentence_2_1273879_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_1273879'>蠢尔女真，惏虐无已，敢为残贼。<div id='poem_sentence_3_1273879_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_1273879'>骋其臣仆，奸求越度，以显凶愎。<div id='poem_sentence_4_1273879_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_5_1273879'>皇帝仁圣，贷不加诛，渗渗然休泽。<div id='poem_sentence_5_1273879_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_6_1273879'>乃敢不悛厥心，蛩跳贙啖，是兴兵革。<div id='poem_sentence_6_1273879_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_7_1273879'>东航沧海，西陵蜀汉，凭淮之宅。<div id='poem_sentence_7_1273879_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_8_1273879'>犬羊是率，虔刘是肆，罔遗馀力。<div id='poem_sentence_8_1273879_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_9_1273879'>剜精剔孕，藉骀台耇，害及弱息。<div id='poem_sentence_9_1273879_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_10_1273879'>覆侵王略，列州十五，震惊八极。<div id='poem_sentence_10_1273879_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_11_1273879'>皇帝瘅怒，曰惟汝亮，而惟此极！<div id='poem_sentence_11_1273879_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_12_1273879'>朕承天休命，子畜元元，奉天行殛！<div id='poem_sentence_12_1273879_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_13_1273879'>天堑斯凭，镞无遗矢，靡舂矛戟。<div id='poem_sentence_13_1273879_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_14_1273879'>狂奴左计，自西徂东，天夺之魄。<div id='poem_sentence_14_1273879_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_15_1273879'>风师借便，混漭沧茫，戈船既克。<div id='poem_sentence_15_1273879_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_16_1273879'>灵旗警夜，弋阳内溃，明神效职。<div id='poem_sentence_16_1273879_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_17_1273879'>女真之旅，莫不疾视，乃心万亿。<div id='poem_sentence_17_1273879_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_18_1273879'>前徒倒戈，中坚靡抗，罪人斯得。<div id='poem_sentence_18_1273879_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_19_1273879'>虏骑如云，其鼓如霆，涣然冰释。<div id='poem_sentence_19_1273879_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_20_1273879'>三公列将，咸拜稽首曰：惟我皇帝，顺天之则。<div id='poem_sentence_20_1273879_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_21_1273879'>受天之福，天戈所指，独夫自踣。<div id='poem_sentence_21_1273879_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_22_1273879'>戎兵不战，屈兹丑类，匪臣之力。<div id='poem_sentence_22_1273879_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_23_1273879'>昔谢安有淮淝之捷，功不遂就，为万世所惜；<div id='poem_sentence_23_1273879_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_24_1273879'>今天威旁阐，愿极其锋，定我王国！<div id='poem_sentence_24_1273879_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_25_1273879'>皇帝恻隐，曰此狂胡，毕天之命，朕心有衋。<div id='poem_sentence_25_1273879_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_26_1273879'>嗟尔将士，乘是吉几，勉扬尔职。<div id='poem_sentence_26_1273879_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_27_1273879'>刷耻明功，平金之乱，虎龙而翼。<div id='poem_sentence_27_1273879_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_28_1273879'>神州黔首，思禀文告，覃于九域。<div id='poem_sentence_28_1273879_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_29_1273879'>飞将拱手，曰毋多𢦤，以惠南北！<div id='poem_sentence_29_1273879_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_30_1273879'>小臣作颂，歌咏神功，请攻镌乐石。</div><div id='poem_sentence_30_1273879_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1162&endYear=1162')">1162年2月1日</a>　在武昌令任上。虞允文为兵部尚书、川陕宣谕使，措置招军市马及与吴璘议事，西行道径武昌，薛季宣与他相识。作品：与虞右相。<div id='poem_1273681' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1273681' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1273681?labeling=true' target='_blank'>与虞右相书</a><span class='authorDate'>（1162年2月1日）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 南宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(31376, "南宋", "薛季宣", "poem_title_1273681")'>薛季宣</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1273681_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1273681'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1273681'>某岁在辛巳、癸未间，试鄂之武昌令，伏遇元戎督视关陕，道出境上，初与齐安郡官旅谒律步，夙仰声谊，遂获一觇钧表，已剧私幸。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1273681_comment'></div>既而螭舫东返，又率戍县诸将迎见于大江中流。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1273681_comment'></div>伏蒙略去等威，席艕而坐，酌以卮酒，出示地图，虽悤悤拜违，接馀论之不款，然蒙钧慈礼遇之意，盖不与常人等矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1273681_comment'></div>当时戎行之士同泛而归，论公之贤，至有加手于额者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1273681_comment'></div>仰窥所以制服诸将、式遏乱略、参功微管者，岂徒然哉！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1273681_comment'></div>感叹之私，中藏亡已。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1273681_comment'></div>嗣以名位悬隔，道路阻修，诇问之函从不复贡，虽聆大拜，亦不敢修贺主书。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1273681_comment'></div>然而每与士夫共论当世王公，未尝不及鄂陵之所亲见，莫不吁嗟称叹，以为近世之所无也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1273681_comment'></div>敢谓精意人物，不遗菅蒯。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1273681_comment'></div>兹者荐蒙命召，寔出造化炉锤之力。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1273681_comment'></div>收之既去，诚出过恩；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1273681_comment'></div>非分得之，秪深愧仄。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1273681_comment'></div>顾今异昔，伏念之，某既蒙特达之知，诇候之仪，不敢自同疏远之士，赤纸奏记，敢冀钧察<span class='inlineComment2'>（云云）</span>。</div><div id='poem_sentence_12_1273681_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1162&endYear=1162')">1162年2月19日</a>　在武昌令任上。二月十九日，作《感沐赋》<div id='poem_1273588' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1273588' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1273588?labeling=true' target='_blank'>感沐赋</a><span class='authorDate'>（1162年2月19日）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 南宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(31376, "南宋", "薛季宣", "poem_title_1273588")'>薛季宣</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1273588_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1273588'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1273588'>壬午中春十有九日，走沐，见二毛焉，因感而赋。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1273588_comment'></div></div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_1273588'>沐余发兮中春，感余心兮泯纷。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1273588_comment'></div>乌头白兮道蒙若，不壮年兮兆衰落。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1273588_comment'></div>元始昆仑，阅岁华之垓载兮，飙如宿昔。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1273588_comment'></div>人生百龄，月过千之云积兮，羌亏盈之不可度。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1273588_comment'></div>羲和叱驭而莫之挽兮，倏焉归于窅漠。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1273588_comment'></div>视权舆为一欠呻兮，矧吾生之略约。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1273588_comment'></div>彼颜子二十九而白头兮，亲圣师而亡悔。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1273588_comment'></div>思文君于鼓琴兮，儃沈吟于本始。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1273588_comment'></div>春归园而秀木兮，果觌花而知实。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1273588_comment'></div>人间世兮，苟托栖于兹室。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1273588_comment'></div>多文饰兮，华发班其可喜。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1273588_comment'></div>一彼此之暂然兮，嘻其云异。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1273588_comment'></div>视老彭为非望兮，若殇子者吾其至愉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1273588_comment'></div>皇苍之司寿夭兮，繄余何意。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1273588_comment'></div>寄悲歌而写志兮，曰生之忽也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1273588_comment'></div>庶汇由天，俱斯物也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1273588_comment'></div>春萼荣华，几其日也？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1273588_comment'></div>班白颠兮，犹之一也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1273588_comment'></div>于乎乐兮，终归没也。</div><div id='poem_sentence_19_1273588_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1162&endYear=1162')">1162年2月</a>　在武昌令任上。二月，赵撙退出蔡州。薛季宣上书汪澈，论敌我形势。作品：上宣谕论北事。<div id='poem_1273675' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1273675' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1273675?labeling=true' target='_blank'>上宣谕论北事</a><span class='authorDate'>（1162年2月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 南宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(31376, "南宋", "薛季宣", "poem_title_1273675")'>薛季宣</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1273675_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1273675'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1273675'>某自涉春以还，稍不贡记室之问，非敢怠也，特以人微位下，谊当自敛。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1273675_comment'></div>不自畏缩，譊譊焉日以猥穰之说躐陈于大君子之前，虽至德包荒，不以为过，不知我者谓之何哉！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1273675_comment'></div>重自黠虏歼灭而来，士夫随复骄惰，私忧过计，必以我为徼幸多事之士，是以虽有寡闻，不敢仰渎台听。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1273675_comment'></div>然而闻见日积，乃心郁如。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1273675_comment'></div>仰惟宠遇之隆，每蒙不赐诛绝，奉头鼠匿，殆将绝于门墙，虽少安小人之私，然非所以为仰报眷予之意。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1273675_comment'></div>偶所闻若有所系，朝廷殊未有以处之，执事奋不顾身，自任以天下之重，故某辄尽底蕴，窃敢言之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1273675_comment'></div>窃以国家比岁用兵之初，实未闻尝有战守之略，宏远之计，谋不素定，将帅乏才，欲以久惰之兵幸其一胜，泛泛然如投无钩之钓，求鱼于三江五湖之间。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1273675_comment'></div>兵不交而丧庐、淝，非虏之计善也，吾谋之不至尔。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1273675_comment'></div>赖天祐宋德，虏恶贯盈，当人情危惧之秋，内有鸣镝之祸，使彼偷生卒岁，纵不渡江，抚淮南而有之，我无息肩日矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1273675_comment'></div>幸彼丧君而返，人情不无二三，蹑而歼之，可使少知惩艾，失此不计，使大定得以缉绥其民，是皆事在以前，悔不可及。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1273675_comment'></div>来者之计在庙堂，不可不图。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1273675_comment'></div>然以今之边防视前日为何似？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1273675_comment'></div>今日师旅视前日为孰多？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1273675_comment'></div>自冬徂春，恬不复计，虏使压境，又复不知所为，彼怒而归，意可见矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1273675_comment'></div>且夫大定之立，岂诚厚于我哉？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1273675_comment'></div>良以国有内忧，上下未睦，死酋之败，政以无故兴师，故此寻盟以和其内，须我待之有阙，师出不为无名，怒其众而用之，庶其有济，是必穹庐之下，君臣朝夕之所自为谋者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1273675_comment'></div>而吾邦不此之忧，猷之未远，使虏再至，果能却之否乎？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1273675_comment'></div>古求欲以胜人，以为莫如自治。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1273675_comment'></div>两淮之战，吾之手足露矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1273675_comment'></div>为今守御之备，当百倍于曩时。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1273675_comment'></div>前日之偾，政以长淮不守。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1273675_comment'></div>守淮之计，庐、寿为急。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1273675_comment'></div>以周世宗之略，尚不能久处淮南，盖刘仁赡坚守寿春，当其冲会。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1273675_comment'></div>寿春不下，固不可越之而有淮南，非仁赡者果能胜周，诚亦兵家之所禁也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1273675_comment'></div>前日以淮为不足守，弃庐、寿而守扬州，既不能军，遂守江面。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1273675_comment'></div>设有台舆失备，守将奈何？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1273675_comment'></div>使虏悟前日之非，又将大举，以重兵当诸将，轻兵乘间浮江，黑帜一建于南，守江之功殆矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1273675_comment'></div>且彼前日之失，以虏身自任之，安知今日北朝不知选任良将，汰其偏僝，救过已往？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1273675_comment'></div>吾非蚤计，恐难悠久。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1273675_comment'></div>为今之策，尤当固守淮南。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1273675_comment'></div>顾诸将之所行，殆儿戏之不若，一州一邑，戍兵才千百，计无补于事，徒析成军。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_30_1273675_comment'></div>吾军政苦乏人，为计岂宜若此？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_31_1273675_comment'></div>传闻陈州之围日急，救兵未闻一至，遗氓报宋，无若此城，弃之不疑，是岂恢复之道？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_32_1273675_comment'></div>前日蔡州之事，尚或可为，第缘守者不勤，救者不至，前功尽弃，虏徒手而得之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_33_1273675_comment'></div>使虏方至之初，游骑出没者寡，伏兵掩击，可以杜其复来；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_34_1273675_comment'></div>比及攻城，援兵要战于后，内外相应，岂无成功？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_35_1273675_comment'></div>汝、邓弃州而归，那复为上蔡地？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_36_1273675_comment'></div>托名援救，实自成其退计尔。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_37_1273675_comment'></div>帅臣举皆若此，缓急讵足恃乎？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_38_1273675_comment'></div>窃闻鄂州之军非果不供于用，特以调发无当，致此纷纭；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_39_1273675_comment'></div>复求忠锐不习之军以为内援，岂惟无补，行复误事。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_40_1273675_comment'></div>方今用人之际，命将尤宜详审。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_41_1273675_comment'></div>御营殿帅，果虏之所畏邪？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_42_1273675_comment'></div>汉王闻魏将之名，即知魏之可取。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_43_1273675_comment'></div>今日诸将，知复如何？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_44_1273675_comment'></div>李横、傅选之徒，于岳军粗有声誉，废居散地，舆论惜之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_45_1273675_comment'></div>处选浙西，固无所事；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_46_1273675_comment'></div>弃横于蜀，将焉用之？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_47_1273675_comment'></div>二公徒不事贵臣，岂皆果不忠者？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_48_1273675_comment'></div>处之襄、邓，未必遂无可观。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_49_1273675_comment'></div>将士得各遂其所安，战气亦十倍矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_50_1273675_comment'></div>是皆愚见所及，欲以少补大谋之一二。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_51_1273675_comment'></div>辞不尽意，执事不以为谬而辱观之，惟所弃置焉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_52_1273675_comment'></div>不任区区战汗之至。</div><div id='poem_sentence_53_1273675_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1162&endYear=1162')">1162年7月</a>　在武昌令任上。七月，张浚为少傅、江淮宣谕使，封魏国公。薛季宣上书张浚，指出“今朝廷之上，既忘前日之殆，宴然以为事处之矣”，主张“以我之不可胜，待敌之可胜，而不恃敌之可胜”作品：上张宣谕书。<div id='poem_1273676' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1273676' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1273676?labeling=true' target='_blank'>上张宣谕论书</a><span class='authorDate'>（1162年7月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 南宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(31376, "南宋", "薛季宣", "poem_title_1273676")'>薛季宣</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1273676_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1273676'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1273676'>某读《诗·小雅》，得文王之所以兴建大业，与宣王之所以绍开中兴，固未始不本之人情，见之肤使；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1273676_comment'></div>而其一时之使，亦未尝非忠信之士，王之同德不二三之臣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1273676_comment'></div>良以四目四门，委之一使，上焉以布宣德意，下焉以道通人情，五侯九伯所为取正，四夷八蛮所为驯服，非忠信之士，王之同德心膂之臣，则亦不能胜其任矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1273676_comment'></div>故《皇皇者华》，君遣使臣之诗也，送之以礼乐，年远而有光华也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1273676_comment'></div>诗之首章不过「每怀靡及」，终篇之议「咨询」、「咨度」而已。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1273676_comment'></div>《六月》，宣王北伐也，言不及于有功之将帅，而其卒章乃称「文武吉甫，万邦为宪。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1273676_comment'></div>来归自镐，我行永久」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1273676_comment'></div>由是言之，使臣之任，顾不重哉！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1273676_comment'></div>使臣而不能及政之阙，尽咨询之义，至于万邦为宪，则虽匹妇不可以情得，昆夷、猃狁何从而正？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1273676_comment'></div>文、宣之政，可谓知所本矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1273676_comment'></div>执事，吉甫等辈人也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1273676_comment'></div>当主上薄伐猃狁、绍开中兴之际，以皇华之使，任吉甫之责，淝水横流而气不为沮，河洛尘昏而谋不为挫，迄能恢复汝、邓，观兵嵩、洛；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1273676_comment'></div>东收陈、蔡之壤，北却萧、刘之寇。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1273676_comment'></div>光华之远，于斯见之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1273676_comment'></div>「我行永久」，宜圣主之渴思而反之也，「来归自镐」，其所为告后者，是必先已有定。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1273676_comment'></div>如民力之彫毙，屯田之劳扰，执事咨询有素，决不置之者也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1273676_comment'></div>至于诸将之才，敌谋之情伪，固文武之馀事，又无待于鄙言矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1273676_comment'></div>窃意诸军进退之实，熟见稔闻之事，如复蒋之妄，入汝之失，救蔡之不力，弃邓之无所顾籍，与夫不恤在行之士，不绥傒后之民，凡若此流，仰惟耳目之布，必已周知其状矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1273676_comment'></div>咈人情，误国计，宜莫此若也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1273676_comment'></div>今朝廷之上，既忘前日之殆，宴然以无事处之矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1273676_comment'></div>在列之士，必未有及是言者；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1273676_comment'></div>纵及于此，又必不能周悉其详。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1273676_comment'></div>咨度咨询，所以仰副虚怀之意，为宪于万邦者，愿执事以身任之也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1273676_comment'></div>光华之美，于此而至，执事必不难之矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1273676_comment'></div>虽然，犹有说也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1273676_comment'></div>虏之未渝平也，盖每言其内乱，刃交兵接，亦又不然。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1273676_comment'></div>自淮而归，告乱者又纷如也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1273676_comment'></div>以我之不可胜，待敌之可胜，而不恃敌之可胜，亦欲朝廷之戒之也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1273676_comment'></div>某窭人也，无寸长之可取，且无先容之助，一言堂下，执事不以俗吏待之；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1273676_comment'></div>以公事言，未尝有不听者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1273676_comment'></div>一邑之赐，于某偏矣，輶轩之复，不可以无言送，敢以所学于《小雅》者仰布于下。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_30_1273676_comment'></div>执事视文、宣之所为攘却昆夷，猃狁之事，可以从知大业中兴之略。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_31_1273676_comment'></div>执事固秉国政，事必优为之矣，非小子之佞。</div><div id='poem_sentence_32_1273676_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1162&endYear=1162')">1162年7月</a>　在武昌令任上。七月，参知政事汪澈（汪澈于四月任参知政事）视师湖北、京西。追复岳飞原官，以礼改葬。薛季宣上书汪澈，认为应该加岳飞以恩数，以激励士伍。作品：与汪参政明远论岳侯恩数。<div id='poem_1273703' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1273703' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1273703?labeling=true' target='_blank'>与汪参政明远论岳侯恩数书</a><span class='authorDate'>（1162年7月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 南宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(31376, "南宋", "薛季宣", "poem_title_1273703")'>薛季宣</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1273703_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1273703'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1273703'>某闻燕王市骏马之骨，贤者归之；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1273703_comment'></div>句践揖怒螳之臂，士为必死。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1273703_comment'></div>是皆推诚异类，犹感切于人心。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1273703_comment'></div>施诸功臣，焉有不格！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1273703_comment'></div>共惟皇上即位之始，首雪岳飞之冤，天下知与不知，无不称庆。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1273703_comment'></div>逮今数月，宜人人有报效之心，求诸军情，乃反有纷纷之论。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1273703_comment'></div>此议者过也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1273703_comment'></div>日者樊建以晋武帝知邓艾之冤而不能直，知其得诸葛亮而不能臣，推恩于飞，宁不类是？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1273703_comment'></div>使飞果反朝廷，不当昭雪；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1273703_comment'></div>为之昭雪，是非真反。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1273703_comment'></div>苟非真反，则亚保之礼不当有废，国家纵不能归其赗赠，追加封爵，犹当反其田宅，畀之恩数，亲降黼座，临奠其丧，会其子孙以礼归葬，使人知为子孙之利，则为善者犹有所劝。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1273703_comment'></div>今独不然，惟复其封而已。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1273703_comment'></div>改葬之礼，非复典彝，官其诸孙，仅同卒伍。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1273703_comment'></div>今夫庶官之死，延赏犹世其家，而独于飞偏有所靳，以求人心之感，不亦难哉？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1273703_comment'></div>德寿中兴之成，不过张俊、韩世忠、刘光世、秦桧四人而已，四人之终，礼有异数，今其子孙或位孤卿；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1273703_comment'></div>飞之功勤不已加于四子，毙于非命，自乎既往，追之来者，乃至于斯人之多言，亦可畏也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1273703_comment'></div>昔魏佛狸饮马瓜步，宋文帝临江而叹，以为檀道济不死，虏不至是，曾不能追录其后，识者有以卜其世祚之脩短。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1273703_comment'></div>逆亮南寇，胡人自为「岳飞不死，大金灭矣」之语。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1273703_comment'></div>然则所以激劝士伍者，安可不厚？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1273703_comment'></div>仰惟都督参政相公以道事君，以诚体国，明飞不反，公议攸归。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1273703_comment'></div>恩礼不加，想当未惬于钧重；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1273703_comment'></div>建言宸极，在乎謦欬之间。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1273703_comment'></div>使优孟不至笑人，则人知乡善之利矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1273703_comment'></div>某鲰生晚进，不知政体，伏念先子荐飞为将，伯父参其军府，今日之事，不忍不为一言。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1273703_comment'></div>顾飞已亡，何有游说？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1273703_comment'></div>徒为国家惜此举措不厌人心。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1273703_comment'></div>管仲所谓知善而不能赏之，与郭公之亡何异？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1273703_comment'></div>是则雪飞之冤而取众怒，不若不为之为愈也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1273703_comment'></div>行府信能终始兹事，史策当不负人，人心之归本朝，又安知不在兹举也？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1273703_comment'></div>况今行营将士往往故飞部曲，求其死力，莫此为善。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1273703_comment'></div>惟钧慈阔略鄙夫之妄，决而行之，不胜至幸！</div><div id='poem_sentence_30_1273703_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1162&endYear=1162')">1162年7月</a>　在武昌令任上。七月，参知政事汪澈（汪澈于四月任参知政事）视师湖北、京西。薛季宣上书汪澈论屯戍。作品：与汪参政明远论屯戍。<div id='poem_1273704' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1273704' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1273704?labeling=true' target='_blank'>与汪参政明远论屯戍书</a><span class='authorDate'>（1162年7月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 南宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(31376, "南宋", "薛季宣", "poem_title_1273704")'>薛季宣</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1273704_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1273704'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1273704'>某比者伏蒙钧旆视师沔鄂，经从下县，得获迎拜道左，深慰久违瞻恋之诚。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1273704_comment'></div>自惟寒贱小官，参谒相府，不敢越次上干掌客，区区之情，有所未尽。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1273704_comment'></div>然某去岁伏蒙眷遇之礼，优出伦辈，感德之厚，未尝一日敢忘，苟有知而不言，实为负恩于下，故敢辄尽底蕴，仰触钧严。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1273704_comment'></div>某昨馈输信阳，自黄陂而北，地形平易，实所备睹，德安虽有军戍，其外并无藩篱。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1273704_comment'></div>古之三关漫不复守，仵落漕舟数百，沙碛不可上通，急缓出口既难，适足济师资寇。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1273704_comment'></div>早来得信阳周判官初九日报，云陈蔡之寇来者日益，或有侵突，当为不可胜以待之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1273704_comment'></div>如仵落东入阳罗，西通汉口，顺流而下，不及数程。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1273704_comment'></div>某自孝感而归，再宿而达县界，今也光、黄既无师众，而德安单弱，如此使三关屯守，犹恐无险之可依，不蚤图之，窃恐无以豫备不测，万一虏以万人侵犯安陆，则我军与之相持，别军取仵落之舟，粮道可以兼得，顺流南略，则武昌、夏口为可深忧。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1273704_comment'></div>不知行府可以先成侯之来为区处否？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1273704_comment'></div>至于黄州一路，去岁申禀已详，更乞钧慈俯赐照察。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1273704_comment'></div>干冒僭越，不胜战栗兢兢。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1273704_comment'></div></div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_11_1273704'>某窃闻行府非晚视师汉上，此固先务。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1273704_comment'></div>然闻蔡寇日急，区区之见，以为此行犹可少缓，要当严戍襄郢，固守德安，东防武昌，以须成侯之来，然后钧旆西引，有如幨车遂发，万一德安而东忽有警报，此既未有主帅，恐失事几。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1273704_comment'></div>愚瞽献言，敢乞恕其狂妄。</div><div id='poem_sentence_13_1273704_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1162&endYear=1162')">1162年7月</a>　在武昌令任上。七月，参知政事汪澈（汪澈于四月任参知政事）视师湖北、京西。薛季宣上书汪澈论边事。作品：与汪参政论边事。<div id='poem_1273707' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1273707' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1273707?labeling=true' target='_blank'>与汪参政论边事书</a><span class='authorDate'>（1162年7月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 南宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(31376, "南宋", "薛季宣", "poem_title_1273707")'>薛季宣</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1273707_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1273707'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1273707'>薄闻虏以重兵戍许昌，遣将攻皇甫倜，倜军无储粟，援兵理不可缓。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1273707_comment'></div>观虏揭榜陈蔡，虽若有善意，然其奸谋诡计似别有指，政当静以待之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1273707_comment'></div>襄邓地连汝洛，不得不以为虞；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1273707_comment'></div>光、黄屯兵不多，尚当益备。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1273707_comment'></div>不识麾下诸将尝有及是言者否？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1273707_comment'></div>此等进见，尤不厌数，如蒙赐之坐席，接以温言，使人人自谓己亲，可以收其死力。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1273707_comment'></div>仰惟宽慈谦厚，于此端不待言。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1273707_comment'></div>某违远匪遥，所见不敢不尽。</div><div id='poem_sentence_7_1273707_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1162&endYear=1162')">1162年10月</a>　在武昌令任上。十月，作《新作殊亭记》<div id='poem_1273843' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1273843' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1273843?labeling=true' target='_blank'>新作殊亭记</a><span class='authorDate'>（1160年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 南宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(31376, "南宋", "薛季宣", "poem_title_1273843")'>薛季宣</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1273843_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1273843'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1273843'>武昌之西，郎亭之首，有亭岿然而高，超然而迥者，县大夫孟士元之殊亭也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1273843_comment'></div>士元为令武昌，才兼政迹，作亭殊异，有聱叟之漫记焉，唐之刻文磨于俗令。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1273843_comment'></div>亭高记古，同永空山，其所以为不亡者，抑有其道。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1273843_comment'></div>武昌古都也，游观之迹往往而在，山川秀异，触处皆有。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1273843_comment'></div>走初易殊亭之迩，未之尝问，泛然一投足。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1273843_comment'></div>虽湖山江沔顾见古人，俛首内观，则亦有未能见殊于世者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1273843_comment'></div>尝谓为政法古，犹宜继古人之志。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1273843_comment'></div>当其事任，漫不加理，使奇人旧迹堙没自我，其政为可知矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1273843_comment'></div>庾公南楼，犹虚成于江鄂之郡，殊亭伟观，故不可堙诸草莽也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1273843_comment'></div>以亭居涧饮寺后，爰命主僧作而新之，斥广旧基，粗为宽大。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1273843_comment'></div>建以九月甲子，以十月甲子落之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1273843_comment'></div>聊记载其岁时，用见废兴之自，至山川之殊状，游眺之殊极，则次山之记在。</div><div id='poem_sentence_11_1273843_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1162&endYear=1162')">1162年12月</a>　在武昌令任上。十二月，作《余仲美墓志铭》，论及科举制度之弊端。<div id='poem_1273886' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1273886' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1273886?labeling=true' target='_blank'>余仲美墓志铭<span class='inlineComment2'>（绍兴三十二年十二月）</span></a><span class='authorDate'>（1162年12月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 南宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(31376, "南宋", "薛季宣", "poem_title_1273886")'>薛季宣</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1273886_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1273886'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1273886'>自国家以科举取士，士以程文觅举，一不中治，见诎于有司，虽负王佐之才，怀治世之具，悉摈弃不用，而阘茸脂韦之士，厕名科级，有阶以致清显者，实系其人之幸与不幸，盖不足计其贤否。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1273886_comment'></div>德兴余仲美，其贤而不幸者与！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1273886_comment'></div>初，仲美受经于从父石月先生，蚤见知重，尝举才武，一旦不屑去之。<div class='inline'
